# 圣火纪行:东区黎明 - Chronicles of Uluru: London Dawning

## 目录

- LD-01 伦敦第一日 / First Day Back in London
- LD-02 烟囱里的雨燕 / Swallows in the Chimney
- LD-03 雾中鬼婆 / "Fog Hag"
- LD-04 久远的辉煌 / Past Glory
- LD-05 小叫醒工 / Little Knocker-Upper
- LD-06 黑天鹅 / Black Swan
- LD-07 早午餐 / Brunch
- LD-08 小巷落难记 / Raining Fish
- LD-09 天平与角逐 / Hesitation and Challenge
- LD-10 明珠蒙尘 / Dust-Covered Pearl
- LD-11 叮叮当当！ / Clang! Clang!
- LD-12 老木头 / Old Wood
- LD-13 剪彩仪式 / Ribbon-Cutting Ceremony
- LD-14 一粒灰尘 / Soot in the Petri Dish
- LD-15 触底反弹 / Back in the Game
- LD-16 我们的乌卢鲁 / Our Uluru Games
- LD-17 开幕式 / Opening Ceremony
- LD-18 灰黄的对话 / Hazy Memories
- LD-19 雾中独舞 / Dancing in the Smog
- LD-20 伦敦今日晴 / London, Sunny

## LD-01 伦敦第一日 / First Day Back in London

**牙仙**：我们走吧。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I'm ready to go.

**司机**：好的，那我们就出发了，小姐。\
**Driver**: Please fasten your seat belt, Miss. We're setting off now.

**司机**：您以前来过伦敦吗？\
**Driver**: You ever been to London, Miss?

**牙仙**：是的……在很久之前。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Yes. A long time ago.

**司机**：五年？十年？\
**Driver**: Long, eh? Five years? Ten years?

**牙仙**：要更久远。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Longer than that.

**司机**：能有多久呢！您看上去年纪并不大。\
**Driver**: Come on then, how long? You don't look a hundred years old.

**牙仙**：呵呵。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Heh heh.

**司机**：再过两条街就是您要去的那家医院了，噢，对了，顺带一提——\
**Driver**: The hospital is two streets away. Oh, by the way—

**司机**：——按照流程，您应该先和福葛先生见一面，之后他会带您仔细参观一遍这家医院的。\
**Driver**: It's been arranged for you to meet Mr. Fog first, and then he'll show you around the hospital.

**牙仙**：我只是来看一眼，犯不上这么大的阵仗。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I don't see why we need to make a big deal out of a simple visit.

**司机**：这倒是千真万确，女士。如果让服务于王室的老爷安排一场正式的访问，这家医院保管会被装点得像是要过圣诞节。\
**Driver**: Couldn't agree more, Miss. But as this is an official visit by Mr. Fog as a servant of the crown, you can rightly expect that they're going to have the whole place decked up like Christmas.

**牙仙**：嗯，谢谢你愿意为此绕路。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Thank you for taking me there directly.

**牙仙**：我会在参观完后自己去福葛先生的办公室，你不用等我了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I will go to Mr. Fog's office after my visit. You can leave without me.

**牙仙**：其实，我很愿意见识一下伦敦出名的地铁。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I think I'd like to take the underground.

**司机**：地铁？这可不行，女士，那东西和运煤车没什么区别，体面人从来不会坐地铁。\
**Driver**: The Tube? You won't like it, Miss. Not the kind of place for a decent young lady.

**司机**：我就在这等您，别担心我会没事儿做——我所有的精力都要用来克制我对一杯爱尔兰威士忌的渴望。\
**Driver**: I'll wait here for you, love. I'll do my best not to crack into my flask of whiskey while I wait.

**牙仙**：好吧，我很快就会结束。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Thank you. I'll be back soon.

**牙仙**：——！\
**Tooth Fairy**: ...!

**Z**：第一防线学校校医院的生活还不算太糟吧，牙仙？听说那些吵吵闹闹的学生们都很喜欢你。\
**Madam Z**: How are things at the SPDM, Tooth Fairy? I'm hearing rave reviews about their school physician.

**牙仙**：年纪小的孩子们总是比较好安抚，只要他们能听话，我会给一颗他们喜欢的糖果。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I'm glad to hear it. Young children are particularly easy to soothe. A few candies, and they'll behave just fine.

**牙仙**：通常太妃糖就能起作用，其次是水果硬糖——都是一些能让他们忘记牙仙味道的东西。\
**Tooth Fairy**: A little toffee, or a nibble of a fruity sweet, and they've forgotten all about the toothfairy's taste.

**牙仙**：适当分量的甜食能帮助你放松神经，不管对大人还是小孩都一样。\
**Tooth Fairy**: A proper dose of sweets serves to calm the nervous system, and that doesn't just apply to kids.

牙仙取出一枚白纸包的奶糖，轻轻放在Z女士装满特浓茶水的搪瓷杯旁。\
She pulls a piece of milk candy out of her pocket and softly places it beside Madam Z's mug of strong tea.

**牙仙**：副会长身边的麻烦事一定比校医院要多，况且你还要关照我们新任的司辰——她是个爱闯祸的孩子。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Your work here is undoubtedly busier than mine at SPDM. Besides, you're directly responsible for our Timekeeper—the little troublemaker.

**牙仙**：所以，我想你叫我来这间办公室并不是为了一颗糖，以及一次闲聊。\
**Tooth Fairy**: But I am sure you didn't summon me here all for a little chit-chat.

**Z**：……\
**Madam Z**: ...

Z剥开糖纸，将奶糖置于口腔中慢慢融化。与此同时，一沓规格不一的纸张被递至牙仙面对的桌前。\
Madam Z unwraps the candy and places it in her mouth, allowing it to slowly dissolve. Then, she places a stack of papers on the table before Tooth Fairy.

**Z**：鉴于上一次“暴雨”中，基金会已经确定了时代动乱与“暴雨”的关联性，各分部正在收集有关社会运动的报告。\
**Madam Z**: The Foundation has now confirmed a correlation between social turmoil and the emergence of the "Storm." Our branches around the world are now making efforts to collect information on these key social movements.

**Z**：这是伦敦分部提交的一份报告，内容是刚刚在伦敦结束的罢工运动……不，你暂时不用关心有关罢工的细节。\
**Madam Z**: As you may know, there was a strike that has only just ended in London, and there's something I'd like to show you besides the strike itself.

年轻的校医迅速翻动文件，还未经指引，就已抓住了关键词汇。\
Tooth Fairy rapidly flips through the papers. She quickly spots the crucial element.

**牙仙**：肺结核。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Tuberculosis.

**Z**：没错，附录中的伦敦空气污染和肺结核病例报告里有一些异常的数据。\
**Madam Z**: Indeed. There appears to be abnormalities concerning air pollution and the reported cases of TB.

**Z**：比对史实资料来看，该时期伦敦的肺结核发病率不可能高到这种程度，这几乎达到了1952年伦敦烟雾事件时的水平。\
**Madam Z**: Compared to our records before the "Storm," TB morbidity rates are extraordinarily high, approaching levels that shouldn't be seen until the Great Smog of 1952.

**Z**：而且，这个年代的“雾行者”福葛先生也声称，浓雾的成分有些异常。\
**Madam Z**: Our Mr. Fog, the Fogwalker, has also reported that there's something unusual about the composition of the fog.

**牙仙**：需要有一位对“暴雨”知情的人员前往伦敦，最好还有医学背景……\
**Tooth Fairy**: So, we need an insider with knowledge of the "Storm" to visit London, ideally one with a medical background.

**牙仙**：我明白了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I see.

**Z**：我知道你的冬季假期刚刚开始，但基金会仍旧处于人力不足的状态中。我会为你的这次特别外勤申请额外津贴的。\
**Madam Z**: I know your winter vacation just started, but I'm sure you understand the dire situation we find ourselves in. I'll apply for a special allowance for this field mission. What do you say?

**牙仙**：不必担心，我很乐意前往。或许此行能收集到一些在其他时代见不到的牙齿。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I'd be happy to go. Perhaps I'll collect some rare teeth from this era.

**Z**：祝你好运。等你到了伦敦，福葛先生会与你接洽——他奉王室之命，是英国政府与基金会之间沟通的桥梁。\
**Madam Z**: Good luck then. Mr. Fog will contact you when you arrive. He is our liaison between the Foundation and British Government.

**Z**：按照以往的流程，他会先带你参观伦敦市内收治呼吸系统疾病病人的医院。\
**Madam Z**: He'll take you to the hospital, handling many of these respiratory patients.

**Z**：在此之后，你可以自由决定如何行动。\
**Madam Z**: You will be given full trust to resolve this problem.

**Z**：顺带一提，伦敦人对乌卢鲁预选赛的热情可能会影响到你的调查效率。\
**Madam Z**: There is something else: The Uluru Qualifier will soon be held in London. It may factor into your investigation.

**牙仙**：乌卢鲁？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Uluru Qualifier?

**牙仙**：“乌卢鲁伦敦预选赛开幕在即，十字街将为神秘学家举办预热集市……”\
**Tooth Fairy**: "Uluru London Qualifier Coming Soon, Arcanist Fair in Cross Street ..."

**牙仙**：“……为你支持的运动员呐喊助威……”\
**Tooth Fairy**: "Support your favorite competitors ..."

**牙仙**：“……不列颠的运动员将带着荣耀前往澳洲参加决赛。”\
**Tooth Fairy**: "... Winners will represent Great Britain in the Australian finals."

**司机**：澳洲？——我叔叔可是一边哭着一边登上了去澳大利亚的船，我们都认为一个人必须要打得过袋鼠才能在那地方安身立命。\
**Driver**: Australia? They shipped my uncle off to Australia back in the day. I always figured he got done in by a kangaroo.

**司机**：但要是伦敦街头天天来上刚才那一遭，我绝对会把车卖了，去澳洲给我叔叔帮把手——他可能打不过袋鼠。\
**Driver**: But if the smoke here gets any worse, I think I might chance it. Maybe I'll find him in the outback there, or at least avenge him.

眉头紧皱的乘客将偶然得到的传单叠好，乌卢鲁运动会并不是她现在正在关注的问题。\
With a tense frown, Tooth Fairy folds the flyer. The Uluru Games are not her current focus.

**牙仙**：我们刚刚遭遇的黑雾几乎摧毁了一座医院，而你好像不太惊讶。\
**Tooth Fairy**: That smoke seems to have severely damaged that hospital, but you don't seem concerned.

**司机**：这算不得什么大事，女士，每年光是煤气管道爆炸都能掀翻好几座屋子。\
**Driver**: We've seen worse, Miss. You wouldn't believe how many houses we lose in a year to gas line explosions.

**司机**：见怪不怪是一种生活智慧，还是一种绅士风度，尤其是你出门喝杯茶，都能把全世界的神秘学家碰一个遍的时候。\
**Driver**: Nothing much can shock us Londoners. It's a city where you can meet arcanists from all over the world.

**司机**：伦敦全是阿拉伯人、北非人、印度人，还有日本人……天知道他们会使些什么神秘术呢？\
**Driver**: Arabians, North Africans, Indians, and Japanese ... Who knows what kind of arcane skill they can cast?

**牙仙**：警察接管了事故现场，可我担心他们能否做好肺结核医院的善后工作。\
**Tooth Fairy**: The police are on the scene now, but can they really do anything to clean up the hospital?

**司机**：警察厅自有一套办事方法……不算特别友善的那种。所以我说，这事您要尽早和福葛先生通气。\
**Driver**: Well, the police have got their own way of dealing with things. None too friendly. I think you should bring this up to Mr. Fog.

**司机**：也就他还愿意花时间和大人物磨嘴皮，就为了救济院每天能多领到几磅面包配额。\
**Driver**: He's one of the few folks that look out for the working man, and he's never afraid of calling out the upper class.

**牙仙**：福葛先生得知消息的速度肯定会比我们去传话更快。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I suspect Mr. Fog will have known before we did.

**牙仙**：我仍然认为，对我们来说，最好的做法是沿着黑雾在街道上留下的裂痕继续追踪，说不定有机会追上它，或是它的主人。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Let's follow the path of this dark soot on the street. Maybe we can find it or its owner.

**司机**：如您所愿，女士。\
**Driver**: As you like, Miss.

汽车沉默地向东行进，经过一条又一条越来越狭窄的街道。\
The car makes its way eastward, weaving through the increasingly narrow streets.

**司机**：……再往前走就是东区了。\
**Driver**: Seems it's leading us to the East End.

**司机**：东区，没错，女士，就是东区。酒鬼和流浪汉游荡的东区，开膛手杰克曾留下罪行的东区……\
**Driver**: Only thing that comes out of the East End are drunks, tramps, and Jack the Ripper.

**牙仙**：——！\
**Tooth Fairy**: ...!

一次全力以赴的急刹车，刹车片发出尖厉的哀嚎，车头传来不祥的撞击感与孩子的惊叫。\
The brakes screech as the car comes to an abrupt halt. The car shudders from some impact as a child's scream fills the air.

**司机**：——臭小子！！\
**Driver**: Bloody!

太阳穴上的神经一阵刺痛，牙仙几乎是跌跌撞撞地冲出车厢。\
A sudden, stabbing pain strikes the nerve in Tooth Fairy's temple. She almost stumbles as she rushes to exit the car.

司机从车窗里探出头，争抢着为自己的失职辩解。\
The driver pokes his head through the car window, scrambling to justify his mistake.

**司机**：女士，我绝没碰一滴酒，但东区就是这个样，好司机不会在这种地方开车，尤其还是这种大雾天。\
**Driver**: Miss, I swear to high heaven that I have not had a drop of drink today! This is the East End for you!

**司机**：要么是你撞到了什么人，留下一摊血迹，要么是被人用石子砸碎了车窗。\
**Driver**: Either you hit someone or someone hits you.

**司机**：……你看清我撞着什么东西了吗？告诉我吧，我承受得住。\
**Driver**: Please, Miss, take a look for me. Tell me if I hit anything. I can take it.

**牙仙**：可……车前没有人。\
**Tooth Fairy**: It appears ... there's no one in front of the car.

**司机**：没有人？\
**Driver**: No one?

**？？？**：向上看。\
**???**: I'm up here!

**司机**：小心头顶，女士！\
**Driver**: Look up there, Miss!

牙仙仰起头。漫天飞舞的纸片旋转着下落，其中有一团色彩驳杂的布团格外显眼，仿佛是被人遗弃的旧麻布袋。\
Tooth Fairy looks up to see a flurry of papers fluttering and spinning through the sky. A particularly vibrant bundle of fabric resembling some kind of burlap sack hurtles through the center.

**“麻布袋”**：你想接住我吗？\
**"Sack"**: Can you catch me?

**牙仙**：——！\
**Tooth Fairy**: ...?

女孩的裙角被风鼓起，她如一朵水母般浮游于半空。\
The little girl's skirt catches the wind, and she drifts weightlessly through the air.

空中的彩色纸片沿着漩涡的轨迹，缓缓汇集在女孩身边——它们都是尚未散发的乌卢鲁宣传单。\
The colorful scraps of paper spiral through the air and swirl around her. They're all Uluru flyers still waiting to be distributed.

**牙仙**：风……她毫不费力地用神秘术将自己的身体托了起来，在她这个年纪，可真少见。\
**Tooth Fairy**: She's being lifted up on the wind. Is this her arcane skill? If so, she's amazing for her age.

小麻布袋缓缓地降了下来，牙仙凭本能伸出双手，可它忽然在空中飘向了另一个方向，轻巧地落在几步之外的路肩上。\
She gently descends, seemingly headed straight into Tooth Fairy's arms, but at the last moment, she shifts direction and lands softly a few steps away.

**“麻布袋”**：你输了，你不是一个厉害的运动员。\
**"Sack"**: You lose. You ain't goin' to qualify for nothin' like that!

**牙仙**：你受伤了吗，孩子？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Are you hurt at all?

**“麻布袋”**：我为什么会受伤？我还没有飞到和金丝绵雀的窝一样高，只要轻轻地落下来就好了。\
**"Sack"**: Why would I be? It's not even as high up as a canary nest. It's no sweat with the help of a little wind.

**“麻布袋”**：可是奇奇比翁受伤了，黑色的汽车把他的腰给撞断了。\
**"Sack"**: But the Sootikiki was hurt. The car hit his waist.

**司机**：奇奇比翁？他是你的朋友吗？\
**Driver**: Is this Sootikiki your friend?

**“麻布袋”**：是的，他被撞到之后就跑开了。不过他很记仇，说不定马上就会找回来了。\
**"Sack"**: Yes. But he ran away. He's probably angry. I'd bet he's still around. He don't forgive easy!

小麻布袋指向道路左侧的暗巷，阴暗而多雾的角落中，有一对闪闪发光的眼睛掩藏在垃圾箱之后。\
She points toward the shadowy alley to her left, where, in a dark, smoggy corner, a pair of glowing eyes peek out from behind a garbage bin.

**“麻布袋”**：他就是奇奇比翁，而我是纸信圈儿。\
**"Sack"**: See? Over there. That's the Sootikiki, and I'm Flutterpage.

**司机**：……叫你的朋友出来吧，我得为他的腰道歉。他或许这辈子也没法去码头讨生活了。\
**Driver**: Could you bring your friend out? I'd like to make amends if I hurt him, especially if he can't work.

**纸信圈儿**：他不用去码头做工，不过道歉是应该的。\
**Flutterpage**: Oh, he doesn't work. But you still need to apologize!

纸信圈儿面向小巷，如招呼最亲热的好友那般向小巷深处挥着手。\
Flutterpage turns toward the alley, waving into the shadows to call over her friend.

**纸信圈儿**：奇奇比翁，快出来，这位先生想要向你道歉，也许他买了保险呢。\
**Flutterpage**: Come on out, Sootikiki! This bloke here wants to apologize to you.

藏在阴暗街角中的奇奇比翁蠢蠢欲动，它搅动着淡黄色的雾气，突然跃出。\
The Sootikiki stirs in the shadows, disturbing the pale yellow smog before suddenly leaping forward.

**奇奇比翁**：奇奇——嗡——嗡——\
**Sootikiki**: *roars*

**司机**：这玩意——这玩意根本就没有腰！它比袋鼠还大啊！\
**Driver**: That thing doesn't even have a waist! And he's as big as a kangaroo!

**纸信圈儿**：是你看不见他的腰！\
**Flutterpage**: Nuh-uh! His waist is right there! Can't you see?

**牙仙**：受惊的魔精很危险。退后。\
**Tooth Fairy**: A frightened critter is dangerous. Please stay back, child.

**司机**：哦！哦！哦！该死！该死！\
**Driver**: Bollocks! Bollocks! Turn over already, you stupid car!

发动机再次启动，活塞缸打着撤退的鼓点，带着汽车远离这片满是脏污的街区。\
The engine roars to life again, its pistons drumming the retreat as the car careens through the streets.

**纸信圈儿**：开车的先生像奇奇比翁一样溜走了，他不和我们一起去玩吗？\
**Flutterpage**: Why did Mr. Driver run away like the Sootikiki?

**牙仙**：这位先生担心留在这条街上会弄坏他的车，他不想因此丢掉工作。\
**Tooth Fairy**: He was worried for his car. If it got damaged, it could cost him his job.

**纸信圈儿**：丢掉工作？这个我明白，我也不想丢掉工作。\
**Flutterpage**: Lose his job? Oh, got it. I don't want to lose my job, neither.

小女孩极富同理心地点头。可在更成熟的大人眼中，这个年纪的孩子和工作这一词完全没有关联。\
The little girl gives an empathetic nod. But a child her age has no place in anything to do with the word "work."

**纸信圈儿**：他一周赚的钱肯定比六便士更多，不然可买不起一辆车……他是做什么攒到这么多钱的？我也能做到吗？\
**Flutterpage**: He has a car, so I wager he makes more than six pence a week. How did he get that job? Can I do it too?

**牙仙**：你需要再长大些才行。来，张口。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I suppose you could, once you grow up. Here, open your mouth.

牙仙指尖出现了一份金光闪闪的药膏——由金色仙子添加羊毛脂后研磨而成，用以避免初次生吞牙仙的恐惧。\
Tooth Fairy produces a shimmering jar of ointment made from ground golden fairy and lanolin—a concoction capable of soothing one's fear of swallowing a toothfairy for the first time.

**纸信圈儿**：这是什么？\
**Flutterpage**: What's this?

**牙仙**：药膏。你受伤了，内服可以止痛，外用可以消炎。\
**Tooth Fairy**: You were hurt. It's a kind of ointment. It will numb the pain if you ingest it, or reduce the inflammation if you rub it on your wound.

**纸信圈儿**：我身上有些疼，可是消……炎？什么是“瞎咬”？女巫小姐还没教会我怎么“瞎咬”。\
**Flutterpage**: Was I hurt? I feel a little pain. But whatcha mean by in-flame-ation? Does that mean I'll catch on fire?

**牙仙**：总之，它能让你变得更舒服。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Take it, and you will feel much better.

**牙仙**：听医生的话，好吗？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Doctor's orders, kid.

孩子的好奇心轻易战胜了对未知事物的抵触，她伸长脖子，一口吮住牙仙沾满药膏的手指。\
The little girl's curiosity easily trumps her hesitation toward the unfamiliar. She stretches her neck and sucks Tooth Fairy's ointment-covered finger.

**牙仙**：……\
**Tooth Fairy**: ...

**纸信圈儿**：唔……有点酸，还有点像发霉的覆盆子，但总的来说还是甜甜的，为什么别的药不像你的这样甜？\
**Flutterpage**: Hmm. It's a bit sour, like a moldy raspberry, but still sweet. Why aren't other pills as sweet as yours?

**纸信圈儿**：你戴着很奇怪的金属“面具”，胸前还有好多牙齿，罐子里装着金色的小精灵。你是巫医，对吗？\
**Flutterpage**: I see! So, you're a witch doctor, aren't ya? I can tell from your metal mask, teeth necklace, and the golden fairies in your jar.

**牙仙**：你也可以这么认为。\
**Tooth Fairy**: That is a reasonable assumption.

**纸信圈儿**：那你一定是来参加乌卢鲁欢庆集市的！看，你还带着集市的宣传单呢。\
**Flutterpage**: So, you're here for the Uluru Fair, then! Must be, you even got the flyer with you.

**牙仙**：我是来伦敦调查肺结核病的医生，可是一道奇怪的黑雾摧毁了我正要造访的医院。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Actually, I'm here as a doctor to investigate a tuberculosis outbreak. But this strange black fog damaged the hospital I was heading to.

**牙仙**：我在追踪这道烟雾的去向，所以才来到了这里。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I followed the trace it left behind to this area.

**纸信圈儿**：这里没有什么黑雾，空气一直都是黄乎乎的，又高高地飘在天上。只有红砖厂的烟囱会冒黑烟，但那些厂房都不在十字街。\
**Flutterpage**: Black fog? There ain't no black fog. 'Round here, the smog is yellow. And sometimes I've seen black smoke puffin' up from the factory chimneys, but never in Cross Street.

**纸信圈儿**：十字街上的人都在关心乌卢鲁，这里很多人都会神秘术，会神秘术的人都在庆祝将要到来的乌卢鲁。\
**Flutterpage**: As like to be an arcane skill, Miss. Lots of us arcanists here. That's why we're all chuffed up for the Uluru Qualifiers.

**纸信圈儿**：这儿有草药师、通灵师、占星师、魔术师……\
**Flutterpage**: There's herbalists, psychics, diviners, magicians ...

**牙仙**：我明白你的意思了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Thank you, Flutterpage. I think I've got the idea.

如果不被打断的话，纸信圈儿能把这条街上的每一份神秘学活计都念一遍。\
Left to her own devices, Flutterpage could recite the job of every arcanist on the entire street.

**纸信圈儿**：你明白就好了。我带你去看看，你一定会喜欢的。\
**Flutterpage**: Great! Then I'll show you 'round. You'll like it here.

纸信圈儿拉住客人的手，把她往十字街的深处拽去。\
Flutterpage grabs Tooth Fairy's hand and drags her toward the heart of Cross Street.

## LD-02 烟囱里的雨燕 / Swallows in the Chimney

**纸信圈儿**：这里就是十字街！\
**Flutterpage**: Welcome to Cross Street!

神秘学家们在空地上支起简陋的摊位，庆祝即将到来的乌卢鲁预选赛。这场比赛将决定谁能代表英国前往澳洲的总赛场。\
Makeshift stalls line the street as the arcanists celebrate the approaching Uluru Qualifiers. This event will decide who gets to represent Great Britain in the finals in Australia.

纸信圈儿将手中最后一把乌卢鲁传单撒出去，纸片被轻风吹到了数个街区之外，其中有不少都钻进了半掩的窗户中。\
Flutterpage lets the last of the Uluru flyers slip from her fingers. They scatter as they soar on the wind and drift into half-open windows.

**威尔**：不要再乱扔垃圾了，小坏种！\
**Will**: Stop litterin', you grimy little bug!

**纸信圈儿**：嘿！欢迎参加乌卢鲁欢庆集市～\
**Flutterpage**: This is the Uluru Fair!

与传单小工一同到来的造访者正在谨慎地搜寻街巷中的不起眼角落，可杂乱的布置让她一无所获。\
Tooth Fairy inspects the street, studying the alleys on either side, but finds nothing.

**牙仙**：黑雾的踪迹消失在神秘学家聚居的街区……它很会选地方。\
**Tooth Fairy**: The trace of the black fog seems to have disappeared into a large gathering of arcanists. A wise choice.

**牙仙**：但这样想来，我或许可以假设黑雾具有某种程度的自主智慧。\
**Tooth Fairy**: A choice, I'm already assuming, that has a certain level of intelligence.

说到底，她只是一个医生，面对疾病之外的未知，牙仙一筹莫展。\
Ultimately, she is only a doctor. When it comes to things outside of illness, she often finds herself lost.

**纸信圈儿**：黑雾，听上去像老婆婆嘴里用来吓唬小孩的怪物，但我确实在房梁上听过几句别人对它的描述，有人说，它出生在工厂的大烟管里。\
**Flutterpage**: It sounds like a monster. Like from tall tales what adults make up to scare us. But I heard people talkin' when I was sittin' on the roof. They say it was born from a smokestack!

**牙仙**：嗯，它看起来像是浓重的煤烟。\
**Tooth Fairy**: It does appear to have a similar composition to soot.

**纸信圈儿**：真可怕，我希望它不要到十字街来，不然它肯定会毁了乌卢鲁欢庆集市，还会把烟囱里的金丝绵雀都吓走的。\
**Flutterpage**: That's no good for the birds, Miss Doctor. I sure hope it don't come here. I don't want it to muck up the Uluru Fair or scare the canaries away from the chimneys!

**牙仙**：金丝绵雀？\
**Tooth Fairy**: What's so special about the canaries?

**纸信圈儿**：烟囱里的金丝绵雀知道羊脂蜗牛藏在哪里，只要给他们一些草籽和面包，他们就会带我去找蜗牛。\
**Flutterpage**: They always know where the lanolin snails are hidin'. All do is give them a bit of old bread or seeds, and they find me the snails.

**纸信圈儿**：今天就是我去捉蜗牛的日子，你先随便逛逛，我弄到羊脂蜗牛之后马上就来找你——不要走丢了。\
**Flutterpage**: It's my snail-catchin' day! Stay right there, Miss. I'll be back soon as I finish! Don't go gettin' off your sauce while I'm gone!

还没有等同行的大人答应，纸信圈儿就飘乎乎地靠近了一处用米字旗装饰的摊位，随后像一阵轻柔的微风般消失不见。\
With that, Flutterpage drifts toward a stall decorated with Union Jack bunting, before disappearing like a whisper on the wind.

在纸信圈儿消失的那处摊位前，站立着一位身穿上等烟灰色羊毛外套的绅士，他身板笔直，和整片街区格格不入。\
A gentleman in a fine gray woolen coat stands tall nearby. He is utterly incongruous with the rest of the street.

**牙仙**：嗯？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Hmm?

**？？？**：瞧，这是《神秘学家集市信息报备表》，只要填写所有的空白，并得到市政厅的审批，没有人会找这场集市的麻烦。\
**???**: This is an Arcanist Fair Booth Application Form. You need only fill this and get proper approval from the city government, then no one can bother you.

**摊贩**：审批？等审批下来的时候，我都能知道谁拿下了澳洲的冠军。\
**Vendor**: Approval, eh? What's the point? The Games will be over by the time they've even looked at my application.

**？？？**：这场集市是非办不可吗？你们……咳，你们不觉得这种天气根本不适合任何户外活动吗？\
**???**: *sigh* Are we entirely certain we even want to hold the fair in these conditions? Don't you think ...*cough* the weather now isn't appropriate for that kind of strenuous physical activity?

**摊贩**：还能怎么办呢？你能解决空气里的脏东西吗，雾行者先生？别打官腔。\
**Vendor**: What else can we do? We need to earn our bread, or perhaps you could clean the air for us, eh, Mr. Fogwalker?

**？？？**：……我正在尽最大的努力。\
**???**: I'm doing all that I can.

**摊贩**：这句话的意思就是“做不到”，对吧？\
**Vendor**: Which means you can't do nothin' at all, don't it?

**摊贩**：咳嗽归咳嗽，但生意还要做，我们不像你一样能吃到王室的津贴。\
**Vendor**: Yeah, we're coughin', but what we make in a day at the fair here is more than an entire week anywhere else! Not like we have royal allowances to rely on, unlike you.

**摊贩**：好了，现在请你让一让，后面那位女士已经等了半天了。\
**Vendor**: Enough of it, already. Now, would you mind moving aside for the little lady behind you? She's been waiting a while.

**？？？**：女士……是你？！\
**???**: Oh, I do apologize, Miss. I ... Ms. Tooth Fairy?!

**牙仙**：福葛先生，没想到会在这里遇见你。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I didn't expect to run into you here, Mr. Fog.

**福葛先生**：十分荣幸与你相见，牙仙女士。\
**Mr. Fog**: The pleasure is all mine, Miss.

**福葛先生**：哦，对了，看我多失礼——欢迎来到伦敦！\
**Mr. Fog**: Oh, where are my manners! Welcome to London!

一位十字街的居民匆匆路过，发出了一阵猛烈的咳嗽。\
A Cross Street local hurries by, letting out a sharp, violent cough.

**福葛先生**：……好吧，我们原本应该在伦敦清洁大气委员会的办公室里见面的，我还为你准备了上好的印度茶叶。\
**Mr. Fog**: Of course, we were supposed to meet in the office of the London Atmospheric Clean-up Committee. I'd have prepared a fine Indian tea for you.

**福葛先生**：但我不得不先来十字街处理一些棘手的问题……倒也正好，这样你就不用在会客厅里干等着了。\
**Mr. Fog**: But I was called away to deal with matters here on Cross Street. It's a happy coincidence that you popped by. It will save us both some time.

福葛先生有些局促地摩挲着手套，看来这场不体面的会面还在让他感到尴尬。\
Mr. Fog awkwardly fiddles with his gloves, clearly feeling embarrassed at the indecency of their meeting.

好在远道而来的医生显然更关注“问题”本身。\
Thankfully for him, Tooth Fairy seems more concerned about the issue at hand.

**牙仙**：棘手的问题？你说的是伦敦的空气污染吗？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Something the matter? You mean the air pollution?

**福葛先生**：空气污染——当然，你就是为这个而来的，对吧？总的来说，一切小问题都可以归结在这个大问题之下。\
**Mr. Fog**: Not precisely, no. Though one could say the problem is related. In fact, it seems just about every one of our problems comes down to these sticky contradictions.

**福葛先生**：但总有一些更加细致和独特的麻烦。譬如，十字街的居民不相信那些雾气有蹊跷！简直不讲理了。\
**Mr. Fog**: For example, contrary to good wisdom, the people of Cross Street have opted to continue their fair despite the obvious dangers of the fog! That's just unreasonable.

**摊贩**：是你不讲理在先，因为有一点雾气，就要禁止乌卢鲁欢庆集市吗？\
**Vendor**: You're the unreasonable one here, mate. Stop the Uluru Fair on account of a bit of fog? Fog, in London! Should we cancel if there's water in the Thames next?

**福葛先生**：人们应该明白雾气的危害，减少开展户外活动。\
**Mr. Fog**: Citizens should be made aware of the harm caused by fog and reduce unnecessary outdoor activities.

**威尔**：欸——二位是政府的长官吗？\
**Will**: Pardon me. You lot government officials?

一些爱管闲事的居民凑近基金会调查员与伦敦雾行者，准备获取今日的谈资。\
A few busybodies gather near the two of them, ready to catch the latest gossip.

**威尔**：长官，我们干嘛不能庆祝乌卢鲁预选赛呢？如今能让我们神秘学家在家门口庆祝的活动可不多了。\
**Will**: You sayin' we ain't allowed to celebrate the Uluru Qualifiers? So what you expectin' us to do? Just watch the games and then pop off home?

**威尔**：难道要——咳咳，干等着比赛开始吗？那可太没意思了。\
**Will**: It's not like there are many events left for us arcanists ... *cough* to celebrate in our own country ...*cough*

**牙仙**：先生，你咳嗽得很严重……\
**Tooth Fairy**: Sir, you seem to have quite a severe cough.

**威尔**：这只是恶毒的诅咒罢了，不是什么大问题，只要能找到一个有能耐的疗愈师……\
**Will**: Oh, it's not so bad. Just a little curse, is all. Doesn't matter none. A good arcanist healer can cure me.

**福葛先生**：你看，他们一直是这么说的——诅咒？我的天！这病叫肺结核！你们应该去看医生。\
**Mr. Fog**: That's exactly what I've been talking about! A curse? Good lord, man. You have a disease called tuberculosis! You need a proper doctor, not a healer!

**牙仙**：或许十字街的居民们正在经受某一类神秘学家思维惯性的影响。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Maybe this is just how citizens in Cross Street best comprehend the disease, in the arcanist way.

**牙仙**：肺结核源于空气中的病菌，无法用“驱邪”或“净化”之类的方式治疗。\
**Tooth Fairy**: It's not a matter of arcanists or humans. Tuberculosis is caused by the presence of bacterium in the air. It can't be cured through ritualistic "purification" or "exorcism."

**威尔**：不，绝不是这么回事，你们不见得明白十字街的事。\
**Will**: You just don't get it, do you? It's not like that.

**威尔**：如果是肺结核，我的胸口怎么会像火烧一样难受？我从没听过这种症状。\
**Will**: If this, tuber-what-have-you is the reason, then why does my chest burn like hell? I've never heard of no bacteria what could do that.

**牙仙**：有火烧感？\
**Tooth Fairy**: You feel like your chest is burning?

**威尔**：没错，就像你吞了一颗烧红的煤球。就是从这个月开始，以前从来没有过这种感觉。\
**Will**: Like swallowing a flaming coal it is. It all started this month! Never felt anythin' like this before.

**摊贩**：我说了，长官，这病是人类治不好的，这是雾中鬼婆的诅咒。\
**Vendor**: Like I said, there's no disease. This has to be the Fog Hag's curse!

**摊贩**：她就住在十字街，本是一只被邪恶炼金术士扔进坩埚的癞蛤蟆，生来就会召唤黑色的烟雾……\
**Vendor**: She's the one who summoned this damnable black fog. She used to be a toad, before she was thrown into an alchemist's cauldron and came out as a twisted old hag that haunts our street.

**牙仙**：……黑色的烟雾？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Could you tell me more about the black fog?

摊贩缄口不言，只是向十字街深处投去不怀好意的一瞥。\
The vendor remains silent, shooting a hostile glance down Cross Street.

**威尔**：嘘——！别在我面前谈这么晦气的东西。\
**Will**: Shh! Don't say anythin' about it. It'll bring bad luck!

咳嗽的“自称受诅咒者”挥挥手，像驱赶蚊子一样扰乱了众人的目光，随后消失在暗黄色的薄雾中。\
He coughs, waving his hand to scatter the attention of the crowd, then vanishes into the yellow smog.

**福葛先生**：雾中鬼婆？——听听看，这下又来了什么新花样？\
**Mr. Fog**: So, now we have a Fog Hag? What's to come next, I wonder?

福葛先生无奈地摊开手，出于绅士的体面，他不该再谈论这种话题。\
He raises his hands in resignation, knowing that, as a gentleman, he should speak no further on the matter.

**福葛先生**：唉——有时候我也搞不明白神秘学家同胞的脑子里在想什么，但这就是伦敦现状的一个生动展示。\
**Mr. Fog**: *sigh* Sometimes, despite being an arcanist myself, it's hard to understand my own people. But that's what they think around here.

**福葛先生**：总之，我的同僚正在街区内调查他们口中的诅咒。相信我，这位优秀的骑手绝不会有什么收获的。\
**Mr. Fog**: My colleague is presently out investigating this "curse" they mentioned. But, to say nothing of his intrepid skills as a ranger, I doubt he'll produce any evidence of this so-called "hag."

**福葛先生**：事实上，他——\
**Mr. Fog**: In fact, he—

**？？？**：吁——\
**???**: *whistle*

一道悠长又尖锐的口哨，如同红土地上纵马驰骋的骑手，可紧随而至的并非紧凑的马蹄声。\
A long, sharp whistle cuts through the air, like that of a rider galloping across the plains of the land down under. But what follows is not the sound of hooves.

**？？？**：别在那杵着了，福葛伙计，我们碰上了硬茬！\
**???**: Arthur, a little help, mate! We've got trouble!

一顶骑着棍马的帽子飞奔而来，披风在浓雾中猎猎作响，如同刚刚探索归来的斥候骑兵。\
A hat riding a hobbyhorse races forward, its coat fluttering in the thick smog like a cavalryman returning from a reconnaissance mission.

帽子之后，是紧随而至的黑色雾气。\
A dark cloud follows close behind him.

**牙仙**：它果然藏在这里。\
**Tooth Fairy**: So, here it is.

**福葛先生**：我的老帽儿啊，你惹到什么东西了？！\
**Mr. Fog**: What's that after you now, Old Hat?

**“老帽儿”**：对十字街的探索惊扰了黑色的雾气，它派出了可怕的魔精，想要危害无辜者的安危！\
**"Old Hat"**: It's the black fog! Seems I've startled it, and now it's sent out critters into the streets!

**“老帽儿”**：准备战斗！像鸸鹋战争中的勇士那样前进！\
**"Old Hat"**: Steady on! Let's charge like soldiers of the Great Emu War!

**煤烟卡邦克鲁**：呼——呼呼——\
**Carbuncoal**: *hissing*

**摊贩**：鬼婆——那鬼婆一定听见我们在说她坏话了！\
**Vendor**: It's the hag. The hag's curse is coming for us!

**威尔**：魔精从她的花园里钻出来了，快跑！\
**Will**: Those nasty critters are comin' from her garden! Run!

**宽檐帽**：我是宽檐帽，福葛伙计的同僚与斥候，很高兴在战斗中成为你的护卫，女士！\
**Brimley**: May I say it was an honor to serve as your bodyguard, Miss. I'm Brimley, the ranger colleague of my mate here, Arthur Fog.

**牙仙**：谢谢，我没有受伤。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I wasn't hurt, thanks to you.

“福葛伙计”在一旁轻轻拍去身上的烟尘，随后来到牙仙面前。他在战斗中驱散了大多数的黑色雾气，现在脸色很差。\
Mr. Fog lightly brushes the soot from his coat before walking over to Tooth Fairy. Despite clearing away most of the black fog, his expression looks grim.

**福葛先生**：咳咳——好了，我想现在是时候做个总结了。牙仙女士，谢谢你转述发生在市区救济医院的事故。\
**Mr. Fog**: *cough* Thank you, Ms. Tooth Fairy, for telling us what happened at the hospital. We ought to make a summary of our investigation so far.

经验老到的政府职员总是善于做总结。\
Seasoned government employees are particularly good at providing summaries.

**福葛先生**：今天遭遇了三件怪事。第一，黑色的雾气。第二，一些肺结核病人的火烧感。第三——\
**Mr. Fog**: We've encountered three oddities thus far today: this mysterious black fog, the unusual burning chest symptom, and ...

福葛先生酝酿了很长时间，才终于把难以启齿的第三点说出口。\
He carefully considers his words before bringing up the difficult third point.

**福葛先生**：——第三，住十字街里的“雾中鬼婆”。\
**Mr. Fog**: This so-called Fog Hag living on Cross Street.

**宽檐帽**：好样的，福葛伙计，你说出来了！这对你缺失的幽默感来说是一次绝好的补充。\
**Brimley**: Well done, mate, you did it! You said it out loud! We may just break the ice off your soul yet.

**福葛先生**：我不会站在事实面前否认它！\
**Mr. Fog**: I'm only doing my due diligence by quoting the title verbatim.

**福葛先生**：我还要做出这样一种假设——这三件怪事之间有因果联系，鬼婆释放出黑雾，让伦敦居民染上了奇怪的肺结核。\
**Mr. Fog**: Back to the topic. Combining these clues together, we should assume a causal connection: the hag releases black fog, giving Londoners this variant of TB with the "burning chest symptom."

**宽檐帽**：我从来不知道你也是贝克街221号的租客，福葛伙计。\
**Brimley**: When did you move into 221B Baker Street, mate?

雾行者望向一旁，想必再让他吸入一吨重的雾气，也不会让他的表情变得更糟糕。\
The Fogwalker shifts his gaze, knowing that, even if he were to inhale a mouthful of that black fog, his face couldn't look any grimmer.

**牙仙**：我也认可这种看法，如果确实有一位这样的女士住在十字街，那我们最好去和她谈谈。\
**Tooth Fairy**: It's a reasonable speculation. If so, then the first thing is to determine if such a lady lives here on Cross Street. We'd better pay her a visit.

**宽檐帽**：好吧——如果你一定要这么坚持的话。\
**Brimley**: If you insist, darl.

**宽檐帽**：事实上，本斥候已探明她堡垒的方位，那是十字街向南尽头的一幢花园独栋小屋。\
**Brimley**: I can already confirm that for you. She's here alright. Down at the house with the mangy front garden at the south end.

**福葛先生**：如果这位“雾中鬼婆”带有敌意，贸然造访不见得是个好主意。\
**Mr. Fog**: Very well, but might I suggest we don't all go in a rush to pay her a visit? We know nothing about her, or even whether this hag is a danger.

一个瘦小的影子挤了进来。\
A little figure squeezes its way in.

**纸信圈儿**：巫医小姐，你和福葛先生还有帽子先生说完了吗？\
**Flutterpage**: Oi, Ms. Witch Doctor, you done talkin' to Mr. Fog and Mr. Hat?

**牙仙**：纸信圈儿——你到哪里去了？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Flutterpage. Where have you been?

**纸信圈儿**：嗯——你也没有认真听我说话。我说过我去烟囱里找金丝绵雀了。\
**Flutterpage**: Hmm? Wasn't you listenin'? I was off catchin' snails.

**纸信圈儿**：而金丝绵雀会帮我找到蜗牛。\
**Flutterpage**: With a bit of help from the canaries.

纸信圈儿举起一只废旧的玻璃罐，容器中装着的蜗牛有孩子的半个手掌那么大。\
Flutterpage lifts an old glass jar filled with snails.

**宽檐帽**：了不起的冒险收获，纸信圈儿小姐。\
**Brimley**: Good on you, little tacker. That's quite the harvest.

女孩把玻璃罐藏在层层衣物之内，随后紧紧拽住牙仙的衣摆。\
She tucks the jar away in the folds of her clothing, then lightly grabs the hem of Tooth Fairy's coat.

**纸信圈儿**：走吧，巫医小姐。\
**Flutterpage**: Shall we then, Ms. Witch Doctor?

**牙仙**：要去哪儿？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Where are you taking me?

**纸信圈儿**：我说过要带你逛逛十字街的，你找不到比我更好的导游了。\
**Flutterpage**: Thought I'd show you around Cross Street! Figurin' since I'm the best guide here.

**牙仙**：那么，你熟悉十字街向南尽头带花园的小屋吗？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Are you? Then do you happen to know about the house at the south end of the street?

女孩思索了一会，露出恍然大悟的表情。\
Flutterpage ponders for a moment before her eyes widen in realization.

**纸信圈儿**：我当然熟悉，那是女巫小姐住的屋子。我这就带你去吧，正好，这一罐蜗牛就是要送给她的。\
**Flutterpage**: Sure do. Actually, these snails are for her! You can tag along with me to see her, if you like.

## LD-03 雾中鬼婆 / "Fog Hag"

花园中的雾气似乎格外浓郁，它难以被描述为一种烟尘，更近似于乳白色的胶质。\
The smog in the garden feels unusually dense. It has taken on an almost milky, gelatinous quality.

略带腥味的潮湿空气粘在访客身上，爬山虎光秃秃的根须缠在古老的石砖墙上，只有少数叶片还在苟延残喘。\
The damp, fishy air sticks to the visitors. Sparse ivy winds around the ancient stone wall, its bare roots clinging desperately to it.

**纸信圈儿**：女巫小姐的家就是这儿——一栋很大的房子，而我只有一个很小的房子……不过我的房子很高。\
**Flutterpage**: This right here, Miss, is the Fog Lady's house! As you can tell, it is a very big, big house, not like mine. Mine is small, but very high up!

**牙仙**：尖锐的三角形屋顶，狭窄的装饰性平开窗……或许是维多利亚时期的建筑。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Steep, tilted roofs, sash windows, it's very Victorian.

**纸信圈儿**：嗯？\
**Flutterpage**: Hmm?

**纸信圈儿**：我还不知道她叫什么名字，但是应该不叫维多利亚，不过也许她真的叫维多利亚吧。\
**Flutterpage**: Oh, no, her name ain't Victoria, Miss. At least, I don't think so.

**牙仙**：不，我只是在说，这栋房子应该已经有很久的历史了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: No, no. I mean Victorian architecture is a kind of style of house. I'm saying this house must have a long history.

**纸信圈儿**：哦……这么说没错吧，我出生之前她就在这儿了。\
**Flutterpage**: Oh. Too right about that, Miss. It's been here for ages!

**纸信圈儿**：来吧，我带你进去。\
**Flutterpage**: Come along then. I'll take you in.

纸信圈儿没有敲门，或是触动任何类似于门铃的机关。她牵着牙仙径直向花园内走去。\
Flutterpage doesn't knock, nor does she touch anything resembling a doorbell. She simply leads Tooth Fairy straight to the garden gate.

**花园卡邦克鲁**：吱——吱——\
**Vines Carbuncle**: Squeak! Squeak!

几只浑身缠满藤蔓的卡邦克鲁在荆棘中探出半截身子，又立马缩了回去，但仍然紧盯着访客。\
Several Carbuncles peek out from among the vines before quickly retreating, their eyes still locked on the visitors.

**牙仙**：这是在花园中豢养的魔精？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Ah! Are these her critters?

**纸信圈儿**：你们的肚子饿了，是不是？\
**Flutterpage**: You lot are hungry today, ain't you?

纸信圈儿从宽大的衣袍里拿出装满蜗牛的罐子。\
From the folds of her oversized frock, Flutterpage pulls out a jar filled with snails.

**纸信圈儿**：可这不是给你们吃的，这是给女巫小姐的，让我和巫医小姐进去。\
**Flutterpage**: They ain't for you! They're for the lady of the house. Now please let me and Ms. Witch Doctor through.

**花园卡邦克鲁**：吱！\
**Vines Carbuncle**: Squeak!

卡邦克鲁们并不放行，几根木质的触须也加入拦路的阵型。\
The Carbuncles refuse their entry, shooting out a few tendrils to form a blockade.

**纸信圈儿**：他们以前从来不是这样的，巫医小姐。\
**Flutterpage**: Sorry, Ms. Witch Doctor, they was much friendlier before.

**牙仙**：你进去过吗？\
**Tooth Fairy**: You've been here before?

**纸信圈儿**：当然，我一向都是直接进去的，为什么他们这次会拦着我呢？\
**Flutterpage**: Yep, they always let me in straight away. No clue what set them off this time.

纸信圈儿踮着脚，打算通过一次跳跃翻越阻碍，可她回头看了一眼巫医小姐，立刻放弃了这个只能她一个人执行的想法。\
Flutterpage stands on her tiptoes, planning to hop over the barrier, but after a quick glance at Tooth Fairy, she abandons the idea.

**纸信圈儿**：这很奇怪。\
**Flutterpage**: I don't rightly know what to do.

**纸信圈儿**：也许我能叫女巫小姐出门——不，不行，她从来只会呆在家里，不会出门的。\
**Flutterpage**: I'd try callin' her, but it won't do much good. Even if she heard me, she won't come out.

**牙仙**：她从来不会出门？\
**Tooth Fairy**: You're saying she never leaves her house?

**纸信圈儿**：我没见过。\
**Flutterpage**: Not that I ever seen.

**牙仙**：她见过别的客人吗？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Do other people visit her?

**纸信圈儿**：嗯……没有。\
**Flutterpage**: Hmm ... No.

**牙仙**：可你却经常见到她？\
**Tooth Fairy**: But you visit her often?

**纸信圈儿**：她喜欢我带给她的蜗牛……也许是喜欢吃这个？\
**Flutterpage**: She likes when I bring her snails. You think she eats them?

**纸信圈儿**：我把蜗牛带给她，她就让我在她家玩一会儿。\
**Flutterpage**: All I know is I gave her snails, and then she asked me to stay round her house for a while.

**纸信圈儿**：女巫小姐心情好的时候，就会教我一些单词……一些神秘术。女巫小姐心情不好的时候，她就给我看一些很复杂但很有趣的书。\
**Flutterpage**: When she's not in a sour mood, she even teaches me some words, for arcane skills. But if she is sour, then all she does is hand me some books, and I can't even read most of them.

**纸信圈儿**：但是你不能在她面前说太多次为什么，如果这么做了，她就会让我“出去”。\
**Flutterpage**: Don't go askin' her too many "whys." If you do, she says "get out," and you got to go.

**纸信圈儿**：有一次我在她家待了一个下午才“出去”。\
**Flutterpage**: So far, the longest I stayed was a whole afternoon!

**牙仙**：……我明白了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I see.

牙仙再次审视着小城堡一般的古宅，决定不要去惊扰其中蛰居的强大女巫。\
Tooth Fairy surveys the old mansion. To her, it looks more like a small castle than a house. She decides not to disturb the formidable witch dwelling within it.

**牙仙**：女巫小姐可能不希望见到别的客人，你去把蜗牛送给她吧。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Maybe I'm the reason they aren't letting you in. I'll just stay back here.

**纸信圈儿**：那也只能这样了，我会把你介绍给她的。\
**Flutterpage**: Alright then. Stay there, and I'll tell her about you, Miss.

不速之客的主动退让令阴森的守卫者们放松了警惕。女孩步入花园的分岔小径，古怪的植物与魔精纷纷避让出一条道路。\
The Carbuncles lower their guard as Tooth Fairy retreats. The strange plants and critters in the garden clear the way for Flutterpage as she makes her way down the path.

纸信圈儿把蜗牛罐子高高举过头顶，仿佛在展示一件信物。\
Flutterpage raises the snail jar high above her head, as if presenting some kind of token.

**纸信圈儿**：女巫小姐！\
**Flutterpage**: Miss!

**纸信圈儿**：你听得到吗？该起床了——\
**Flutterpage**: Do you hear me? Wakey-wakey!

“喀啷——”\
*creak*

沉重的锁具撞在一起，不甘的铰链发出呻吟。\
The lock clatters heavily, and the hinges on the old oak door give a mournful groan.

**纸信圈儿**：唔。\
**Flutterpage**: Hmm.

**“雾中鬼婆”**：……\
**Fog Hag**: ...

**牙仙**：……！\
**Tooth Fairy**: ...!

**纸信圈儿**：这是这周的蜗牛。\
**Flutterpage**: Here you go, Miss, a fresh batch of snails!

但女巫的眼神紧紧地盯着花园门口那名从未见过的女人。\
She doesn't respond. The witch's stare is fixed on the unfamiliar woman by the garden entrance.

**“雾中鬼婆”**：…………\
**Fog Hag**: ...

**“雾中鬼婆”**：她是谁？\
**Fog Hag**: Who is this?

**纸信圈儿**：她是——嗯？我也没搞懂巫医小姐是谁。\
**Flutterpage**: Hmm, well, I don't know her name, but she's a witch doctor.

**纸信圈儿**：她是坐着汽车来到十字街的，手里还拿着乌卢鲁运动会的宣传单。我想她是来参加乌卢——\
**Flutterpage**: She came here in a car, with a flyer of the Uluru Qualifiers. So I think she's here for the Ulu—

**“雾中鬼婆”**：嗯？！\
**Fog Hag**: Mm?

**纸信圈儿**：哦！我忘记了……你不想听那个词。\
**Flutterpage**: Oh, I forgot that you don't like the word.

**牙仙**：女士，我是为调查黑雾而来，你可以叫我牙仙。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Hello, Miss. I'm here investigating the source of the black fog. You can call me Tooth Fairy.

**“雾中鬼婆”**：出去。\
**Fog Hag**: Go away.

**纸信圈儿**：为什么“出去”？我今天还没有问为什——\
**Flutterpage**: But why? I ain't ask too many "whys," Miss, did I? That was only my first one today.

**纸信圈儿**：噢。\
**Flutterpage**: Oh.

女孩意识到了什么。\
She realizes something.

**纸信圈儿**：好吧……那我今天不能进来玩了吗？你上次不是答应了要再带我练习一次神秘术——\
**Flutterpage**: So, I can't come in at all? You promised you'd help me practice my arcane skill.

**“雾中鬼婆”**：那你的嘴巴里就最好别再蹦出“乌卢鲁”这个词！\
**Fog Hag**: Then you better not let me catch you saying "Uluru" ever again!

女巫有些紧张地从孩子的手中接过了蜗牛罐子，随后关上了大门。\
The witch anxiously snatches the snail jar from the girl's hand and closes the door.

“哐——”\
*slam*

橡木大门合上了。\
The door closes.

**纸信圈儿**：啊……\
**Flutterpage**: Awh ...

**纸信圈儿**：但是，女巫小姐给我留下了一本书……那本画着卡邦克鲁的书。\
**Flutterpage**: Oh, she left me a book. Look, it's got a Carbuncle on it.

**牙仙**：纸信圈儿，快回来。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Come here, Flutterpage. Are you alright?

**纸信圈儿**：我今天本来是打算在她家玩一会的。\
**Flutterpage**: I thought I could play at her house today.

**牙仙**：我带你去别的地方，怎么样？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Would you like to do something else?

**纸信圈儿**：去哪儿呢？\
**Flutterpage**: Like what?

**牙仙**：想和帽子先生交朋友吗？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Like, see your new friend, Mr. Hat?

**纸信圈儿**：帽子先生？\
**Flutterpage**: Mr. Hat?

**宽檐帽**：纸信圈儿小姐，把我戴在头上不会给你带来任何好处。\
**Brimley**: Ms. Flutterpage, I'll ask you to not wear me on your head.

**宽檐帽**：不行，我会飞，不意味着我可以变成一只风筝，我必须要去伦敦的街头巡逻了。\
**Brimley**: I know I can fly, but that doesn't mean you can treat me like a kite. Besides, I'm due to begin my patrol. I need to—

**宽檐帽**：唔啊——\
**Brimley**: WHOAAA!

一阵风将帽子先生吹到了走廊上，纸信圈儿追了出去。\
A gust of wind blows Brimley into the hallway, spurring Flutterpage to give chase.

**福葛先生**：……终于可以坐下来谈一谈了，牙仙女士。首先我必须要对你的冒险精神表示敬佩。\
**Mr. Fog**: That gives us some time for business. First of all, allow me to express my respect for your adventurous spirit.

**福葛先生**：一座被诡异植物包围的女巫阴宅？宅子的女主人还把蜗牛当成食物？噢，你肯定冒了很大的风险。\
**Mr. Fog**: A haunted hag mansion whose owner feeds on snails? To visit her so quickly on your own initiative was a bold move, Ms. Tooth Fairy!

务实的公职人员此刻也不得不承认女巫的存在。\
He now has no choice but to admit the existence of the witch.

**福葛先生**：这是你的茶，按照你的要求，没有加糖。\
**Mr. Fog**: Here's your tea. No sugar, just as you asked.

务实的公职人员当然也不会忘了承诺过的印度红茶。\
And, of course, he has kept the promised Indian tea at the forefront of his mind.

**牙仙**：这位女巫和伦敦大雾的关联性还需要找机会做进一步查验。但在我看来，她似乎不太关心外界的情况。\
**Tooth Fairy**: The connection between this lady and the black fog will require further confirmation. However, judging from our encounter, she doesn't seem to have much concern for the world outside her home.

**牙仙**：不过，“乌卢鲁”这个词会给她带去某种刺激。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I also noted that the word "Uluru" seemed to irritate her.

**福葛先生**：乌卢鲁？她不喜欢乌卢鲁运动会吗？\
**Mr. Fog**: Uluru? As in the Uluru Games? Not a fan, I take it.

**福葛先生**：那也是，一千个神秘学家里，总得有那么一两个不会为乌卢鲁运动会发狂，不然这个世界就太完美了。\
**Mr. Fog**: It's certainly odd for an arcanist to have a negative impression of the Games, though not unprecedented.

**福葛先生**：听听这个，牙仙女士，这或许能让那个女巫满意。\
**Mr. Fog**: Which reminds me of this letter. I suspect our Fog Lady might be glad to hear it.

福葛先生将一封有声信置于二人之间，崭新的信纸变化为一张大嘴。\
Mr. Fog places a voiced letter between the two of them. The paper swiftly transforms into a wide mouth.

**有声信**：“圣洛夫基金会乌卢鲁运动会组织委员会致信乌卢鲁伦敦预选赛组织委员会：”\
**Voiced Letter**: "Letter from the St. Pavlov Foundation Uluru Games Organizing Committee to the Uluru London Qualifiers Organizing Committee."

**有声信**：“……抄送伦敦清洁大气委员会办公室……”\
**Voiced Letter**: " ... copied to the Office of the London Atmospheric Clean-up Committee ..."

**有声信**：“鉴于伦敦空气质量在短期内极度恶化，并存在未探明的神秘学肺结核致病原……”\
**Voiced Letter**: "Due to the rapid deterioration of air quality in London and the presence of an unidentified arcane-related tuberculosis outbreak ..."

**有声信**：“为保护运动员与现场观众的身体健康，故此通知：乌卢鲁伦敦预选赛将酌情取消……\
**Voiced Letter**: " ... we regretfully have decided that the Uluru London Qualifiers will be canceled until further notice to protect the health of competitors and spectators."

**有声信**：“有意向参赛的运动员请转至巴黎或其他城市的分赛场报名参加预选赛。”\
**Voiced Letter**: "Competitors still wishing to participate are encouraged to register for the qualifiers in Paris or other cities."

信纸叠好自己，伴随着福葛先生的一声叹息，它落回桌面上。\
The paper folds itself up and drops back onto the table. Mr. Fog sighs.

**福葛先生**：我把十字街里发现的异常上报给基金会，这就是他们的回信。\
**Mr. Fog**: I received this shortly after submitting my report concerning the events on Cross Street.

**牙仙**：为了所有人的健康着想，伦敦确实不再适合举办运动会。\
**Tooth Fairy**: They're right. It's better for everyone's health.

**福葛先生**：我头疼得想把脑袋摘下来当球踢！\
**Mr. Fog**: No objections here, but it's certain to cause a stir!

**福葛先生**：牙仙女士，你见过十字街里生活的神秘学家了，如果他们知道预选赛会被取消，一定会发疯的。\
**Mr. Fog**: Ms. Tooth Fairy, you saw how passionate the citizens were about this event, what it means to them. They'll eat us alive when we announce this.

**福葛先生**：如果光是这一件事倒还算好说……因空气质量而取消预选赛，这对王室来说也会是一次莫大的耻辱。\
**Mr. Fog**: So much more so that it's canceled because of air quality. The Firm will not be pleased, I can assure you.

**福葛先生**：大英帝国的伟大首都会成为欧洲和全世界神秘学家的笑柄！\
**Mr. Fog**: This great city will be the laughingstock of Europe, if not the entire world!

**福葛先生**：除非……除非我有办法让伦敦拨云见日，这样或许能说服组委会……\
**Mr. Fog**: Unless ... Unless there's a way to clean the air in London. Perhaps then I might convince the Foundation to reconsider.

**牙仙**：雾行者先生，现在距离乌卢鲁预选赛开始，只剩下不到三周。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Mr. Fog, there's only three weeks left before the qualifiers.

**牙仙**：你没有办法在这么短的时间内解决弥漫在整个伦敦的暗黄色雾气，何况有关“黑雾”和特殊肺结核的问题，我们还没有多少头绪。\
**Tooth Fairy**: It's a serious effort just to address the smog over London, let alone this new black fog and the disease that has come with it.

**福葛先生**：也就是说，我还有三周时间——一周时间用来思考，一周时间用来执行，一周时间用来验收结果和办理手续。\
**Mr. Fog**: Three weeks. One for making plans, one for enacting said plans, and still one more for the final procedures.

福葛先生一屁股坐在办公椅上，双手抱胸，以恼怒的眼神盯着桌上的有声信。\
He slumps into his chair with his arms crossed and glares furiously at the voiced letter on the desk.

**牙仙**：你在做什么，福葛先生？\
**Tooth Fairy**: What are you doing now, Mr. Fog?

**福葛先生**：我在思考，牙仙女士——从现在开始。\
**Mr. Fog**: Thinking, Ms. Tooth Fairy, is how I make the plans.

被追逐的帽子终于找到了回来的路。\
Brimley, fleeing pursuit, eventually finds his way back.

**宽檐帽**：很……很抱歉打断你刚开始不久的思考，福葛伙计，我的巡逻任务不得不提前结束。还有，牙仙女士？\
**Brimley**: Forgive me for interrupting, Arthur, but I had to call off my patrol earlier than expected. I'm afraid I need a favor of you, Ms. Tooth Fairy.

**牙仙**：嗯？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Hmm?

**宽檐帽**：你愿意向伦敦的肺结核病人伸出援手吗？\
**Brimley**: Would you mind helping us with some of the sick?

**宽檐帽**：——那场黑雾出现过后，患有“煤炭肺结核”的病人像大自流盆地的野兔一样泛滥成灾了！\
**Brimley**: After that black fog rolled through, patients with this "tuber-coal-sis" variant seem to be multiplying as fast as hares in the Great Artesian Basin!

## LD-04 久远的辉煌 / Past Glory

**笃笃骨**：林中之路，雾霭迷蒙。\
**Willow**: Through misty woods, on paths concealed by haze.

柳堆中的火焰，祭场中的女巫。\
By the willow fire, a witch is dancing in the ritual ground.

祭祀者在她创造的一千道阴影中独舞。\
She performs her dance alone. Only the shadows cast by the flames accompany her.

**笃笃骨**：花朵结出硕果，牛羊诞下子嗣。\
**Willow**: Flowers bear fruit, and beasts give offspring's way.

**笃笃骨**：炽热的双眼，刺破云雾！\
**Willow**: With eyes of fire, pierce through the cloudy maze!

**笃笃骨**：该死的，仪式失败了。\
**Willow**: Ugh! Failed again. Damn it!

女巫狠狠地掐着她的右腿，指尖已然发白。\
She clenches her right leg, her fingers turning white at the tips.

**笃笃骨**：就因为做不好那个动作！\
**Willow**: I won't get anywhere so long as I can't move right.

**花园卡邦克鲁**：吱吱——！咯啊！！\
**Vines Carbuncle**: Squeak! Squeak!!

一向温顺的花园卡邦克鲁有些癫狂地嚣叫着。那本该具有安抚效果的仪式因为一步之差，成为了使它们喋血的战鼓。\
The typically docile Carbuncles are now locked in a frenzied shrieking match. What should have been a calming ritual has quickly turned into a bloodied war drum, and all because of a single misstep.

**笃笃骨**：够了！这家里有我一个发疯的就够了！\
**Willow**: Enough! The last thing this haunted old place needs is another crazy creature!

**纸信圈儿**：笃笃骨——！\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Willow—

**笃笃骨**：——！\
**Willow**: ...!

**笃笃骨**：天杀的——！\
**Willow**: I swear to God—

女巫摔倒在柳条火堆旁，炽热的火舌明事理地骤然熄灭，笃笃骨赶忙从杂物中扯过一张毛毯遮住腿部。\
She collapses by the willow fire, causing the intense flames to suddenly die down. She swiftly grabs a blanket from the pile to cover her legs.

**笃笃骨**：无论你是什么东西，有没有脖子，我都要掐死你！\
**Willow**: Whatever thing you are, don't think I won't strangle you to death with my bare hands!

她挣扎着要起身，一条腿却陡然卸力。\
She struggles to her feet, but just as she's about to stand, one leg gives way.

**笃笃骨**：呃——\
**Willow**: Ugh!

**纸信圈儿**：呀！\
**Flutterpage**: Ah!

扒在窗户上的女孩跃入室内。\
The little girl tumbles through the window and into the room.

**笃笃骨**：该死的！\
**Willow**: Bloody!

第二次尝试爬起，女巫却只能撑起自己半截身体。她仰起头，仿佛看见了一张缝缝补补一个世纪的旧床单。\
She tries to lift herself up for the second time but can only support half of her body. She looks up to find a little face among a pile of stitched and re-stitched clothes.

不会有比这样更令她难堪和恼火的见面方式了。\
There could be no more embarrassing or infuriating way for another to behold her.

**笃笃骨**：你？你来这里做什么？！\
**Willow**: You! What are you doing here?

**纸信圈儿**：我想向你展示你叫我练习的神秘术。\
**Flutterpage**: I only wanted to show you the arcane skill you taught me.

纸信圈儿灵巧地从地上爬了起来，顺便还蹦着抖了抖灰尘。\
Flutterpage nimbly gets back on her feet, bouncing around as she shakes off the dust.

看见纸信圈儿安然无恙，女巫别过脸去，隐掉了些许担忧。\
Seeing that the girl is unharmed, the witch turns her face, hiding her fleeting look of concern.

**纸信圈儿**：可你的心情很糟糕，发生什么事了？那次我也没有在其他人面前叫你笃笃骨。\
**Flutterpage**: But you are in a bad mood, aren't you? What happened? I promise I didn't call you Ms. Willow in front of others!

**纸信圈儿**：但是你说在没有人的时候可以这么叫你，对吗？\
**Flutterpage**: You said I can call you Ms. Willow when there's just you and me, right?

**笃笃骨**：小鬼，你用你头上的小皮球想想，这根本不是名字的事。\
**Willow**: And you actually listened? First time for everything, ay? But it's not about what you call me.

**纸信圈儿**：那是什么事？\
**Flutterpage**: Then what is it?

纸信圈儿带着疑惑凝视着仍然趴在地上的笃笃骨。突然，她想明白了。\
She stares at Willow in confusion. Suddenly, she realizes why she's lying on the ground.

**纸信圈儿**：——我扶你起来。\
**Flutterpage**: Let me help you up.

**笃笃骨**：我不用你扶。\
**Willow**: I don't need it.

笃笃骨轻甩手腕，外套与帽子便如犬般扑到了自己的身上。\
With a flick of her wrist, Willow's coat and hat leap onto her like loyal dogs.

她第三次尝试爬起，靠在粗糙的石柱上才勉强站直了身子。\
She tries to stand up for a third time, using the rough stone pillar beside her for support, and finally manages to straighten herself out.

**笃笃骨**：我难道没有和你说过，我不需要你叫我起床吗？\
**Willow**: So then, if you value my words so highly, what about the time I told you I don't need a knocker-upper?

**纸信圈儿**：我不是来叫你起床的，要去工厂的人早在两个小时之前就出门了，我已经把整条街的窗户都敲了个遍。\
**Flutterpage**: I remember! You told me, "There's no sense waking me up for anythin'. I don't have any work to go to."

**纸信圈儿**：而你是不用工作的。\
**Flutterpage**: But I'm not here to wake you up, am I? I already did that for the whole street hours ago!

**笃笃骨**：……工作完了就哪儿凉快哪儿待着去，允许你踏入花园不是你放肆的理由。\
**Willow**: Oh, have you now? Then maybe you can buzz off and bother someone else. I didn't give my permission to let annoying little flies in my house.

**笃笃骨**：我有很重要的事情要做，现在别来烦我。快离开。\
**Willow**: I'm in the middle of something important. So leave me be.

笃笃骨拽过一根扫帚杆，指向被纸信圈儿打开的窗户。\
Willow grabs a broom handle and points it toward the window Flutterpage opened.

**纸信圈儿**：我不会烦你，我会讲得很快。\
**Flutterpage**: Just one more question, Miss! I'll be quick.

**纸信圈儿**：牙仙女士和福葛先生说十字街的女巫小姐用黑色的雾让人生怪病了，但这不是你做的，对吧？\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Tooth Fairy and Mr. Fog say you made people sick with the black fog, but I know you didn't do it, did you?

**纸信圈儿**：你从来没说过你会召唤黑色的雾。\
**Flutterpage**: You never told me you can summon black fog.

**笃笃骨**：我真是受够了，如果你来敲窗户就是为了说这些鬼话——\
**Willow**: Done with all that nonsense, are you? If that's all you knocked on my window for—

**纸信圈儿**：如果不是你做的，我可以把实话告诉他们。\
**Flutterpage**: But if you didn't, I can tell them the truth.

**纸信圈儿**：或者你也可以帮他们找到黑雾，你是我认识的最厉害的女巫。\
**Flutterpage**: Or you could even help them find the black fog! You're the best witch I know.

**笃笃骨**：他们的死活与我无关。\
**Willow**: Their problem is no concern of mine.

**纸信圈儿**：但……我偷听到了一个消息，来，我告诉你。\
**Flutterpage**: Em, oh, but I did hear somethin'. I was thinkin' maybe you'd like to hear it, too.

**纸信圈儿**：圣洛夫基金会发来信函——\
**Flutterpage**: Letter from St. Pavlov Foundation:

**纸信圈儿**：“鉴——鉴于……什么？恶……恶化，并存在未——未探明的神秘学……神秘学肺结核……”\
**Flutterpage**: Um, due to ... what? De-teary-on air quality? And arcane tube-or-key-old-kiss ...?

**纸信圈儿**：嗯……“故此通知：乌卢鲁……将——酌——酌情取消……”\
**Flutterpage**: Um. They said the Uluru Qualifiers are canceled.

**笃笃骨**：……别背了。\
**Willow**: Stop.

**笃笃骨**：你知道这些词是什么意思吗？\
**Willow**: Do you understand at all what you're saying?

**纸信圈儿**：我不知道，可——\
**Flutterpage**: No, but—

**笃笃骨**：出去。\
**Willow**: Go away.

**纸信圈儿**：唔？\
**Flutterpage**: Aww ...

**笃笃骨**：——出去！\
**Willow**: I said get out!

女巫两手钳着纸信圈儿，半拖半拽地靠近了窗户。\
She seizes Flutterpage with both hands, half dragging, half pulling her toward the open window.

**纸信圈儿**：啊！\
**Flutterpage**: Ahhh!

**笃笃骨**：我最讨厌屡教不改的小孩，而你——\
**Willow**: You know what I don't want to hear, eh lass? Your voice!

女孩被抛出了窗户，像脱了线的风筝那样飞走了。\
Flutterpage is flung out the window and carried away like a kite with a broken string on the breeze.

**笃笃骨**：——就是这个小孩！\
**Willow**: And your infernal knocking!

**纸信圈儿**：啊——\
**Flutterpage**: Whoaa!

**笃笃骨**：永远——永远别想再踏进我家一步！\
**Willow**: Don't you never take another step into my house, never!

“哐。”\
*crash*

屋内再次恢复了熟悉的沉寂，一如过去的十年般了无生机。\
The room reverts to its familiar silence, no life save for its solitary resident, just as it has been for the past decade.

临时披上的外套与帽子滑到了地上，笃笃骨扶着右腿，一瘸一拐地靠近装满瓶罐的储物台。\
Her hastily thrown-on coat and hat slide to the floor as Willow leans on her right leg and limps over to the storage table filled with bottles and jars.

昨天收下的蜗牛留有足够使用的黏液，她把罐子里的液体倒入一口坩埚中。\
There's still enough mucus left over from yesterday's snails for her to use. She pours the liquid from the jar into the cauldron.

**笃笃骨**：还剩下一点……\
**Willow**: Just a wee bit left.

她点起火苗，开始熬煮坩埚中的润滑脂。\
She sets the fire alight, and the lubricant starts to bubble in the cauldron.

**笃笃骨**：吃蜗牛？呵——\
**Willow**: Heh! Eat snails? Hmph!

**笃笃骨**：就让他们觉得我真会生吃蜗牛吧。\
**Willow**: Let them think what they will. I don't care.

**笃笃骨**：雾中鬼婆……青蛙和苍蝇化身的怪物……古代炼金术师恶心坩埚中爬出来的失败之作……\
**Willow**: The Fog Hag, a toad monster, the failed work of an ancient alchemist ...

**笃笃骨**：是的，躲在十字街古宅中的女巫，雾中鬼婆，丑陋、善妒、心胸狭隘——太好了，还有什么比这些更适合夏洛特·奥黑根？\
**Willow**: Yes, yes, of course. Charlotte O'Hagan, you're nothing but an ugly, evil, terrifying Fog Hag living in a haunted house. You deserve every bit of it.

她站起身，端详有些歪斜的旧油画。泛黄的颜料与蒙尘加重了画中黄昏的烈度。\
She lifts her eyes and gazes out the window. To her surprise, she can see the moon, a flurry of small clouds slowly making their way across it, and a flock of silhouetted birds swooping and swerving in tacit harmony.

绵延的多石丘陵上有洁白的羊群漫步，身穿黑袍的女巫们结群而舞。\
Like the white sheep that roamed those vast rocky hills. Like the witches in black robes who danced together in perfect unison.

**笃笃骨**：多好的年代——女巫们一点也不用担心自己在睡梦中被抓出屋子，用一根木桩刺穿，或者在薪柴上烧死。\
**Willow**: What an age—At last witches no longer need worry about being captured in their sleep, pierced on a stake, or burnt alive.

**广播员**：“即将登场的是爱尔兰的女巫，她是十万分之一的四叶酢浆草——”\
**Announcer**: Our next competitor is our witch from Ireland, a once-in-a-generation talent!

**笃笃骨**：古老的祭祀也变换了模样……女巫们可以用富有灵性的舞步一分高下，就像一场愉快的游戏——\
**Willow**: The ancient rituals are different now. We dance, communicating with spirits, like a joyful game.

**广播员**：“乌卢鲁——乌卢鲁——”\
**Announcer**: The Uluru Games—

**笃笃骨**：一场优雅的比赛……\
**Willow**: Or a graceful competition ...

**广播员**：“自由祭祀项目的冠军是——”\
**Announcer**: And the winner for the Floor Ritual is—

**笃笃骨**：一次令人渴望的……\
**Willow**: A desirable ...

**笃笃骨**：——！\
**Willow**: ...!

**笃笃骨**：润滑脂！\
**Willow**: I left the pot on!

烧焦的烟雾宣告着为时已晚，新鲜的黏液在失调的火候中化为煤渣般的粘稠物。\
The smell signals a point of no return for the lubricant, and its appearance confirms it as she sees a small blackened mass stuck to the bottom of the cauldron.

假肢因缺少润滑而产生的摩擦硌得笃笃骨髋骨处有些痒，膝盖处的球形关节相互咬合着，蚕食着，吱呀的声响从不肯放过她。\
Willow's prosthetic leg grinds and creaks as the joints rub up against each other, causing her hip to itch.

**笃笃骨**：该死的！\
**Willow**: Feck! Fecking! Feck!

**笃笃骨**：——该死的废物！\
**Willow**: Fit for the rubbish now!

**笃笃骨**：废物……\
**Willow**: Rubbish!

## LD-05 小叫醒工 / Little Knocker-Upper

清晨的第一声鸡鸣并不动人，它预告着一天的劳苦和麻烦事即将到来。\
As morning breaks, the rooster crows, announcing the start of another day of hard labor for the people of the East End.

众多造船厂与纺织厂正嗷嗷待哺，急需用大量的煤炭、燃油与工人来喂饱。\
In this land of industry, shipyards, and factories, there is a dire need of coal, fuel, and the labor to sustain them.

**纸信圈儿**：——你好，先生，太太，该起床了。\
**Flutterpage**: Good mornin'! Sir, madam, this here is your wake-up call!

**纸信圈儿**：天真的快要亮了——该去上工了！\
**Flutterpage**: Rise and shine! Wakey time!

纸信圈儿仰起头，灰中透蓝的天幕笼罩在头顶，太阳、星星和月亮都还不见踪影。\
Flutterpage looks up to the gray sky above. There is only a touch of blue, and no sun, stars, or moon to be seen.

**十字街居民**：够了——够了，小崽子，我早就醒了，不要再像一只讨人厌的苍蝇那样来烦我了！\
**Resident**: Enough! I said enough with it, girl! I'm already awake, ain't I? So, stop buzzing around!

在一盆洗脚水落下之前，经验老到的小叫醒工就已经灵巧地躲到了一旁，钻过小巷来到相邻的另一条街道。\
The seasoned knocker-upper deftly dodges the basin full of foot-washing water that has just been flung out the window and slips through the alley and onto the next street.

工作仍需继续。\
She still has a job to do.

**纸信圈儿**：起床起床，天就快要亮了！\
**Flutterpage**: Wakey, wakey! Morning's here!

**纸信圈儿**：威尔森太太？——你可不能再迟到了，那个猪眼睛的先生把打人的柳条换成皮带了！\
**Flutterpage**: Mrs. Wilson? You awake? You can't be late again, or old Mister Pig-Eyes will be on you with his belt!

**纸信圈儿**：嗯？为什么没有反应？\
**Flutterpage**: What happened? Didn't she hear me?

有人从身后推了她一把。\
Suddenly, she's shoved from behind.

**纸信圈儿**：呀——\
**Flutterpage**: Ahhh!

**纸信圈儿**：是谁？\
**Flutterpage**: Oi! Who did that?

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：别吵了，利伯蒂，你不知道威尔森太太已经生病了吗？\
**Freddy the Rascal**: Shut up already, Liberti. Didn't you know Mrs. Wilson was sick?

**纸信圈儿**：她生什么病了？难道她的喉咙里也像吞下了一颗煤炭那样疼吗？\
**Flutterpage**: She's sick? What's wrong? It doesn't hurt like swallowin' a burnin' coal, does it?

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：呵，你可真会说，谁教你的？\
**Freddy the Rascal**: Who told you that?

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：但你说的没错，就是这么回事。一种全新的诅咒，越来越多人中招了。\
**Freddy the Rascal**: Yeah, maybe. Plenty of folks been gettin' that too. My dad says it's a curse!

**纸信圈儿**：这不是诅咒，你是白痴吗？\
**Flutterpage**: It's not a curse, dummy!

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：你才是白痴，利伯蒂，我知道你总是偷偷去见那个鬼婆，但她骗了你，还在报复街坊的邻居。\
**Freddy the Rascal**: I'm no dummy, Liberti. You are! Believin' anythin' what that hag told you! She's a dirty, ugly, old liar, and she's the one who cursed everyone here!

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：她一辈子见不得光，被阳光晒到就会现出原形——一只癞蛤蟆，所以乌卢鲁预选赛的欢庆集市让她不快活了。\
**Freddy the Rascal**: She's a toad! A toad what can't get out of her house to see sunlight, and decided to curse us all just 'cause she didn't like the fair!

**纸信圈儿**：胡说，别来烦我了！我还要工作呢。\
**Flutterpage**: Have you gone off your rocker, Freddy! Just leave me alone! I got work to do.

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：工作？你在开什么鬼玩笑——早晨起来敲人家的窗户就是工作吗？\
**Freddy the Rascal**: That's work, eh? You call knockin' on people's window work?

男孩捋起袖管，拍了拍手臂。\
The boy rolls up his sleeve and pats his bicep.

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：我可以爬到蒸汽轮机里头拧下一颗比你脑袋还大的螺栓，还可以钻进烟囱里刮下煤渣，你做得到吗？\
**Freddy the Rascal**: I climb up in the steam turbines to tighten up the screws, and I clean them chimneys from the inside. Think you can do that, eh?

**纸信圈儿**：我不想去拧下一颗比我脑袋还大的螺栓，也不喜欢闻烟囱里的味道。\
**Flutterpage**: But I don't want to tighten screws or climb up chimneys! I don't like the smells.

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：那你喜欢闻现在的味道吗？看看那个鬼婆干的好事！\
**Freddy the Rascal**: Oh, so you like the smell of this black fog, do you? All thanks to your wicked hag friend.

**纸信圈儿**：走开！\
**Flutterpage**: Go away!

长长的晾衣杆敲上男孩的膝盖，磕出一声脆响。\
She whips a clothesline pole at the boy's knee with a sharp crack.

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：嗷——\
**Freddy the Rascal**: Ow-ah!

男孩向女孩扑过去，却在一大把碎布条中迷失了目标。\
The boy leaps toward the girl but loses her among the heap of rags.

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：……？\
**Freddy the Rascal**: Huh?

他随着声音扭过脖子，惊讶地发现敲打膝盖的仇敌已经轻巧地从自己头顶飞跃。\
He swivels his head toward the sound and stands there shocked as Flutterpage deftly leaps over him.

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：搞什么？\
**Freddy the Rascal**: What the ...

**纸信圈儿**：女巫小姐教我的。\
**Flutterpage**: The fog lady taught me this.

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：啊，女巫……你这个小怪物和她真是好一对儿！\
**Freddy the Rascal**: Lady? You mean that hag? I should've guessed you'd be that ugly toad witch's apprentice!

**纸信圈儿**：你别想和我做朋友了！\
**Flutterpage**: You're not my friend anymore!

纸信圈儿向十字街的深处跑去。\
She runs off deeper into Cross Street.

怪异的花园一切如旧，古宅还是那座云雾中的孤岛。\
The old mansion looks just as it always does. From the strange garden to the ominous building half lost in the haze of the smog.

但纸信圈儿有种说不上来的陌生感。\
Even so, Flutterpage is hit by an unusual feeling, one she can't quite place.

**纸信圈儿**：今天不是和女巫小姐见面的日子，但她上次把我赶出家门了，我可以去说一句“对不起”。\
**Flutterpage**: It's not snail delivery day, but after she threw me out of the house last time, maybe I'll go apologize.

**纸信圈儿**：然后我就又可以跟着她学些戏法，或者翻翻她家那些画着好玩的东西的书。\
**Flutterpage**: Maybe then I can learn some more tricks from her, or at least read her books!

**花园卡邦克鲁**：吱吱——？\
**Vines Carbuncle**: Squeak?

坏脾气的生物警惕地盯着眼前的花园常客。\
The creature eyes her wearily.

**纸信圈儿**：嘿，又是你。\
**Flutterpage**: Hello, hello!

**纸信圈儿**：你太坏了，上次为什么要把牙仙女士拦在外面？她是个好人，给我吃了酸酸甜甜的消——呃，“瞎咬”药物？\
**Flutterpage**: Now, why didn't you let Ms. Tooth Fairy in last time? She's not a bad person. She even gave me some flyin' medicine. It was sweet and sour.

**纸信圈儿**：女巫小姐太孤独了，她需要交一些新朋友，或许也需要一些“瞎咬”药物。\
**Flutterpage**: You think Ms. Willow's lonely? She needs new friends, and maybe some flyin' medicine too?

**花园卡邦克鲁**：吱！\
**Vines Carbuncle**: Squeak!

花园卡邦克鲁仿佛并不认可女孩的诊断，它左右横跳，摆出明显的抗拒姿态。\
The Carbuncle seems to reject her assessment, leaping side to side in a clear display of defiance.

**纸信圈儿**：好吧，上次爬窗户是我的错，但为什么女巫小姐会那么生气？是我打扰到她吃早餐了？\
**Flutterpage**: But this time I won't go through the window. Not that I get why she was so mad? Was it that I stopped her from eatin' breakfast maybe?

**纸信圈儿**：我可以去问个清楚？嗯，这次我走正门，她应该就不会生气了。\
**Flutterpage**: Well, time to figure it out. I bet if I walk in from the front door, she won't be so angry.

纸信圈儿像往常那样踏入花园，卡邦克鲁与神奇的植物们向来不是她的阻碍。\
Flutterpage enters the garden like she always does, except this time, the Carbuncles don't make way for her.

**花园卡邦克鲁**：吱！吱！\
**Vines Carbuncle**: *roar*

但这次却是一场意外——花园卡邦克鲁们扑了上来。\
They leap at her.

**纸信圈儿**：怎么了？！\
**Flutterpage**: What's wrong?

纸信圈儿挥动晾衣杆，却无法起到驱赶的效果。黑糊糊的生物们不怀好意地向女孩聚拢。\
Flutterpage swings the clothesline pole, but fails to drive them off. They close in on her, malice in their eyes.

还好，援兵从雾霭中策马而来。\
Fortunately, reinforcements come galloping through the smog.

**宽檐帽**：纸信圈儿小姐，你怎么在这？！上帝保佑——但愿本骑手没有错失良机！\
**Brimley**: Ms. Flutterpage? What in the blazes are you doing here?! Good lord! I hope you didn't get hurt!

**纸信圈儿**：帽子先生！\
**Flutterpage**: Mr. Hat!

**宽檐帽**：卡洛琳小姐，请你在安全的距离外等候。\
**Brimley**: Ms. Bartley, I'd advise you to please stay a safe distance back.

**卡洛琳**：不……\
**Caroline Bartley**: No ...

**卡洛琳**：这花园……夏洛特，你的品味已经糟糕到这种地步了？\
**Caroline Bartley**: Just look at the state of this garden. Oh, Charlotte, what have you been through to fall this far?

**宽檐帽**：太好了，你完好无损，纸信圈儿小姐。\
**Brimley**: Thank goodness, you're in one piece.

**纸信圈儿**：我不明白，他们从来不会咬人的。\
**Flutterpage**: I ... I don't get it. They ain't never bit me before.

**宽檐帽**：对环境中的危险时刻保持警惕，小姐，即使它只是一颗石头，这是一名骑手能够传授给你的经验。\
**Brimley**: Well, you must always stay alert when you encounter critters, even in a familiar place. That's some genuine ranger's advice.

**纸信圈儿**：骑手？可是你并没有真正的马，这也能叫骑手吗？\
**Flutterpage**: A ranger? Are you really a ranger? Can you be a ranger without a real horse? Will I get a hat like you if I get to be a ranger?

**宽檐帽**：哎呀……\
**Brimley**: Errrrr.

还好一顶帽子不至于露出尴尬的表情。\
Fortunately, a hat's range of expressions doesn't include awkwardness, or much else for that matter.

**纸信圈儿**：还有，小姐，你好，你也是来找女巫小姐的吗？\
**Flutterpage**: Hi, Miss. Are you here for the lady livin' here?

纸信圈儿好奇地围着那位从未见过的小姐走了一圈。\
Flutterpage circles the unfamiliar lady, looking her up and down.

**纸信圈儿**：你也像笃……夏洛特小姐那样挺着背，昂着头，你就像……白天鹅。\
**Flutterpage**: Miss, you look a lot like Ms. Willow—the Fog Lady. So straight and proper like a swan.

**卡洛琳**：笃？笃笃骨？\
**Caroline Bartley**: Ms. Willow, you said?

**纸信圈儿**：唔。\
**Flutterpage**: Hmm.

纸信圈儿赶忙捂住嘴，旋即发现这个名字并不是她自己说出口的。\
Flutterpage claps her mouth before realizing she wasn't the one to utter this name.

**纸信圈儿**：是的，笃笃骨……她也允许你这么叫她的名字吗？\
**Flutterpage**: Y-Yes, Ms. Willow. Did she say you were allowed to call her that too, Miss?

**卡洛琳**：允许？\
**Caroline Bartley**: Allowed?

**卡洛琳**：唉——\
**Caroline Bartley**: *sigh*

即使是一声叹息，也蕴藏着优雅的旋律。\
Even her sigh carries an elegant, melodious quality.

**卡洛琳**：她现在变成了一个怎样的……怪胎？\
**Caroline Bartley**: What kind of nutter has she become?

**卡洛琳**：谢谢你带我来这，宽檐帽先生，剩下的事让我自己处理吧。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Thank you for taking me here, Mr. Brimley. I can handle the rest myself.

卡洛琳轻轻摆手，示意她已不愿再聊。\
She makes a gentle motion with her hand, signaling that she has finished talking.

**宽檐帽**：我们先走吧，纸信圈儿小姐，你不应该再留在这儿了。\
**Brimley**: You're welcome. Let's go shall we, eh little tacker? It's not safe to leave you here.

**宽檐帽**：我带你去医院见牙仙女士，她说希望得到你的帮助。\
**Brimley**: I'll escort you to the hospital. Ms. Tooth Fairy needs your help.

**纸信圈儿**：哦……\
**Flutterpage**: Alright.

纸信圈儿拽着宽檐帽的大衣离开了花园，她三五次地回头，每一次看到的都是卡洛琳小姐一动不动的背影。\
Flutterpage holds onto Brimley's coat as the two of them leave the garden. She looks back a few times. Caroline remains totally unmoving.

仿佛她用凝视就足以与房屋的主人对话。\
It's as though she can converse with the owner of the house through her stare alone.

**纸信圈儿**：我没有见过这样子的医院，首先，医院要装在一栋房子里。\
**Flutterpage**: I thought a hospital was a big, big buildin'! This is more like a fair, only with sick people.

病人们躺在简易的钢架床上，原本白色的床单沾染了不少黄与灰的污渍。\
Patients lie on basic steel-frame beds, their once-pristine white sheets now marked with yellow and gray stains.

在这景观之下，乌卢鲁运动会热情洋溢的旌旗也显得萎靡不振了。\
In the face of such a scene, the bright flags of the Uluru Games now look lifeless and limp.

**宽檐帽**：这当然并非通常意义上的“医院”，所以福葛先生称之为“伦敦特殊煤炭肺结核患者应急救助与管理中心”。\
**Brimley**: Well, you're right there, mate. It's not your typical hospital. Arthur's calling it the "London Emergency Relief Centre for Special Tuberculosis Patients."

**纸信圈儿**：那不就是医院吗？\
**Flutterpage**: But it's still kind of a hospital, ain't it?

女孩儿不再去想词句的差别到底在哪里，笃笃骨花园前陌生小姐的背影在她脑中还是挥之不去。\
She doesn't linger on this thought for long. The image of the unfamiliar lady in Willow's garden won't leave her mind.

**纸信圈儿**：“白天鹅小姐”到底是谁？她不是十字街的人，她是从哪儿来的？她怎么会认识笃……夏洛特小姐？\
**Flutterpage**: Who's that Swan lady? She's not from Cross Street. How did she know Ms. Wi-Fog Lady?

**福葛先生**：你是说卡洛琳女士吧？卡洛琳女士会是我们的救星——也许吧！\
**Mr. Fog**: Swan? I suppose you mean Ms. Caroline Bartley. We're hoping she'll be our lifesaver.

脸色发灰的福葛先生出现在他们身后。\
Mr. Fog appears behind them, looking rather pale.

**纸信圈儿**：救星？\
**Flutterpage**: Lifesaver?

**福葛先生**：没错——救星。\
**Mr. Fog**: Exactly so.

福葛先生的眼中闪着一丝诡谲的光芒，他目视前方，似乎只是在自言自语。\
There's a curious spark behind Mr. Fog's eyes. He looks straight ahead as he speaks.

**福葛先生**：瞧见没，老帽儿，我们公职人员可不全是一群只会就着红茶看《泰晤士报》的无能之士。\
**Mr. Fog**: See, my hat friend, we civil servants can actually accomplish a thing or two!

**福葛先生**：我找到了卡洛琳，她是个大人物，大明星，知名乌卢鲁运动员！更重要的是，她还是个知情人士。\
**Mr. Fog**: We found Ms. Bartley, a shining star of Uluru, a talented competitor! And above all, she's an insider.

**福葛先生**：据她所说，十字街的女巫和她曾是老相识。她前几天刚到伦敦，正在打听女巫的下落——多棒的巧合！\
**Mr. Fog**: She arrived in London days ago, looking for our Fog Lady. She claimed to be an old acquaintance. Some luck, isn't it?

**福葛先生**：她会搞清楚黑雾和肺结核是怎么一回事的——对了，那个女巫被人称作笃笃骨，真是个——难以评价的名字，嘿嘿。\
**Mr. Fog**: If she can figure out the connection between her, the black fog, and this fiery TB—Oh! Speaking of which, that "Ms. Willow" truly has a ... special name. Heh heh.

**宽檐帽**：嘿嘿？你在笑什么？你多久没睡了，福葛伙计？\
**Brimley**: Heh heh? What are you laughing at? How long have you been up, mate?

一个猜测浮现于宽檐帽的“脑海”，就是他的好伙计可能一周都没怎么合眼。\
A thought crosses Brimley's "mind." His partner has probably hardly slept all week.

一阵荣光在雾行者面孔上来了又去，如同灰蒙蒙的天空中，偶然有阳光穿透云层的罅隙。\
A burst of glorious vigor illuminates the Fogwalker's face, like sunlight breaking through a gap in the gray sky.

**福葛先生**：从来没有比现在更好的时刻了，我可是精神百倍！\
**Mr. Fog**: Sleep? Who needs to sleep at a time like this? I'm more than energetic. I'm a veritable locomotive, better than ever!

**宽檐帽**：或许你该合眼了，福葛伙计。\
**Brimley**: Arthur, you need to get some shut-eye, mate.

**福葛先生**：什么？不，我只是路过“伦敦特殊煤炭肺结核患者应急救助与管理中心”，你以为我是回家睡觉的吗？才不是这样。\
**Mr. Fog**: Is that what you think? That I'll just go back home for a little rest now? Now of all times? Dead wrong, mate. We've got rounds to make at the London Emergency Relief Centre for Special Tuberculosis Patients.

**福葛先生**：来吧，老帽儿，我们还有一整个伦敦要拯救。\
**Mr. Fog**: Come with me, my chapeau chap! We've got a city to save!

福葛先生挽起棍马，强行带走了他的帽子斥候。\
Mr. Fog grabs the hobbyhorse and forcibly drags Brimley away with him.

**宽檐帽**：喔……喔！去找牙仙女士，纸信圈儿小姐！她说你的神秘术可能会起作用！\
**Brimley**: Oh, alright. Ms. Flutterpage, go find Ms. Tooth Fairy, would you? She said your arcane skill might be of some help!

雾行者与他的同僚很快就消失在伦敦街头。\
The two of them quickly vanish into the streets.

**纸信圈儿**：……我的神秘术？\
**Flutterpage**: My arcane skill?

**纸信圈儿**：好吧，或许牙仙女士会告诉我我的神秘术有什么用。那我就去找牙仙女士……可她在哪里？\
**Flutterpage**: Help? How can I help a witch doctor? Maybe Ms. Tooth Fairy will tell me. But where is she?

**纸信圈儿**：这里到处都是人，大家都埋着头忙碌，根本分不清谁是谁。但是牙仙女士身边有金色的仙子，我或许可以看见她……\
**Flutterpage**: So many people here. I can hardly tell them from one another. Oh, but she has got those golden fairies with her. Maybe I can "see" them.

**纸信圈儿**：就像笃笃骨之前说的那样……\
**Flutterpage**: Like how Ms. Willow taught me.

**笃笃骨**：“如果需要控制风，那就需要先看见风。”\
**Willow**: To control the wind, you need to learn to see it first.

**笃笃骨**：“你能看见风吗，小崽子？”\
**Willow**: Can you see the wind, lass?

**纸信圈儿**：嗯，如果有碎纸片儿，或者破布条，我能看见风在哪里。\
**Flutterpage**: Only when it's blowin' somethin' around, like dust or old paper.

**纸信圈儿**：但是我身上已经没有碎布条了，它们全都被扔在了十字街，都怪那个讨厌鬼要来抓我……不过……\
**Flutterpage**: But I ain't got nothin' like that with me now. I used all of it when Freddy tried to catch me. Is there anythin' else I can use?

一双眼睛在淡黄色的薄雾中搜寻，飘荡的乌卢鲁旌旗告诉了她风的方向。\
She scans through the pale yellow smog, the fluttering Uluru flags informing her of the wind's direction.

**纸信圈儿**：哦——我看到了！\
**Flutterpage**: Oh, I see it!

气流开始搅动，旌旗与人们的衣摆开始朝着同一个方向飘荡。\
The wind picks up, and the flags, along with the people's clothes, start to flutter in the same direction.

**病人Ⅰ**：怎么回事，起风了？我的帽子！\
**Patient I**: What with this wind, eh? Where's it coming from? Oi! My hat!

**病人Ⅱ**：有没有好心人，咳咳——快给我添一条毯子，上帝保佑你！\
**Patient II**: *cough* Please, is there any good Samaritan who can spare a blanket? Oh, God bless you!

雾气随着气流向四周逃逸，在一方小天地中，空气难得清澈了几分。\
The smog dissipates in the wind, and for a brief moment, the air is noticeably clearer in this small corner of the world.

在二十七个床位之外的地方，一只金闪闪的小精灵正被人捏住翅膀，往另一人口中送去。\
At one of the beds, a little golden fairy is being held by its wings and placed into a patient's mouth.

**纸信圈儿**：牙仙女士！\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Tooth Fairy!

**牙仙**：纸信圈儿？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Flutterpage, there you are.

医生赶紧合上病人的嘴，令他强行咽下古怪的药物，随后快步朝纸信圈儿走来。\
She swiftly closes the patient's mouth, making him swallow her bizarre medicine before walking briskly over to Flutterpage.

**牙仙**：怎么了？\
**Tooth Fairy**: What's wrong?

**纸信圈儿**：我们来研究吧！研究让天变晴的办法！\
**Flutterpage**: We've got to find a way to clear up the sky!

## LD-06 黑天鹅 / Black Swan

爬满裂痕的木门缓慢开启，室内的空气泄出，吹起些微雾气，像一道无声的叹息。\
The oak door slowly creaks open, the inside air meeting the outside and stirring up a faint mist.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

她拎着一只火盆，在花园中艰难踱步。\
She struggles her way through the garden, a brazier in her arms.

**笃笃骨**：已经快过去一周了……\
**Willow**: It's been near a week.

每一英尺的前进，右腿都会发出令人牙酸的“咯哒”声。\
With every step, her right leg gives out a painful creak.

女巫看着半开的窗户，这一周里，时有“不速之客”闯入，却都不是她想的那个。\
She looks at the half-open window. This week has seen a number of uninvited guests, but not one of them was the one she's been hoping to see.

那个对什么东西都感到好奇的，还会像麻雀一样到处乱飞的……\
That curious little thing who flutters back and forth like a sparrow.

**笃笃骨**：世道本就是这样，是我不该有所期望。\
**Willow**: Heh. This is how the world works. I should've known. I'm always too naive.

清理花园的工作通常都是这么开始的——\
She carries out her usual task of clearing out the garden.

笃笃骨先挑选了一批较为干燥的断枝与落叶，以充作引火的燃料。\
First, she gathers dry twigs and leaves to use as kindling.

然后擦燃一根火柴，扔进火盆，等待火焰战胜枝叶。\
Then, she strikes a match, throws it into the brazier, and waits for the fire to grow.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

火势渐起，她可以开始焚烧今日花园中的垃圾，其中绝大部分都来自她的好邻居们。\
As the fire intensifies, she gathers the trash from around the garden, most of which is flung into her garden by her neighbors, and adds it to the fire.

**笃笃骨**：死耗子。经典，但总能让我反胃。\
**Willow**: A dead mouse. Classic, sure to disgust me.

笃笃骨捡起腐烂的鼠尸，抛入火中，猛烈窜起的火苗几乎要点燃她的眉毛。\
Willow picks up the decaying mouse carcass and tosses it into the flames, the fire flaring up so fiercely it nearly scorches her eyebrows.

在最初的几年里，她总是从窗中向外窥望，以幽暗的眼神紧盯着从她花园前经过的人们。\
In the early years, she would often watch from the window, her dark eyes fixed on the people who passed by.

**笃笃骨**：烂苹果和臭鸡蛋，全部来自于那个老不死的臭虫，他的牙齿正在一年年地减少，总有一天他只能靠喝粥维生。\
**Willow**: Rotten apples and eggs from that boring old codger. I suppose he's down to his last teeth now. Soon enough, the only thing he'll be eating is porridge.

**笃笃骨**：他最讨厌的就是粥，很高兴知道这点。\
**Willow**: Bit of comfort in knowing he hates porridge.

时至今日，古宅门窗紧闭，人们已经许久未见屋主人的模样，只知道有一位可怕的女巫幽居于此。\
Even now, the old mansion's doors and windows remain firmly shut. The owner's face hasn't been seen for many years. All the neighbors know is that a fearsome witch lives there.

**笃笃骨**：被蒸汽烫伤手臂，在夏末节碰见鬼魂，甚至是在股票市场上倾家荡产……\
**Willow**: Hands burnt by steam. It's a curse, bumping into ghosts during the Samhain. Curse, lost everything betting on the ponies.

**笃笃骨**：所有的不幸都可以是女巫的诅咒。\
**Willow**: Each and every misfortune must surely be "Willow's curse."

笃笃骨从垃圾中拣选出大蒜，收集起来。它们本身只是调味品，可以用作种子或肥料。\
She picks out some garlic from the garbage bin. This simple seasoning can be repurposed as seeds or fertilizer.

**笃笃骨**：迷信的老东西……\
**Willow**: Superstitious fools.

无法利用的是一些木雕的奇特符号，每一种都据说有着驱魔的功效。\
The only items that cannot be utilized are the wooden carvings with bizarre symbols on them, rumored to possess the power to ward off demons.

**笃笃骨**：招摇撞骗的江湖骗子……\
**Willow**: Shysters.

“驱魔水”是最愚笨和粗陋的办法，但却也是最好应付的一类。\
Demon-Banishing Water is the most clumsy and silly item, but it's also the most manageable to deal with.

笃笃骨只需放任不管，把洒进她院子的水当成是免费的灌溉就好。\
Willow simply lets it be, treating the water poured into her garden as free irrigation.

**笃笃骨**：恶毒的、大脑发育不健全的小孩子……\
**Willow**: Brats.

盐——这是最坏的家伙。它会让一整块土地上的植物脱水而死，园丁必须尽快刨出盐化的泥土，留待日后清洗。\
Salt—this is the worst offender. It dehydrates the plants, often killing them outright. She digs up the tainted soil, ready to wash later.

**笃笃骨**：现在还有些恶心的新玩意——沾了血的破麻布。\
**Willow**: Oh. Well, now these are new, aren't they? Blood-stained rags. Wonderful.

**笃笃骨**：但愿他们把肺管子也咳出来。\
**Willow**: Sooner or later they'll all cough their lungs out.

“咯哒——”\
*click-clack*

**笃笃骨**：……！\
**Willow**: ...!

右足的僵硬已经无以复加，耳中尽是蚊虫奏出的嗡鸣。\
The stiffness in her right leg is unbearable. Mosquitoes incessantly buzz in her ears.

片刻后，笃笃骨瘫倒在一丛土豆花之中。\
Moments later, Willow's leg gives way, and she collapses into a patch of potato flowers.

**笃笃骨**：——\
**Willow**: ...

软烂的土地。\
Soft, soggy soil.

……\
...

软烂的躯体。\
A limp, decomposing body.

……\
...

**笃笃骨**：不……！\
**Willow**: No!

膝盖遭到了猛烈的锤击，好像这样就能让关节恢复正常。\
She smacks her prosthesis on the knee, as if the blow will set the joint back in its rightful place.

她刨起一把泥土，挣扎着站起……挣扎……她早就习惯了如此挣扎。\
She grabs the dirt as she fights to get to her feet, struggling. This is a struggle she's long grown used to.

**花园卡邦克鲁**：吱——！\
**Vines Carbuncle**: Squeak!

寄居花园的卡邦克鲁们被敲击声吸引，纷纷向笃笃骨靠拢。\
Lured by the sound of her strikes, the Carbuncles slowly make their way toward her.

**笃笃骨**：滚开！\
**Willow**: Away with you!

魔精们一哄而散，躲在宽大的花瓣和叶片后偷偷窥视。\
The critters scatter, ducking behind the leaves and watching her quietly from a distance.

她单手攀住一根藤蔓，却因用力过猛而失去平衡，摔倒在地。\
She clutches a vine with one hand, but it only throws her off balance, and she falls to the ground once again.

**笃笃骨**：唔——！\
**Willow**: Ugh!

**笃笃骨**：恶心……\
**Willow**: Horrible.

她明明比任何人都精通平衡之道，却又比任何人都难以适应哪怕一点残缺。\
She is more proficient in the art of balance than almost anyone, yet she also finds it more difficult than anyone to adjust to even the smallest imperfection.

**笃笃骨**：不。不需要……神秘术。\
**Willow**: No. I don't need to cast my arcane skills.

**笃笃骨**：站起来，废物——呃。\
**Willow**: Stand up, stand up! You loser, you. Ugh.

**笃笃骨**：得出去……去买点润滑脂来。\
**Willow**: I need machine lubricant. I suppose I need to buy some.

她再次爬起，这次终于掌握了诀窍。\
This time, she makes it to her feet.

“笃——笃——”\
*clack—clack*

**笃笃骨**：这种小玩意，靠我自己也能弄到手。\
**Willow**: I can do this. I will do this, all by myself.

踏步的声音变得清脆。一只手搭住栅栏门上纤细的金属花纹。\
Her steps grow clearer, more steady. She grips the delicate metalwork of the gate.

**笃笃骨**：出去……\
**Willow**: Nothing to it.

**笃笃骨**：——我做得到。\
**Willow**: Let's go.

“笃——笃——”\
*clack—clack*

如悲怆悠长的慢板，她一头扎进雾霭昏沉的伦敦。\
Her leg clacking like a slow, mournful melody, she steps into the smoggy, somber streets of London.

临时写成的告示牌拒绝了来客的访问。\
There's a makeshift sign on the door.

**笃笃骨**：“店主肺病发作，已前往牙仙女士的特别医院就诊。请在表单上留下姓名、住址与所需商品，店主病愈后将登门贩售。”\
**Willow**: "Shop closed due to illness, while the owner has gone to Ms. Tooth Fairy for treatment. Please leave your name, order, and address on the list below, and we will deliver it to your home as soon as the owner recovers."

访客捏起笔又立刻放下，始终未落一字。\
She picks up the pen, then sets it down again without writing a single word.

**笃笃骨**：牙仙……\
**Willow**: Tooth Fairy.

**笃笃骨**：也许我能去所谓的特别医院，找到莱恩父子商店的老板……算了，绝对碰不上好事，那里的医生对我来说也毫无作用。\
**Willow**: Alright, then I can find the owner if I go to this Tooth Fairy? Is she some kind of doctor, then? Not that she could treat what ails me anyway, eh.

**笃笃骨**：但是伦敦还有哪里会卖金丝绵雀唾液和羊脂蜗牛清晨时产生的黏液？\
**Willow**: What other shops might sell canary saliva and Lanolin Snail's slime?

失落的顾客裹紧了衣袍，以此抵御不断侵蚀单薄衣物的潮湿冷风。\
She wraps her cloak tighter around her body in an attempt to fend off the cold, damp air.

**笃笃骨**：……我不应该在这种事情上生疏的，这是我过分依赖其他人的报应。\
**Willow**: Heh. All this time I could have done this, if only I hadn't relied on others for so long.

**笃笃骨**：伦敦肯定不会只有这一家神秘学商店，可是……\
**Willow**: There must be another store for arcane supplies. But ...

“咯哒——咯哒——”\
*click-clack, click-clack*

**笃笃骨**：……我需要休息。\
**Willow**: I think I need a lie-down.

午夜的冷色仍然有部分残留在伦敦的晨雾中，泰晤士河畔几乎从未如此安静过。\
The cold hues of the night still linger in the morning mist. The Thames has never looked so quiet.

河对岸的土红色旗帜随风摇摆，像一列列捉摸不定的火团，灰白色的临时医疗帐篷于其间搭设。\
Across the river, earth-red flags flutter like burning balls of fire. A smattering of white emergency medical tents are scattered below them.

一张被践踏过的乌卢鲁预选赛宣传单飘至脚边，抓挠她的脚踝。\
A trampled Uluru Qualifiers flyer floats down to her feet, brushing against her ankle.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

**笃笃骨**：幼稚的运动会狂热，不知从何而来的黑雾，要命的肺结核……这些都与我无关，我只是出来寻找能让我恢复灵活的润滑脂。\
**Willow**: Sports fanatics, black fog, strange tuberculosis ... All these things have nothing to do with me. All I need are my ingredients. Nothing more.

**笃笃骨**：我可以找到一个信守承诺的商家，让他每周在花园门口给我留下商品。\
**Willow**: I ought to just order what I need as a home delivery, ask them to leave the package at the entrance of the garden once a week.

**笃笃骨**：我可以把奖牌都卖了，换来的英镑足够我花到变成一个满脸沟壑的老妪——一个真正的鬼婆，朝所有人吐口水。\
**Willow**: As for the fees, I'll just have to sell all me old medals. That'll be enough to support me until I become a proper hag, then I can never leave my house till the day I die.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

**笃笃骨**：嗤——\
**Willow**: Heh.

**笃笃骨**：……嗯？\
**Willow**: Hmm?

有什么黑糊糊的东西划开了水面。\
There's something dark rising up from the water.

**笃笃骨**：可能是一团纠缠的缆绳，或者泡烂的旧靴子。\
**Willow**: It's nothing special. A bit of old rope, or an old boot.

为什么不能是一只天鹅？比如……真正的天鹅？\
Why can't it be a swan?

**笃笃骨**：我从未见过黑色的天鹅。\
**Willow**: A black swan here, really?

看看你，成天闷在家里，错过了多少东西。你差点连这只绝无仅有的黑色天鹅也错过了。\
That's why you ought to go out more often. Else you'll miss these precious moments—a chance to see something special like a black swan.

瞧，有些动物生下来就有漆黑亮丽的羽毛，当你把它们置于晴朗的日光下，就会发现这种黑色有多么璀璨夺目。\
Look at it. Some creatures are born with these smooth, pitch-black feathers. But it's only under the sunlight that you can see their iridescent shine.

所有不生黑羽的动物都会钦羡不已，即便是白色的天鹅也会自愧不如，因为它们永远不能如此与众不同。\
That's when all the other animals can only look on and feel themselves inferior. They can never stand out from the crowd in the same way.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

你的沉默通常都是认可，一如你的咒骂都是自责。来吧，夏洛特，现在你能欣赏它了——\
Your silence is an answer. I know it, just as I know every time you lash out and curse, you're cursing your own failure. Walk closer, Charlotte. Why don't we take a better look at it?

弯曲的颈项，壮丽的羽翼，拨开水面的粼粼水声……黑色的羽毛正是造就它完美的最后一块拼图。\
Look at its gracefully long neck, those magnificent wings, and how it glides across the water. All swans are beautiful, but only the black feathers make it truly stand out.

它的每一个动作都在唤起你的回忆，不是吗？因为你记得起舞时的每一寸细节，记得那种“天鹅般的心境”。\
It brings back some memories, don't it? The feeling of "being one with the swans" and the flow of each step of our dance.

你知道自己有多么趋近于完美——你随时可以拨开水面，向没有尘土的天空中飞去。\
We were so close to perfection. All we needed was for you to spread your wings and fly.

飞去巴黎、开罗、伊斯坦布尔……最后是红土地上的乌卢鲁之岩。\
Fly to Paris, Cairo, Istanbul ... and eventually to the Uluru Rock.

**笃笃骨**：它向我游来……\
**Willow**: Then it comes to me.

**笃笃骨**：我可以捧起它，拥之入怀。\
**Willow**: And I can hold it in my arms, lift it above my head.

**笃笃骨**：一枚完美无缺的、闪耀的金牌。\
**Willow**: This perfect, shining golden medal.

**笃笃骨**：在乌卢鲁之岩上……\
**Willow**: Standing on Uluru Rock.

**笃笃骨**：——！\
**Willow**: ...!

**？？？**：笃笃骨——你怎么在这儿？\
**???**: Ms. Willow! But what you doin' out here?

**？？？**：黑色的风朝你吹来了，快躲开！\
**???**: You got to move! The black fog is comin' straight for you!

**笃笃骨**：别管那些声音了，快看——天鹅。\
**Willow**: Ignore the noise. Eyes on the swan.

啧啧啧……\
Tsk-tsk-tsk.

原来她披着一身俗气的白羽毛，只是身上落满了煤渣。\
It's only a tacky white swan, covered in soot.

它一定是被货船上的帮工照着脑袋浇下了一筐锅炉里的废料，真是滑稽透顶！\
How ridiculous it looks now! Wearing that false disguise, the poor thing. It must have been covered accidentally.

**？？？**：你在看那只天鹅吗？——她……已经死了。\
**???**: Ms. Willow, why you lookin' at that swan? It's ... dead.

我说呢——原来它早就已经死了。\
Of course, it's dead and gone.

这才对，不落得个这样的结局才是奇怪了，有哪只天鹅愿意和浑身煤渣的丑东西呆在一起？\
That's right. What kind of swan would want to be with something so ugly and stained?

离群索居，孤独终老……得了，得了，你还在期待什么呢？\
Of course, it's ended up alone, died alone. What else were you expecting?

你不会真的信了那些鬼话吧？\
