You didn't really believe that "spread your wings and fly" bollocks, did you?

**？？？**：你真的听见我说话了吗，笃笃骨？\
**???**: Hello, can you hear me, Ms. Willow?

感谢那一阵无名的黑风吧，它掀开了迷雾，让你看见了最终的真相——\
You ought to thank the black fog for lifting your illusion. Now you can see it rightly.

你并不是一只生下来就卓尔不群的黑天鹅，你只是——\
You're not some special black swan that was born to greatness. You're nothing but—

**？？？**：笃笃骨？你——\
**???**: Ms. Willow? You ...

**？？？**：你的腿……这是你的腿？！\
**???**: What's wrong with your leg?

——一个可笑的残废。\
But a cripple.

**？？？**：别靠过去，纸信圈儿！\
**???**: Come back, Flutterpage!

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

笃笃骨低下头，察觉到纸信圈儿早已靠到脚边。牙仙站在几步外呼唤，但她并没有退却的意思。\
Willow lowers her head to see that Flutterpage is standing at her feet. Tooth Fairy stands a few steps away, calling out to her.

一根细小的手指触碰到用来弥补残疾的假腿，那是她为了自尊而隐藏了十年的秘密。\
Flutterpage gently touches her prosthetic leg, revealing the secret she has been too proud to admit for the last ten years.

**纸信圈儿**：……你……为什么你从来没有和我说过……\
**Flutterpage**: Why? Why didn't you tell me about your ...

**牙仙**：你比我所想象的要更加坚强，笃笃骨小姐——如果你允许我用这个称呼的话。\
**Tooth Fairy**: You're much stronger than I thought, Ms. Willow, if you allow me to address you as such.

**笃笃骨**：别烦我，让我回家……\
**Willow**: Leave me be. I'm going home.

**纸信圈儿**：我……我送你回去，你可以扶着我，或者我扶着你。\
**Flutterpage**: I'll walk you home. I got you.

**纸信圈儿**：虽然牙仙女士正在带我去追黑色的雾——但、但我还是先送你回家吧——\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Tooth Fairy and I was just chasin' after the black fog, but, but I can walk you home fir—

**笃笃骨**：我要回去。\
**Willow**: I just want to go home.

笃笃骨使出浑身解数，也无法做到一个体面的转身。僵硬的右腿又在拖累她的行动。\
Willow uses all her might to turn, but still can't do it with any grace. Her stiff right leg continues to impede her.

**纸信圈儿**：我和你一起回去。\
**Flutterpage**: I'll go with you.

孩子伸出手，笨拙地想要通过拽住衣角来挽留离去的朋友。\
She stretches out her hand and pulls at Willow's clothes in a clumsy attempt to stop her friend from leaving.

**牙仙**：纸信圈儿——\
**Tooth Fairy**: Flutterpage.

女孩的手被甩开了。\
Willow swats her hand away.

**纸信圈儿**：——？\
**Flutterpage**: Hmm?

**笃笃骨**：别再跟着我了！\
**Willow**: Stop following me!

**纸信圈儿**：笃笃骨——\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Willow!

**笃笃骨**：我要回家！\
**Willow**: I just want to go home.

**纸信圈儿**：不是——我、我——\
**Flutterpage**: I ... I ...

纸信圈儿呆立在原地，眼眶蓦然红肿，牙仙上前将她揽入怀中。\
Flutterpage remains in place, her eyes suddenly filled with tears. Tooth Fairy steps forward and pulls her into a hug.

**纸信圈儿**：呜哇——\
**Flutterpage**: *crying*

**笃笃骨**：……别跟上来。\
**Willow**: I don't want you to follow me.

**牙仙**：……\
**Tooth Fairy**: ...

她们目送女巫颤颤巍巍地朝十字街的旧宅归去，每一步都踩碎着些许自尊。\
They look on as Willow shakily walks into the smog, each step grinding away a little more of her dignity.

## LD-07 早午餐 / Brunch

**卡洛琳**：……自由祭祀是最受瞩目的乌卢鲁项目之一，因为它不仅是奇诡瑰丽的表演，还是数千名观众与舞者的情绪共鸣。\
**Caroline Bartley**: The Floor Ritual is one of the most popular events of the Uluru Games. It has a bewitching style that generates a resonance between the dancer and audience.

**卡洛琳**：夏洛特……她就像是为此而生的天才，并且奇遇般地与那位浑身插满乌鸦羽毛、终日研读古代凯尔特部落符文的教练结识。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Charlotte was a genius. She was born for it. And God has sent her a coach covered in dark feathers and skilled in ancient Celtic runes.

**卡洛琳**：乌鸦教练将最原始的女巫之舞传授给夏洛特，从而彻底点燃了她内在的火焰——直到十年前的悲剧带走了她的右腿。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Coach Raven taught her the primal witch dance that ignited a fire within her. At least, until that tragedy 10 years ago which took her leg.

**卡洛琳**：夏洛特得到了一袋花种作为练习的奖励，传说这些种子来自于格拉斯顿伯里森林中隐居的德鲁伊。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Coach Raven had given her a pocket of flower seeds as a reward for all her diligent practicing. It's said they were from the druids in the forests of Glastonbury.

**卡洛琳**：这片花园就是如此诞生的，奇异植物与花园的主人终日共享同一种呼吸。\
**Caroline Bartley**: I guess she planted them around her house and got this garden. Now all these bizarre plants share the same strange air with their owner.

巨大多脉的叶片垂落于泥土中，牙仙记得第一次来到这座花园时，生命并未散发这样委顿的气息。\
The plants in the mansion's garden are all drooping toward the ground. There is a new sense of weariness that wasn't present during Tooth Fairy's last visit.

门边的女人轻轻摇头，而纸信圈儿则直接蹲在了骇人的植物之下，将头伸进了茂密的植物丛中，找寻着奇形怪状的虫子的痕迹。\
The woman by the door gently shakes her head as Flutterpage crawls around on her knees, searching for bugs among the foliage.

**卡洛琳**：谢谢你们再次邀请我过来……关于夏洛特，我也只能说这么多了。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Thank you again for having me over. That's all I have to say about Charlotte.

听到了总结性的话语，纸信圈儿站了起来。\
Flutterpage's head pops out from between the plants.

**纸信圈儿**：你说的那些地方，那片森林，那个德鲁伊，我也能去吗？\
**Flutterpage**: What's a druid? Is it a place? Do they have canaries and snails there?

**卡洛琳**：德鲁伊不是地名，而是一种身份。\
**Caroline Bartley**: A druid isn't a place. It's a title, an identity.

**纸信圈儿**：身份……就像我是纸信圈儿一样？\
**Flutterpage**: Identity. Oh, like a name, just like Flutterpage, right?

孩子又陷入了自己的思索中。\
She quickly falls back into her own musings.

**牙仙**：感谢你的坦诚与合作，卡洛琳女士，很抱歉占用了你的练习时间。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Thank you for your cooperation, Ms. Bartley. I'm sorry to be taking you away from your practice.

**卡洛琳**：嗯。我本来也不太喜欢和政府官员打交道。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Yes, you should be. I don't much enjoy being bothered by stuffed-up bureaucrats.

成就斐然的自由祭祀运动员向来直言不讳。\
The accomplished Floor Ritualist has never been one to hold back her words.

**卡洛琳**：只是……\
**Caroline Bartley**: But if you ask me—

卡洛琳再次瞥向维多利亚古宅紧闭的窄窗。\
Caroline glances once more at the narrow window of the old Victorian house. It's tightly shut.

**卡洛琳**：如果官方还在怀疑夏洛特就是召唤黑雾的女巫，那我现在就告诉你——她不是。\
**Caroline Bartley**: I will tell you that it isn't Charlotte that's summoning the black fog.

**卡洛琳**：我以我作为乌卢鲁运动员的所有荣誉向你保证。\
**Caroline Bartley**: I stand by that. I swear it on all my honor as an Uluru competitor.

**卡洛琳**：她和我一样，不是传统意义上的女巫。我们练习巫术是为了拿奖牌，而不是为了召唤魔鬼或者下毒诅咒。\
**Caroline Bartley**: We're witches, but not in the traditional sense. We practice witchcraft to win medals instead of summoning devils.

**牙仙**：这一点应该是足以取信的。如此一来，有关“雾中鬼婆”的调查事实上已经结束了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: We trust you at your word. It seems like that concludes our investigation into this Fog Hag. Thanks again, Ms. Bartley.

**卡洛琳**：……牙仙女士，如果你觉得应该为我的配合提供报酬，那么，请帮我个忙。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Ms. Tooth Fairy, if you do want to thank me, mind doing me a favor?

牙仙点头，向来直率的女人却还在酝酿措辞。\
Tooth Fairy nods, but Caroline seems to have an unusual hesitation as she deliberates over her choice of words.

最终，她放弃了。\
In the end, she yields.

**卡洛琳**：总之……做点什么，牙仙女士，她不能再这么邋遢下去。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Please do something, anything, to bring her out of this hole she's dug for herself.

**卡洛琳**：你打算做什么都行，砸烂她的门也好，把她拖出来也好，还是要把这栋房子直接掀翻，都随你的便。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Whatever you do, break down her door, drag her out by her hair, even blow up that old mansion.

**卡洛琳**：但就是别让她再躲在这破宅子里了。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Just don't let her hide in her stupid house.

**卡洛琳**：你进去吧，我能感觉到，花园现在没有力量阻拦任何人。\
**Caroline Bartley**: She'll let you inside now. There's no longer any power preventing you. I can sense it.

**牙仙**：……你很了解这片花园。在你上一次造访时，她有没有和你见面？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Hmm. You know this place well. Have you visited her here before?

卡洛琳咬着下唇，强忍着把抵到齿尖的话吞回去。\
Caroline bites her lip, holding back the words on the tip of her tongue.

她头也不回地离开了。\
Then, she walks away.

**纸信圈儿**：……我觉得卡洛琳很想和我们一起进去。\
**Flutterpage**: I think Ms. Bartley wants to come in with us.

**牙仙**：可我们也拦不住她。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Maybe so, but she's made her choice. She doesn't want to join us inside.

牙仙摇晃着手中的罐子——不是通常装满“牙仙”的那只，而是装满羊脂蜗牛的类似品。\
Tooth Fairy shakes the jar in her hand, not containing her usual toothfairies but filled with a collection of lanolin snails.

**牙仙**：来吧，我们还有事情要做。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Let's go, Flutterpage. We still have work to do.

**纸信圈儿**：好吧。\
**Flutterpage**: Whatever you say, Ms. Witch Doctor.

医生与女孩谨慎地踏入花园，疏松多孔的泥土在她足底被压实，没有什么再来阻拦她的道路。\
The two of them step cautiously into the garden, the soil compacting under their feet. There is nothing left to obstruct their path.

她们顺从地绕过一些看起来不好招惹的植物，沿着蜿蜒曲折的道路来到镶嵌铁钉的橡木门前。\
They step around a few threatening-looking plants as they take the winding road to the creaky oak door.

牙仙想要敲门，却没有料到沉重的大门轻轻一推就向后退去。\
Tooth Fairy goes to knock, but the door swings open the moment her knuckle hits its surface.

**牙仙**：门没有上锁，进来吧。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Ah! The door isn't locked. Let's get inside.

女巫坐在餐桌后，就着一盘茄汁焗豆吃苏格兰炸鸡蛋。\
Willow sits at the table prepared for one, surrounded by an exorbitant amount of half-finished food.

只服务于一位食客的餐桌上，还能见到吃剩的烤苹果派、油炸鳕鱼和薯条的影子。\
Aside from the full English she's currently tucking into, there's a scotch egg, a half-eaten cod and chips, and a steaming apple crumble.

**牙仙**：打扰了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Sorry to interrupt.

房屋主人将最基本的礼仪都抛至九霄云外，根本不在乎提醒客人入座，自顾自地切下又一块烤香肠。\
Willow casts aside basic manners, neglecting to invite her guests to sit, and cuts herself another piece of sausage.

**笃笃骨**：唔咕——\
**Willow**: *swallow*

**牙仙**：突然吃下太多油腻和高含糖量的食物会让你得胃病的，夏洛特女士。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Diets high in sugar and fatty oils may well lead to stomach illness, Ms. O'Hagan.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

随即选择继续食用丰盛到近乎异常的早午餐。\
She continues to eat her lavish brunch.

**牙仙**：我选择用“牙仙”来代替“坎贝尔”，并且早已习惯，但你是否接受这个其他人附加于你的称呼？\
**Tooth Fairy**: I choose the name, Tooth Fairy, instead of my real name, Campbell. But did you choose to let people call you Willow?

**牙仙**：还是，你更习惯夏洛特·奥黑根这个名字？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Or, do you prefer the name Charlotte O'Hagan?

**牙仙**：一个……优秀的乌卢鲁运动员的名字。\
**Tooth Fairy**: That is the name of ... an excellent Uluru Floor Ritualist.

餐具碰撞的声音再次中断，这次等了很长时间都没有再度响起。\
The crash of silverware interrupts her once more.

她仰起头，双手扫过桌面。\
Then, Willow sweeps her arm across the table.

镀银的餐盘丁零当啷地滚向地面，敲响一段毫无美感的聒噪音乐。\
The silver dishes clatter loudly as they fly to the floor.

**笃笃骨**：你的眼神最好没出问题，医生。我的腿断了，是个残疾人。\
**Willow**: Tooth Fairy, some kind of doctor, right? I think your prescription is a little fuzzy. I'm no athlete. I've only got one leg.

**笃笃骨**：夏洛特就是夏洛特，笃笃骨就是笃笃骨。\
**Willow**: This Charlotte has nothing to do with Willow.

**笃笃骨**：我和乌卢鲁没有关系。\
**Willow**: Just like I've nothing to do with the Uluru Games.

**牙仙**：据我所知，乌卢鲁运动会并没有拒绝残疾人参赛的传统。\
**Tooth Fairy**: So far as I know, the Uluru Games do not exclude people with disabilities from full participation.

**笃笃骨**：如果你喜欢扮演马戏团里的小丑，那就去吧，但我没有这种癖好。\
**Willow**: To be sure, but only if you enjoy parading yourself around for embarrassment. I think I'll pass, thanks.

**牙仙**：没有人会在赛场上丢脸，尤其是愿意挑战自我的人，这与乌卢鲁的精神不谋而合。\
**Tooth Fairy**: No one should feel embarrassed by competing, least of all the competitors challenging themselves. That is the point of the Uluru spirit.

女巫挣扎，站起，愤恨地用假肢锤击着地面，仿佛要借此将支撑她的右腿砸个粉碎。\
Willow rises with great effort, furiously stamping the floor with her prosthesis in the process.

**笃笃骨**：我不记得什么时候请了一个烦人的家庭教师。\
**Willow**: Excuse me? I don't remember having asked you for a running commentary.

**牙仙**：你比我更加年长，想必先我一步知晓了生活的答案。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I'm sure you already know the answer in your heart. You have wisdom and experience.

**笃笃骨**：出去，我从没有邀请过你！\
**Willow**: Who even invited you here?! It's time you leave.

**牙仙**：我是为纸信圈儿来的。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I'm here representing our mutual friend, Flutterpage.

听见纸信圈儿的名字，笃笃骨愣了愣神，向后退了一步。\
At the mention of this name, Willow pauses and takes a step back.

**笃笃骨**：你想说什么？\
**Willow**: What for?

**牙仙**：我知道这里通常不欢迎除了纸信圈儿之外的客人，但我正是代替那孩子来向你道歉的。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I understand that usually the only one welcome inside is Flutterpage, but I'm here to apologize on her behalf.

**笃笃骨**：……道歉？\
**Willow**: Apologize?

她将一小罐蜗牛置于桌面。\
She places a small jar of snails on the table.

**笃笃骨**：这是？\
**Willow**: What's this?

**牙仙**：一份表示歉意的礼物，她已经准备多时了——天还没亮的时候，她就从我的看护下逃走了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: An apology gift. She ran off a little before sunrise to collect these for you.

**牙仙**：她一直在帮你收集这些神秘学生物，好让你能制作用于义肢的润滑脂，对吗？\
**Tooth Fairy**: She collects these arcane creatures you use to make the lubricant for your prosthesis, right?

**牙仙**：可她害怕你再次生她的气，所以我决定先替她把礼物交给它应该归属的主人。\
**Tooth Fairy**: But she's afraid that you'll get angry at her again, so she asked me to give it to you.

**笃笃骨**：不要把我说得像一个恶棍。\
**Willow**: Oh, I see. Now I'm the hateful, angry, wicked witch.

**牙仙**：你没做错什么，我也知道，你不是人们口中的那一类女巫。\
**Tooth Fairy**: No, you're not. The things that these people say about you, they aren't true.

**牙仙**：就像我说的，要道歉的是纸信圈儿，错在她“不该伤了你的心”——这是原话。\
**Tooth Fairy**: As I mentioned, Flutterpage wanted to apologize, because, quote, she "didn't want to break your heart."

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

**牙仙**：卡洛琳小姐在她身边说了不少故事，在此之前，纸信圈儿从来不知道你是一位如此优秀又坚强的乌卢鲁运动员。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Ms. Bartley has told her many things about you. She never knew you're such an outstanding competitor.

**笃笃骨**：卡洛琳——\
**Willow**: Caroline?

装满蜗牛的罐子被轻轻推到距离笃笃骨更近的地方。\
Tooth Fairy slowly pushes the jar of snails closer to her.

**牙仙**：你能接受这份礼物吗？\
**Tooth Fairy**: So, will you accept her gift?

笃笃骨伸出手，指腹轻轻搭在罐体上。她没有推开罐子，也没有拿走。\
Willow delicately places her fingertips on the jar, neither pushing it away nor taking it.

**笃笃骨**：多管闲事。\
**Willow**: Ugh, nosy little brat.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

**笃笃骨**：纸信圈儿在哪里？你的临时医院？\
**Willow**: Where is she now? In the temporary hospital?

**牙仙**：你想去找她吗？\
**Tooth Fairy**: You want to see her?

女巫的五官仿佛绞成一股绳。\
The witch's features twist like a knot.

**笃笃骨**：该死的，别在这装腔作势！\
**Willow**: Don't push me!

笃笃骨将蜗牛罐子朝自己的方向拉近。\
She pulls the snail jar closer to her.

**笃笃骨**：——是我有错！我不该那么对一个孩子说话！\
**Willow**: Alright, it's my own fault! I shouldn't have treated her that way!

**笃笃骨**：你在等的就是这个，对吧？\
**Willow**: That what you wanted to hear, is it?

**笃笃骨**：现在你满意了，快带我去见她！\
**Willow**: Fine, then. You'll have what you want. Just take me to her!

**牙仙**：她和我一起来的，已经在门口等候很久了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: She's waiting by the door.

**笃笃骨**：……一起？\
**Willow**: What?

一颗小脑袋从门框边缘悄悄探出来。她瞪大了眼睛，好确认屋内的黑暗中不再有危险。\
Flutterpage cautiously peeks out from the edge of the doorframe, her wide eyes scanning the room for any sign of danger.

**纸信圈儿**：笃笃骨？\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Willow?

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

事已至此，退无可退。\
At this point, there is no turning back.

**笃笃骨**：进来！\
**Willow**: Fine! Come on in then.

**纸信圈儿**：呜呜……\
**Flutterpage**: *sob*

孩子的委屈总是不知道从何而来，现在她又想哭了。\
Unable to deal with her emotions, tears well up in Flutterpage's eyes once again.

**笃笃骨**：别哭——\
**Willow**: Stop your crying.

**笃笃骨**：听好了，我……\
**Willow**: Listen, I—

**笃笃骨**：就是说……\
**Willow**: Urgh, I ...

**笃笃骨**：……我不该用那种态度对你，不管是上一次，还是上上一次。\
**Willow**: I shouldn't have treated you so wickedly the last time, and the time before that.

牙仙轻悄悄地点头。\
Tooth Fairy gives a silent nod.

**笃笃骨**：好了，你不能哭了，别在我家——\
**Willow**: Now would you stop that crying? At least not here in my—

**纸信圈儿**：呵——呵嗯——\
**Flutterpage**: *crying*

她义无反顾地朝餐桌飞奔而来。\
Without a moment's hesitation, Flutterpage charges toward her.

笃笃骨的双手打开又合上，像一只因受到惊吓而立起前肢的蜘蛛。\
Willow's hands open and close like a spider raising its front legs in fear.

她不知道自己能否接得住这一只乱糟糟的破布团。\
She's not sure whether she can catch this chaotic bundle of rags.

**笃笃骨**：喂！\
**Willow**: Oi!

“砰——”\
*bang*

她接住了，但人也向后倒去。\
She manages to catch her, only to be knocked back to the floor.

**笃笃骨**：——\
**Willow**: ...

**纸信圈儿**：对……对不起……是我错了——\
**Flutterpage**: I'm sorry ... I-I'm really very sorry ...

**笃笃骨**：啧……\
**Willow**: Tsk ...

**纸信圈儿**：我以后不会在你家捣乱了，你允许我什么时候来，我就什么时候来……\
**Flutterpage**: I swear I won't break into your house no more. I'll only come in when you let me.

**纸信圈儿**：你让我说什么，我就说什么，你不让我说什么我就什么都不会说……\
**Flutterpage**: I'll do anythin' you ask, say anythin' you need me to say, Miss.

她下意识地想要去看牙仙的表情，却发现后者正把全部的注意力放在墙上的乌卢鲁自由祭祀油画上。\
She unconsciously looks to Tooth Fairy, only to see that her full attention is directed at the Uluru Floor Ritual painting on the wall.

隔着不知多少层旧衣服，女巫轻轻拍了拍纸信圈儿的后脖颈。\
Willow gently taps the back of Flutterpage's neck through several layers of old clothing.

**纸信圈儿**：我——我以后还能到你的花园来，还能到你家来吗？\
**Flutterpage**: So, could I still come around again sometime?

女巫捂住女孩的嘴，打断了她的哭诉。\
Willow presses her hand to the girl's mouth, stifling her sobs.

**纸信圈儿**：唔——\
**Flutterpage**: Wumm.

**笃笃骨**：再哭下去我就要受不了了。\
**Willow**: Stop your crying first, lass.

**纸信圈儿**：好，我……我不哭了。\
**Flutterpage**: Okay! I'll stop cryin'.

女巫轻轻一推，纸信圈儿就像一只被风吹起的布袋子那般飘了起来。\
With a soft push, Flutterpage drifts into the air like a sheet caught in the wind.

可正当她庆幸失去了重压时，一个尴尬的问题向她袭来——她起不来了。\
Even with the removal of Flutterpage's weight, Willow is left on the floor, unable to get up.

**纸信圈儿**：我来……帮你？\
**Flutterpage**: Let ... Can I help you?

纸信圈儿挪到她的右手边，平齐地伸出两只手。\
Flutterpage moves closer, reaching out both hands in line with Willow's.

**笃笃骨**：……呵。\
**Willow**: Heh.

笃笃骨握住援手，完成了一次完美的站立，忽然吹来的风帮助她保持了平衡。\
She takes the offered hands and rises steadily, the sudden gust of wind helping her find her balance.

**笃笃骨**：够了，闹到这种程度已经够我受了。\
**Willow**: Enough, enough. I've had too much of this for one day.

**笃笃骨**：没有什么其他事的话，我恳请二位离开吧。\
**Willow**: Would you mind if I politely asked you to leave?

**笃笃骨**：你们还得去追查那道神秘的雾气，不是吗？\
**Willow**: You do have a black fog to chase after all, don't you?

**笃笃骨**：当然，我必须要说，这和我没有半点关系。\
**Willow**: Just so you know, it truly has nothing to do with me.

**纸信圈儿**：夏洛特……\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. O'Hagan ...

**笃笃骨**：就叫我笃笃骨吧，你还有什么想说的？\
**Willow**: Call me Willow, child. What else do you want to say?

**纸信圈儿**：这次就让那些食物好好地呆在你的肚子里吧，偶尔多吃一点没关系的。\
**Flutterpage**: Would you let the food stay in your tummy for a bit longer? Eat a little more. I don't want you to be so skinny.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

笃笃骨强行解开了纸信圈儿环在自己腰肢上的手臂，将不舍的女孩推得离自己远些。\
Willow pries Flutterpage's arm from around her waist, gently pushing her back.

**笃笃骨**：知道了，快走吧。\
**Willow**: Alright. Now leave me be, please.

牙仙领着纸信圈儿退出了房间，古宅里又只剩了孤寂，敦实厚重的钟咔嚓咔嚓地走着，像是在拧什么东西的发条。\
Tooth Fairy takes Flutterpage's hand, and, as they leave the room, the old house sinks back into silence. There is no sound save for the heavy ticking of the grandfather clock.

**笃笃骨**：让她看到过我太多的不堪了。\
**Willow**: She's seen too much of this embarrassing side of me.

## LD-08 小巷落难记 / Raining Fish

**无线电广播**：……以至于我昨晚睡觉梦见了棉花糖，怎么都嚼不烂！第二天，我妻子问我，为什么要吃掉她用来塞鼻子的棉花。\
**Radio Broadcast**: So, I dreamt of eating a marshmallow last night, but it tasted like rubber! And the next day, my wife asked me why I ate the cotton she had in her nose.

**无线电广播**：我说空气太差了，我甚至要堵住我的嗓子眼，我的妻子却高兴坏了。\
**Radio Broadcast**: I said it's because the air was so dirty that I wanted to block up my throat. And she laughed.

**无线电广播**：……她说这样一来，那些运动员得分的时候你就喊不出来了。\
**Radio Broadcast**: Of course, she says it might be better now that I can't shout and holler whenever someone scores.

一阵杂音响过，收音机的主人似乎换了个台。\
A burst of static fills the air as the radio's owner changes the station.

**无线电广播**：这就是运动员的最高水平！没有比这更高的天花板了，它就是极限，超越人体的极限，超越人类认知的极限，超越一切的极限！\
**Radio Broadcast**: These are the highest level of professional arcanists! Their abilities lie far beyond the limits of our bodies, our perception, and everything else!

**宽檐帽**：你在干什么，伙计？\
**Brimley**: Arthur, mate, do you know what you're doing?

**福葛先生**：非常优秀的嗓门，你大可以喊得再大声一点，告诉所有人你能在垃圾堆里捡到一个活着的国家公职人员以及他会说话的帽子。\
**Mr. Fog**: Go on then, be a little louder. May as well let everyone know a trusted servant of His Majesty's Government and his talking hat are hiding out in a pile of litter!

**宽檐帽**：你是在说我吗？伙计！我敢打包票，再大的嗓门也比不过最近这条街上的热情，没人会发现你躲在这儿，就像没人会发现一颗土豆掉进了土豆堆。\
**Brimley**: Oh, that's what you're worrying about? I guarantee you no person in their right mind will think that a brilliant mind such as yourself would decide to hide in a rubbish pile pretending to be a potato!

**福葛先生**：啊——好，你最近越来越会说笑话了。\
**Mr. Fog**: Ha-ha, since when did you become a comedian?

**宽檐帽**：拜您所赐，希望我带着您的伟大幽默回到故土时，人们能为这顶帽子授予一个“好笑公爵”的称号。\
**Brimley**: I learned from the "best," mate. Once I'm back in Oz, I hope to be awarded the title of "Duke of Syd-knee-slapper."

**宽檐帽**：——噢，我差点忘了，咱们那儿有的是红土、马背以及自由的游骑，公爵的名号还是得往后稍稍。\
**Brimley**: Not that anyone gives a toss about titles of nobility back home. We've got more important things to worry about in the red lands down under.

**福葛先生**：没事，至少在这儿你已经是一个优秀的“人上人”绅士了，只要你肯让人把你戴在头上。\
**Mr. Fog**: You know, Brimley, old chap, you don't have to be a duke to be above people. All you need is someone tall enough to wear you on his head.

**宽檐帽**：那是一万个不行！打着煤油灯都找不到的可能性！任何一个有意识的生物都不会同意将自己最空洞脆弱的地方示人！\
**Brimley**: Bloody oath, mate! Like I'd let anyone pop me on their head. I'm an intelligent being, not a bloody accessory.

**福葛先生**：——嘘！\
**Mr. Fog**: Shh!

垃圾堆里探出一个小小的望远镜。\
A small monocular peeks out from among the garbage.

**福葛先生**：看看他，本家的大儿子，刚从蒂尔伯里码头回来的水手，看到他手上的麻绳了吗，那可是世界上最稳固的一种。\
**Mr. Fog**: Look at that sailor over there. See the ropes in his hand? That right there is presently the most valuable material in all of London to me.

**宽檐帽**：是的，我看到了。\
**Brimley**: Right, a bit of rope, and what about it, mate?

**福葛先生**：它对我的发明研究会有奇用，而我们只需要等待他走过来，把麻绳扔进垃圾堆，我们就能得到它。\
**Mr. Fog**: It's essential that I have it for my invention. We'll just wait for him to throw the ropes into the pile here, and then we'll be off, just as simple as that.

**福葛先生**：……一步、两步、三步……好——！他正在向我们这堆垃圾走来！\
**Mr. Fog**: Come closer, closer. Ready now! He's nearly here!

**福葛先生**：——这麻绳对他已经没用了，没错，好孩子，丢到垃圾堆里，丢到这儿来……\
**Mr. Fog**: It's no longer useful to you, son. Just throw it down.

一盆新鲜的鱼肉糜迎头倒下。\
A bowl of freshly extracted fish guts is poured over him.

**福葛先生**：呸！呸——咳咳，咳咳咳咳咳！\
**Mr. Fog**: BAAAH! *coughs*

**宽檐帽**：咳咳……福、福葛伙计……虽然我喜欢同你一起冒险，但我不愿承担意识觉醒后的感官刺激……咳咳咳。\
**Brimley**: *coughs* Mate, there's a lot of good that's come of being Awakened. I treasure all the adventures we've shared. But I'll tell you right now, I wouldn't have Awakened if I knew I'd end up in a rubbish bin covered in fish guts.

**福葛先生**：一次小小的失误，放宽心，只是一次小小的判断失误。\
**Mr. Fog**: Just a little mistake. Just a LITTLE mistake.

**宽檐帽**：您究竟想做什么？福葛伙计。\
**Brimley**: What are all these for exactly?

福葛先生示意宽檐帽靠近自己，“哗”，他骄傲地打开自己收集了三天的大麻袋。\
Mr. Fog gestures for Brimley to come closer, then, with a proud "whoosh," opens the large sack he's been filling over the last three days.

**福葛先生**：瞧，一个大喇叭、一个耐高温加热的喷壶、巴拉奈婆婆家的圆玻璃鱼缸，还有……\
**Mr. Fog**: These are my collections so far: a klaxon, a watering can, a fishbowl, and ...

**宽檐帽**：还有……一个夜壶？\
**Brimley**: A chamber pot?

宽檐帽露出鄙夷的神情，即使他并没有五官，但福葛先生依然能感知到他现在鄙夷至极。\
Despite his lack of facial features, Mr. Fog can sense Brimley's disdain.

**宽檐帽**：我怎么也想象不到，一个体面的雾行者如今会在这里收拾破烂，还引以为豪！\
**Brimley**: You've gone full bonkers, mate! You're the Fogwalker! Aren't you ashamed of hiding in rubbish, stealing old junk?

**福葛先生**：这些不是破烂，嘿，听着——\
**Mr. Fog**: It's not junk, old chap. Every piece here will be invaluable to our work.

福葛先生的表情突然严肃起来，他看向宽檐帽。\
Mr. Fog's face hardens as he turns his gaze toward Brimley.

**福葛先生**：这些不是破烂，这些都是研究发明的一环。\
**Mr. Fog**: Each one is a necessary component for my invention.

**宽檐帽**：研究发明？为了什么？\
**Brimley**: Your invention?

**福葛先生**：……为了……嘿！水手先生！别跑，您别走了！\
**Mr. Fog**: For ... Ahoy, sailor. You over there! Please wait!

福葛先生的注意力很明显被刚才的水手继续吸引。\
Mr. Fog's attention is clearly still fixed on the sailor.

**福葛先生**：别走，至少把您手里的麻绳留下！\
**Mr. Fog**: Would you mind terribly leaving us those old ropes you've got there!

**宽檐帽**：我的老天爷……他会把自己搞到精神病院去的。\
**Brimley**: Good lord, he's bound for the sanitarium at this rate.

**巡逻警察Ⅰ**：大家让一让，别挤，每个人都有投票权，您最期待的运动员不会因为您的票来慢了而马失前蹄！\
**Police Constable I**: Move along, move along! No pushing! Everyone will have their chance to vote for their favorite competitor!

**威尔**：……瞧您，您已经把我挤到队伍外面了，我又得重新排队，您可真会指挥治安。\
**Will**: Oi, sweeny! You only pushed me out of the queue. Good bloody job, mate.

**街坊Ⅰ**：——我要投票给零零七号！零零七号穆尔森！\
**Neighbor I**: I'm voting for number 007! Mulson!

**街坊Ⅱ**：穆尔森？新秀选手，没有经验！不如我零零五号种子选手卡洛琳小姐！\
**Neighbor II**: Mulson, the first timer? Not on your life, mate! I'm down for 005 Bartley. She's the top seed!

巷子里到处都是有关于乌卢鲁预选赛的摊铺，这里逼仄拥挤，每个人的脸上都涂有乌卢鲁的图案，庆祝着这场盛会。\
The alley is full of stalls for the Uluru Qualifiers. A crowd of people is gathered, their faces painted with Uluru symbols in anticipation of the event.

**摊贩**：比赛还有三天才开始，您现在投票并不算晚！\
**Vendor**: Three days to the qualifiers! Vote while you still can!

**摊贩**：先生，嘿！这位拿着黑雨伞的先生，别急着走啊，瞧，投票给您心中的冠军吧——\
**Vendor**: Sir, oi, you over there with the black brolly, come on over, and vote for the winner!

**摊贩**：嘿！您这先生，怎么撞我？！\
**Vendor**: Oi, mister, stop your pushing!

**福葛先生**：……呼、呼……噢，不好意思，我……\
**Mr. Fog**: *panting* Oh, I'm terribly sorry, I ...

**宽檐帽**：我们在巡逻！不好意思，伙计！\
**Brimley**: Sorry, mate, we're on patrol!

**巡逻警察Ⅰ**：头儿，那边有骚乱。\
**Police Constable I**: Sir, we have a situation over there.

**巡逻警察Ⅱ**：跟上去。\
**Police Constable II**: Let's follow them.

**无线电广播**：现在即将公布我们乌卢鲁分赛区预选赛的初步推举名单……\
**Radio Broadcast**: Now introducing the competitors for the Uluru London Qualifiers.

**威尔**：零零五号！零零五号！零零五号！\
**Will**: Bartley, Bartley, Bartley!

**街坊Ⅰ**：零零……嗷！谁在撞我！\
**Neighbor I**: Oi! Who pushed me?

**街坊Ⅱ**：——啊！好痛！是您在撞我？！\
**Neighbor II**: Ouch! Mind your step, will you?

**街坊Ⅰ**：别胡搅蛮缠，您的眼神可真是好，我什么时候撞您了？\
**Neighbor I**: Me? Was you that pushed me, weren't it! You should be the one minding your own feet!

**宽檐帽**：——完了，完蛋了，福葛伙计，咱们撞到太多人了……这人一多起来，他们也分不清是谁撞的谁……我看他们就要打起来了！\
**Brimley**: Arthur, I think we're only making things worse trying to move through this crowd.

**巡逻警察Ⅰ**：找到骚乱中心了，头儿，要上吗？\
**Police Constable I**: Looks like we've found our troublemakers. What do we do?

**巡逻警察Ⅱ**：跟上去，看看是什么人在引发骚乱！\
**Police Constable II**: Keep up with them, and bring them in!

**巡逻警察Ⅰ**：是！\
**Police Constable I**: Yes sir!

**福葛先生**：呼……呼……呼……\
**Mr. Fog**: *panting*

**宽檐帽**：呼哧……呼哧……呼哧……\
**Brimley**: *panting*

**宽檐帽**：福、福葛伙计……以后这种事，我就恕不奉陪了，我感觉……有点天昏地暗的。\
**Brimley**: Arthur, next time, don't, don't get me involved. I think I'm feeling sick.

**福葛先生**：——哈哈，放宽心，还好那小子最后把麻绳给咱们了。\
**Mr. Fog**: Haha, but he gave us the rope after all.

看着手里一小节麻绳，福葛笑了。\
Mr. Fog grins as he looks at the small length of rope in his hand.

**巡逻警察Ⅰ**：给我站住！\
**Police Constable I**: Stop right there!

一回头，身后站着两位巡逻警察。\
He turns his head, and there, standing behind him, are two constables.

**巡逻警察Ⅰ**：刚才在巷子里发生了一起斗殴事件，我们认为始作俑者正是二位，还希望不耽误你们的时间，跟我们走一趟。\
**Police Constable I**: Seems you two rough sleepers are wanted in connection with a fight breaking out on Cross Street. I'll ask you to come quietly and cooperate.

**宽檐帽**：好伙计，说点什么！\
**Brimley**: Mate? Say something!

**福葛先生**：好……这么一来我的实验道具就齐了，麻绳可以作为传导介质将吸纳口纳入的大颗粒分子过滤进入净化器皿中……\
**Mr. Fog**: Wonderful! Now I have everything I need for my experiment! The properties of this sea-worn rope should be able to conduct the large particles into the purification vessels.

**宽檐帽**：——你还在关心你所谓的“研究”！\
**Brimley**: Mate, shut your gob for a minute and listen!

**福葛先生**：……对对！没错！我想到了！甄别和测量微尘还需要更加精密的实验和仪器……嗯？我怎么被铐住了？\
**Mr. Fog**: Yes, perfection! But how to measure and screen the size of the particles? We will need more sophisticated equipment. Huh? Why am I being handcuffed?

**巡逻警察Ⅰ**：先生，还请跟我们去一趟治安局……\
**Police Constable I**: Because you're being placed under arrest, sir.

两位巡警刚一近身，突然愣住了。\
The moment the two constables draw near, they freeze in place.

**巡逻警察Ⅰ**：等一下……\
**Police Constable I**: Wait a second.

两位巡警瞪大了眼睛。\
Their eyes widen.

**巡逻警察Ⅰ**：——您……您是福葛先生？\
**Police Constable I**: Mr. Fog? Is that you?

**宽檐帽**：——而我是他的助手宽檐帽……一顶会说话的帽子，难道不比一名英国男人显眼得多吗？\
**Brimley**: Bloody hell! Are you seriously telling me you recognized Fog before me! How many talking hats do you know?

**巡逻警察Ⅱ**：不好意思，一定是这雾太大了的缘故……如果不是您的黑雨伞，当真是认不出您……\
**Police Constable II**: Terribly sorry, gentlemen. I might not have recognized you through all this fog were it not for that iconic umbrella of yours.

**宽檐帽**：对，这雾，确实太浓了，我甚至刚才都没看清楚是谁铐住了我……是谁呢？\
**Brimley**: Oh, naturally. Just as I've somehow failed to recognize the two ignoramuses that tried to handcuff a hat!

个子稍矮的巡逻警察一直在向另外一个使眼色。\
The shorter constable gives a series of subtle eye signals to the other.

**巡逻警察Ⅱ**：非常抱歉，雾行者先生，宽檐帽先生。\
**Police Constable II**: We're sorry again, Mr. Fogwalker and Mr. Brimley.

**巡逻警察Ⅱ**：但是介于您……扰乱治安、还——涉嫌偷窃……\
**Police Constable II**: But, we do need to ask you some questions, what with you running around disturbing the peace and nicking all these strange things you've got there.

**福葛先生**：噢！这可不是偷窃，小伙子们，这些可都是……要用作正途的东西，我要用它们治理伦敦的怪雾。\
**Mr. Fog**: Oh, I didn't steal anything! This is all just rubbish, and it's for official business. I'm going to lift the fog from London!

两位巡逻警察思考了片刻后，脸上露出尴尬又刻薄的微笑。\
The two constables pause for a moment before their faces break into awkwardly sardonic smiles.

**巡逻警察Ⅱ**：噢好的，好的，雾行者先生。一场误会。\
**Police Constable II**: I see, I see. All just a terrible misunderstanding then!

**巡逻警察Ⅱ**：我愿意相信这一定又是一系列对您的驱雾研究卓有帮助的玩意。\
**Police Constable II**: Naturally, a bit of old rope, a car horn, unmistakably the latest in technology.

**巡逻警察Ⅱ**：但愿您确实用它们解决了关乎全民的实际问题。\
**Police Constable II**: Anyways, mates. Best we let you go. You've got a city to save.

**巡逻警察Ⅱ**：那我们先走了。\
**Police Constable II**: We'll be off now.

解除手铐，宽檐帽舒展了一下自己的身子。\
With the handcuffs removed, Brimley takes a moment to stretch.

**宽檐帽**：即使我并没有手，但还是被这种用于惩戒罪恶的武器吓得不轻。\
**Brimley**: Glad that's over. I'm no fan of handcuffs, even if I don't have any hands.

**福葛先生**：别吵，老帽儿，我正在思考它们的拼装方式……现在最难的要点在于如何将净化后的……\
**Mr. Fog**: A little quiet, old chap. I'm just in the middle of a thought. How might I assemble it?

**小丽莎**：——不好意思打扰了，我刚刚偷听了你们的对话。\
**Little Lisa**: I-I'm sorry, mister, but I just heard what happened.

**宽檐帽**：……？\
**Brimley**: Huh?

**福葛先生**：……？\
**Mr. Fog**: Huh?

福葛先生和宽檐帽都没发现自己身边探出来一颗小头，她看上去只有纸信圈儿一半的年纪。\
Neither one of them had noticed the little girl who had appeared before them. She looks only half as old as Flutterpage.

**小丽莎**：您一定知道让这团围绕着我们的巨大烟雾怪消失的办法吧，雾行者先生。\
**Little Lisa**: Did you say "lifting the fog," mister? Are you really going to get rid of the big scary fog monster?

她眨巴着亮晶晶的眼睛，像小金鱼一样盯着福葛先生。\
She blinks, her eyes bright and sparkling as she stares at Mr. Fog like a little goldfish in a tank.

**小丽莎**：您一定知道能够治疗妈妈的方法吧！\
**Little Lisa**: Will that mean you can cure my mummy?

**小丽莎**：您一定能让咱们看到绿色的树和蓝色的天吧！\
**Little Lisa**: And bring back the blue sky?

宽檐帽瞥了福葛先生一眼。\
Brimley glances at Mr. Fog.

**小丽莎**：……可以吗？\
**Little Lisa**: Right?

似乎并没有人回答她，于是问话者慢慢变得紧张起来。\
When no one responds, the little girl grows anxious.

**小丽莎**：……那至少，乌卢鲁运动会，一定是能按时召开的吧……？\
**Little Lisa**: And, and then, we can still have the Uluru Games, right?

她的眼睛不停地在宽檐帽和福葛先生身上摇摆，企图得到些许安慰。\
Her eyes dart back and forth between Brimley and Mr. Fog, looking for any trace of comfort.

**小丽莎**：妈妈说，如果雾一直不散，运动会可能就没有办法在这儿举办了，这……是真的吗？\
**Little Lisa**: My mummy said, if the fog keeps sticking around making people sick, then the games won't come.

她声音里开始透出一丝哭腔。\
A faint sob starts to creep into her voice.

福葛先生蹲下身子，他将自己一麻袋的“宝贝”抖了出来，摊在地上。\
Mr. Fog crouches down and shakes his sack of treasures, spreading them out on the ground.

**宽檐帽**：……伙计，这恐怕不是一个炫耀你古怪藏品的好时机……\
**Brimley**: Mate, this really isn't the time or place.

**福葛先生**：一个充气喇叭、一个探头仪、银勺子和一根短短的麻绳……\
**Mr. Fog**: A klaxon, a probe, a spoon, and a spool of weathered rope ...

**福葛先生**：一直连接到玻璃浴缸里……\
**Mr. Fog**: Assembled like so, perhaps using a large pot or a baby's bathtub ...

他皱着眉头，认真鼓捣着。\
He furrows his brow, absorbed in the task at hand.

小女孩也撑着膝盖，弓腰仔仔细细地看着。\
The girl gets on her knees as she leans in to get a closer look.

**福葛先生**：最后，还有一点点的神秘奇迹……\
**Mr. Fog**: It will still need a touch of the miraculous.

福葛先生对着玻璃器皿的肚子轻轻吹了一口气。\
He gently blows into the base of the glass vessel.

玻璃器皿里面突然噼啪作响地闪烁起几簇短暂的烟花。\
There's a crackling sound as a few sparks of light flash briefly in the glass container.

不一会儿，里面亮起细微的光亮。\
Before long, a tiny, steady light is glowing within.

**福葛先生**：你瞧……\
**Mr. Fog**: Voilà!

**小丽莎**：它在吸着什么。\
**Little Lisa**: It's breathing!

机器嗡嗡地运作着，似乎将空气吸进了它的身体中，过滤一遍又从身后排了出来。\
The machine hums as it draws in air, filters it, and releases it through the other side.

**福葛先生**：是的……\
**Mr. Fog**: Yes.

**福葛先生**：小家伙，乌卢鲁运动会是能够在充满阳光的伦敦正常召开的。\
**Mr. Fog**: The Uluru Qualifiers will not just be fog-free, my little friend. They will be sunny.

**福葛先生**：怎么样，要不要一起参与这个伟大的研究？\
**Mr. Fog**: But I'll need some help. Would you and your friends join me in this project, young lady?

小女孩的脸上洋溢起红晕。\
The little girl's face blushes red.

**小丽莎**：——好！我、我要来帮您，我……我还会叫上外公、妈妈、马蒂姑姑一家都来帮您的！\
**Little Lisa**: Y-Yes! I'll help. I'll ask my grandpa, my mummy, and Auntie Martha to help, too!

**福葛先生**：越多人越好，我们要打造的，可是一个史上最大的雾气净化器——“伦敦煤烟污染勘察与清除大使”！\
**Mr. Fog**: The more, the merrier! We're going to build the largest fog purification machine on earth—The London Air Pollution Auto-Detect Cleaner!

**宽檐帽**：……还是叫……吸尘器吧。\
**Brimley**: That just looks like a great honking big vacuum to me, mate.

**笃笃骨**：苏利丝，苏利丝，我猎取生长的万物，作为你的牺牲。\
**Willow**: Sulis, Sulis, all life's offerings I bring, as sacrifice to you, from the growing spring.

**笃笃骨**：萌芽之光，被包于世界之蛋中。\
**Willow**: The light will sprout within the world's egg lay.

**笃笃骨**：你以遍寻无果的终曲，降下父母律法的欢言。\
**Willow**: Your endless quest brings parents' joyful day.

**纸信圈儿**：降下父母律法的欢言……\
**Flutterpage**: Parents' joyful day ...

**笃笃骨**：够了，停下。\
**Willow**: What are you, a parrot?

舞到半空中的笃笃骨，以倒吊的姿势维持了一个小时后终于忍不住开口了。\
After hanging in the upside-down pose of her ribbon dance for an hour, Willow finally decides to break the silence.

**笃笃骨**：你可以再多吵上一个分贝，这样也别去运动会了，直接就地埋了会是我最好的归宿。\
**Willow**: Fine, keep on then. Annoy an old woman to death if you like.

**纸信圈儿**：看来你今天练习的心情特别差，是本周内最差的一天……而且我发现你每隔32个小时都骂一次，骂我、骂蚂蚁还有球刺花。\
**Flutterpage**: Another bad mood, eh, Ms. Willow? This one's your worst this week. I counted it up. Every 32 hours, steady as a clock, you start scoldin' me, scoldin' the plants, the ants, even flowers.

**笃笃骨**：我们说好了，你不能再偷窥我。\
**Willow**: I thought we'd agreed—no more peeking round my house without permission.

**纸信圈儿**：可是你并没有把我赶出去，还给我吃柠檬果酱和黑面包。你明明对我很好，为什么总要装得很凶？\
**Flutterpage**: Yeah, but you didn't kick me out, did you? And you gave me some rye bread and lemon jam. Don't quite know why you keep tryin' to act the big meanie, Ms. Willow. I know you're a softie, now—deep down.

“嗞——”悬吊着笃笃骨的彩带终于承受不住地散了，笃笃骨从倒挂着的空中掉了下来。\
*rrrrip—* The ribbon suspending Willow finally gives way, sending her quickly to the ground.

重重地，摔在了地上。\
She hits the floor with a heavy thud.

**纸信圈儿**：笃笃骨小姐——！\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Willow!

**笃笃骨**：噢……嘶——痛……\
**Willow**: Ouch! Ah, it hurts.

**？？？**：你这是在为了预选赛而练习吗？\
**???**: Are you practicing for the qualifiers?

一个声音从背后遥远地传来。\
A distant voice reaches her.

笃笃骨抽了抽嘴角。\
The corner of Willow's mouth twitches.

**纸信圈儿**：“白天鹅”，你又来了。\
**Flutterpage**: Hello again, Ms. Swan.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

一位银发女性站在花园外，蜷曲的食人球根茎遮掩着她一半的脸庞。\
A blonde woman stands on the other side of the garden fence, her face half-covered by the curled stems of a carnivorous plant.

## LD-09 天平与角逐 / Hesitation and Challenge

**牙仙**：小心一些，来，跟着我一起……吐——\
**Tooth Fairy**: Be careful. Now you can spit it out. Right.

**病人Ⅰ**：呕……呕……\
**Patient I**: *puke*

污秽落入水桶，而神秘学医师没有一丝侧目。\
Vomit plunges into a bucket. Tooth Fairy doesn't spare it a second thought.

**牙仙**：好了，这是今天的第五个。我在糖果里放入了可以短暂稀释咳痰的金粉，他们会感觉呼吸轻松不少。\
**Tooth Fairy**: That's the fifth one today. I added a bit of powder into the candy to loosen up their phlegm. It should help them breathe a little easier.

**护士**：太感谢您了，基金会的小姐……鉴于这种病是最近才流行起来，您的临床经验对于我们来说实在起到了很大的帮助。\
**Nurse**: Thank you so much, Doctor. We really had no idea what to do with this new variant of tuberculosis. You and the Foundation have been a real asset to us.

**牙仙**：不用这么客气。身体及其健康问题，会与每个人切身相关。我很高兴我的办法能够起到一定疗效。\
**Tooth Fairy**: You're welcome. This is a matter of vital health for all of us. I'm very glad to see the treatment is proving effective.

**牙仙**：而且宝贵的临床经验也能为我研究这类“雾病诅咒”提供更大的帮助。\
**Tooth Fairy**: And I hope that our clinical experience here might contribute to solving this "fog curse" as well.

**护士**：……真希望这一切能赶紧到头，大家都能看上运动会。\
**Nurse**: All I'm hoping for is for this mess to end soon, so we can go watch the Games together.

**牙仙**：看来，医护站也有关注运动会的传统。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Really, so the staff here are fans of the Uluru Games as well?

**护士**：实际上，他们每个人都有自己喜欢和追捧的对象，他们跟着一起支持、猜测、紧张甚至……\
**Nurse**: Not just the staff. Everyone here loves a bit of sport! We're always listening to the broadcasts over the radio down in the ward.

**护士**：有些病人还会自己去花园里做些运动呢。\
**Nurse**: It's all quite motivating. Sometimes we even get the patients out onto the commons to practice.

**护士**：运动会期间的医院，是我最喜欢的医院。\
**Nurse**: Something about the coming of a big sporting event always brings people together.

**牙仙**：……\
**Tooth Fairy**: ...

**牙仙**：能够理解——我也注意到一张海报很久了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: That's all very good to hear. But actually, it was this poster that grabbed my attention.

她指了指贴在病床旁边的小海报。\
She points to the small poster pinned beside the bed.

泛黄的画面中呈现出不太清晰的脸庞。\
The picture is faded. It's too difficult to make out the face of the athlete.

**护士**：啊……！她……\
**Nurse**: Ah! That's her!

**护士**：她确实很美，不是吗？\
**Nurse**: Gorgeous, isn't she?

**牙仙**：……她是……\
**Tooth Fairy**: May I ask who she is?

**护士**：……她是这位病人最喜欢的运动员——\
**Nurse**: She happens to be this patient's favorite competitor of all time.

**护士**：这可怜的小姑娘收藏了很多她的海报，每一张照片都用剪刀仔仔细细地剪下来，夹在各种地方——书页里、钱夹子里……\
**Nurse**: She collected all of her posters and clippings. She even keeps a few photos of her as a bookmark, and in her purse.

**牙仙**：这位运动员……\
**Tooth Fairy**: Her favorite ritualist ...

**卡洛琳**：或许，你这么多年不待客是因为没办法煮好一壶最味美的红茶以迎接她远道而来的朋友？\
**Caroline Bartley**: Looks like you haven't had a proper guest in ages. Have you forgotten how to make a cup of tea?

**笃笃骨**：你倒是把我的消息打听得彻彻底底。\
**Willow**: You like to presume, don't you?

**笃笃骨**：既然知道我闭门已久，为什么还要来找不痛快呢？\
**Willow**: So, why are you here, then? Just to enjoy the sound of a door slamming in your face?

**卡洛琳**：噢，那看来是我的过错了。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Oh, how terrible of me for wanting to visit an old friend.

**笃笃骨**：卡洛琳小姐，你似乎是千里迢迢专门从南约克郡赶来报名比赛，并顺便探望你的老对手。\
**Willow**: So then, Ms. Bartley, you came all the way down from Yorkshire just to gawk at an old rival? I should feel lucky, should I?

**笃笃骨**：但很抱歉，我现下确实没有闲工夫陪你谈天说地聊家常，也不愿意叨扰你的冠军梦。\
**Willow**: Truth is I don't care to chatter about with you, not now, not ever.

**笃笃骨**：还请便吧，小姐——纸信圈儿，咱们继续吧。\
**Willow**: So you can just turn around and march yourself home. Flutterpage, back to business.

笃笃骨瞥了一眼站在花园外的女人后，转身回到原地，给了纸信圈儿一个眼神。\
After glancing at Caroline, Willow turns and gives Flutterpage a look.

可是纸信圈儿却一直愣愣地盯着卡洛琳。\
But Flutterpage is too busy staring at Caroline, her face vacant.

**纸信圈儿**：可是她喜欢你，她想找你玩。\
**Flutterpage**: Why'd you send her away like that? She just wants to practice with you. She likes you.

**笃笃骨**：……你管好你的秒表，我数三、二、一就开始，练习一秒都不能耽搁。\
**Willow**: Focus on your stopwatch, on the count of three. No time to waste.

**纸信圈儿**：她并没有离开。\
**Flutterpage**: She's still there.

**笃笃骨**：腿不是长在你身上，你不必操心别人是否物尽其用。\
**Willow**: She's none of our concern.

**纸信圈儿**：她和你很久没见了，她一定很想念你。\
**Flutterpage**: And you ain't seen each other in a long time. Bet she misses you a lot.

**笃笃骨**：看在上天的份上，小知了。人们的好心善意多半不是异想天开就是自欺欺人。\
**Willow**: For Pete's sake, Buzzie, no one does something like that just out of the goodness of their own heart. She has her reasons.

纸信圈儿懂事地闭上嘴，而后又不甘心地瞪着眼睛回头看向卡洛琳。\
Flutterpage obediently closes her mouth but can't help herself from giving Caroline a reluctant glance.

**卡洛琳**：她说的没错，夏洛特。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Charlotte, you know she's right.

**卡洛琳**：我想看看你。如果这样的表述对于你来说有感情上的负担的话，我也愿意换一种方式表述——\
**Caroline Bartley**: I have missed you. I want to see you, but if you really want to know the reason ...

**卡洛琳**：我想与你，再次同台竞技。\
**Caroline Bartley**: I want to challenge you again.

**卡洛琳**：……你认为这样的表述，会更易于接受一点吗？\
**Caroline Bartley**: The question is, do you?

**护士**：您……认识她吗？这个运动员。\
**Nurse**: Do you know her?

**牙仙**：……\
**Tooth Fairy**: ...

**牙仙**：……夏洛特·奥黑根……\
**Tooth Fairy**: Charlotte O'Hagan ...

**护士**：噢——对，对，是叫这个名字。\
**Nurse**: Oh. Right! That's the name.

**护士**：事实上，如果不是这可怜的小姑娘，我也不会记起还有这么一个运动员了。\
**Nurse**: Truth is, if it weren't for our little patient, I doubt I'd remember her.

**护士**：大家都说夏洛特·奥黑根老了、疏于锻炼，早就拿不出曾经的竞技状态了；还有人说她用药成瘾、沉迷于醉生梦死的黑暗中。\
**Nurse**: Most people think she's too old to compete now—that she's retired to God knows where; others say she's become an addict, wasting her life away.

**护士**：甚至前几年还有小报报道她早就死了，尸体被搁置在浴室三个月都没人发现……\
**Nurse**: I guess I heard in the gossip rags that some people think she's keeled over and died.

**护士**：……总之，她不可能再回到赛场了。\
**Nurse**: Too bad for this young lady, but I doubt we'll ever see her in the Games again.

**护士**：这小姑娘喜欢的，是一个不会再为他们带来骄傲的运动员了。\
**Nurse**: Wherever she is, she's like as not to lose, even if she did compete.

**笃笃骨**：挑战？你可真是生怕这世界上有哪个角落不知道小姐你参加了比赛啊。\
**Willow**: You just want to announce to the world you've beat me, eh? Think that'll be a fair challenge, do you?

**笃笃骨**：你要找同场竞技的竞争对手，可以把目光投向可能性更高一点的群体，比如——你的队友们？\
**Willow**: Perhaps you ought to find someone a little more your speed, someone who is still in one piece.

**卡洛琳**：……\
**Caroline Bartley**: ...

**笃笃骨**：我还是那句话，小姐。\
**Willow**: Again, Ms. Bartley.

**笃笃骨**：请便吧——我家里没有合你口味的红茶。\
**Willow**: Please turn around. I haven't any sort of tea you'd like.

**卡洛琳**：……\
**Caroline Bartley**: ...

**卡洛琳**：……你可真是……变了太多了。\
**Caroline Bartley**: You have changed, haven't you, Charlotte?

**卡洛琳**：……呃！\
**Caroline Bartley**: Hmph!

短暂的感叹过后，卡洛琳却突然向笃笃骨抛出了彩带。\
After a brief moment of surprise, Caroline throws a ribbon at Willow.

彩带狠厉地向笃笃骨刺去，紧紧地擦着她身体的边际，冲向了笃笃骨身后。\
The ribbon lashes fiercely, grazing the side of Willow's body before shooting past her.

**笃笃骨**：——你在干什么？\
**Willow**: What the blazes are you doing?

**笃笃骨**：什么？\
**Willow**: What?

彩带收回到卡洛琳身后，此时陶瓷茶杯已然落入她的手里，她好整以暇地看着笃笃骨。\
Caroline pulls the ribbon back toward her, the cup landing squarely in her hand. She stands there calmly, her eyes still on Willow.

**卡洛琳**：你说，我喝不了你的红茶，那你怎么解释它现在完好无损地来到了我的手上。\
**Caroline Bartley**: You just said you don't have any tea I'd like, but I think this one is just to my taste.

**纸信圈儿**：嘿——笃笃骨，她这玩意儿好神奇，就像人们的道德底线一样能屈能伸！\
**Flutterpage**: Wow, Ms. Willow, that ribbon is amazin'! It can go from long to short in a second!

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

**笃笃骨**：脱手小抛彩带，十米隔空操控，带转体接实物，没有失误。问题在于动作的功用性达标，美观度不足。\
**Willow**: Aye, a little toss of the ribbon to take control of an object at a distance of 10 meters, catch an object after a turn. You did it. Well done. But your aesthetics were lazy.

**笃笃骨**：这是你一贯的问题了，但我注意到你改进了动作里的小毛病，你的左肩有意在控制偏移度，这是好的。\
**Willow**: You're controlling the angle of your left shoulder, which is good, but it only means you're compensating for your poor stance.

**卡洛琳**：——！\
**Caroline Bartley**: ...!

**卡洛琳**：哈……感激不尽……\
**Caroline Bartley**: Heh. What then, are you expecting me to say thank you?

**笃笃骨**：不必这样说，你该感激的是你自己这几年来的努力。\
**Willow**: No need. Thank yourself for all that hard practice you must have done over all those years. You're almost good enough, now. Almost.

**笃笃骨**：那杯茶你留着吧，不用还我了——纸信圈儿，我们继续计时。\
**Willow**: Keep the cup. Let's go back to our timing, Flutterpage.

**纸信圈儿**：嗯……那好吧，我先跟您说再见啦，白天鹅小姐～\
**Flutterpage**: Alright. Bye bye, Ms. Swan!

卡洛琳端着茶杯，呆愣在原地。\
For a moment, Caroline stands there motionlessly, cup in hand.

而后，她缓缓垂下眼皮，将茶杯搁在篱笆上，转身离开。\
Then, she gradually lowers her eyes, places the cup on the fence post, and turns to walk away.

刚走了几步后，身后响起笃笃骨的声音，不大，但是清晰。\
She has barely walked a few steps when Willow's voice reaches her from behind, not loud, but clear.

**笃笃骨**：对了——\
**Willow**: Oh, by the by.

**笃笃骨**：你刚才的彩带技术，是从我在贝尔丹火焰节表演赛的赛场上学来的吧？\
**Willow**: The ribbon technique you just did. I know you learnt it from me, from my performance at the Beltane Exhibition Match. Am I right?

**卡洛琳**：……嗯？！\
**Caroline Bartley**: Hmm?

从笃笃骨背影里传来的声音，使人无法就此踱步离开。\
The tone of her voice makes it almost impossible to simply walk away.

**卡洛琳**：……你说什么？\
**Caroline Bartley**: Excuse me?

**笃笃骨**：你的一招一式，甚至连彩带的款式本身，都跟十一岁那时的我一模一样。\
**Willow**: Each and every move, you copied it from my routine, right down to the ribbon.

**卡洛琳**：……呃……\
**Caroline Bartley**: What?

**纸信圈儿**：唔！小姐，您的脸好红，就像我爸爸在《潘趣酒》杂志上看到了一则好笑的笑话。\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Swan, your face is all red, like my daddy's face when he reads a funny joke in his Punch books.

**卡洛琳**：……我……学你？\
**Caroline Bartley**: Me ... Learnt from you?

**笃笃骨**：不要让我往后猜，你刚才的动作也是为了在我面前复刻当时决胜局的最后一招吧。\
**Willow**: You were taunting me right in front of my face, with my own routine, the very innovator that made it.

**笃笃骨**：得到了原创者本人的认可，对你来说真算得上是不小的激励了。\
**Willow**: I suppose it was just an attempt to win my approval, was it?

**卡洛琳**：我……学你？\
**Caroline Bartley**: You really think that, don't you?

**笃笃骨**：可就像我第一次见你的时候一样，你刻苦有余却美感不足……\
**Willow**: But, I'm afraid you're not different than when we last competed, Caroline. Aye, you're diligent, but you were never graceful enough.

**笃笃骨**：如果你愿意将更多的精力放在提高审美这一块，我相信你会走得比现在更远。\
**Willow**: That's what holds you back from glory in Floor Ritual. Your aesthetic sensibility, it's all you've ever needed, but you still don't have it, do you now?

**卡洛琳**：……我……我——\
**Caroline Bartley**: I ... I ...

**笃笃骨**：作为你的前辈，我能给你的指导并不多，不要总是想着从其他人的经验里获得捷径，这对于施展个人的特色和灵性没有一丝帮助。\
**Willow**: You won't make any real progress reusing my old routines. Not unless you find your own way to express your pneuma and your own signature.

羞耻和悔意慢慢爬上运动员的脸上，她正在竭力遏制自己的怒火。\
Shame and regret slowly creep across Caroline's face as she struggles to contain her anger.

很可惜，她失败了。\
Then, it bursts forth.

**卡洛琳**：……我、学你——？\
**Caroline Bartley**: You really are full of yourself, aren't you, Charlotte?

**卡洛琳**：时至如今我在国际赛事上拿到的冠军已经堆积如山，沙漠祭祀公开赛、极光杯世界锦标赛……更不用提乌卢鲁本身。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Do you know how many titles I've won at the international tournaments? The Desert Floor Ritual Open, The Aurora Cup World Championship, and many others, let alone Uluru itself!

**卡洛琳**：在人们心里我的头衔早就盖过你了。我是这一届当之无愧的种子选手，以我名字命名的动作甚至写进了教材……\
**Caroline Bartley**: The name Caroline Bartley has long surpassed yours! I am the uncontested top seed in these Games. The records of my skills, my own skills, are in the training manuals for new witches.

**卡洛琳**：在你之后已经有无数人将这项运动推向了更高峰，难度系数、评分标准都更上一个台阶，你曾经的超越不过是现在所有人的基础。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Do you even know anything about the state of the competition these days? The rules and scoring systems are entirely different and higher in every way. The limits you once broke through are now considered standard for beginners.

**卡洛琳**：呵……我学你……？\
**Caroline Bartley**: Hah! But indeed, I learnt it all from you.

**卡洛琳**：……你早就失去了被模仿的资格，你早已不足为任何人所道。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Face it. You've been left behind. You're no longer the model of perfection.

**卡洛琳**：现在的你、你……不再是他们口中十万分之一的四叶酢浆草，只是一颗曾经在自由祭祀的世界里短暂闪耀过的星星，而我才是他们追捧的、恒常发亮的太阳。\
**Caroline Bartley**: You're just a shooting star that shined too briefly but eventually fell away. I am the rising sun. My name will be eternal in this sport, long after yours is forgotten.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

背对着卡洛琳的笃笃骨不经意地笑了。\
Willow smiles, her back turned to Caroline.

**笃笃骨**：那就是了。\
**Willow**: So be it.

**笃笃骨**：那就带着这份“荣耀”去参加比赛吧。\
**Willow**: Go on. Be the glorious sun.

**笃笃骨**：不要再来烦一个，不再有资格“被你打败”的对手了。\
**Willow**: And leave this fading star alone.

卡洛琳愣在原地。展翅而去的灰白鸽羽像一串白色梨花，散落在她头上。\
Caroline stands in shock as a couple of doves take flight, leaving behind a few drifting feathers.

**小丽莎**：马蒂姑姑！\
**Little Lisa**: Aunt Martha!

**护士**：噢，你回来了！我们正在讨论你呢？\
**Nurse**: Lisa, you're back! We were just talking about you.

**小丽莎**：什么？讨论我什么呀？\
**Little Lisa**: About me? What about me?

**牙仙**：正在讨论着……你似乎有一个非常厉害的梦想，以及一位非常喜欢的运动员。\
**Tooth Fairy**: About your dream and your favorite competitor.

**小丽莎**：噢噢！你们说的是夏洛特吗！\
**Little Lisa**: Oh, oh, you mean Charlotte O'Hagan?

**牙仙**：是的，我们……\
**Tooth Fairy**: Yes, we—

**小丽莎**：那太好了！我正好得知了一个好消息——福葛先生要弄一个大工程！\
**Little Lisa**: That's great! But Mr. Fog needs us for a project!

**小丽莎**：只要我们都参与进来，运动会就能顺利举办！到时候说不定夏洛特……甚至更多更多的运动员都会来参加比赛！\
**Little Lisa**: He says we can still have the Games if we all work together! Then maybe everyone will be able to attend the qualifiers! Maybe even Charlotte O'Hagan!

**牙仙**：大工程？\
**Tooth Fairy**: A project?

**护士**：什么大工程？\
**Nurse**: What sort of project?

小女孩的叫嚷似乎吸引了医院里许多人，人群疑惑地吵嚷起来。\
The girl's cries draw the attention of everyone in the hospital, creating a buzz of confusion.

**病人Ⅰ**：什么大工程？上次的除烟法案被下议院驳回之后，他们清洁大气委员会又要闹腾什么？\
**Patient I**: Give me a break. What are they planning to do this time? Another useless bill that won't pass the House of Lords?

**牙仙**：不好意思……但你说，福葛先生？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Sorry for interrupting. Did I hear you mention Mr. Fog?

**小丽莎**：是的！福葛先生！福葛先生说，他找到了一个好办法，能够让全伦敦的雾都被驱散！\
**Little Lisa**: Yes, Mr. Fog! He said he's making something that will lift all the fog from London!

**小丽莎**：——那就是他的大机器！\
**Little Lisa**: It's his great invention!

**小丽莎**：只要大家都来帮忙，这个机器能建得非常巨大。他现在需要的材料有很多……唔、有……玻璃丝器官、机械肺的活塞……还、还有……\
**Little Lisa**: With everyone's help, we can build a huuuge machine, but he says we'll need lots and lots of things, such as, um, pistons for the mechanic lung, and ...

稳重的脚步由远及近，一双大手揉了揉小女孩的头发。\
Calm, steady footsteps grow nearer, and a large hand tousles the little girl's hair.

**福葛先生**：接下来，就让我为大家讲解一下吧……\
**Mr. Fog**: I'll take it over from here. Thank you, Lisa.

**小丽莎**：福葛先生！\
**Little Lisa**: Mr. Fog!

**牙仙**：福葛先生？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Mr. Fog?

## LD-10 明珠蒙尘 / Dust-Covered Pearl

嘀嗒、嘀嗒、嘀嗒……\
*drip-drip-drip*

**纸信圈儿**：……\
**Flutterpage**: ...

**纸信圈儿**：……笃笃骨小姐，好像停水了。\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Willow, I think the water's been shut off.

**纸信圈儿**：您的水龙头里，一点儿水都没有了。\
**Flutterpage**: I opened it all the way, but nothing's coming out.

纸信圈儿歪着头观察着卫生间的水龙头，锈迹斑斑之下，要将小尾指伸进铁管内才能摸到一些湿润。\
Flutterpage tilts her head as she brings it in close and sticks her little finger into the faucet, feeling only a few drips of water.

嘀嗒、嘀嗒、嘀嗒……\
*drip-drip-drip*

吊在半空中的笃笃骨擦了一下脸上的汗珠。\
Dangling in midair, Willow wipes the beads of sweat from her face.

**笃笃骨**：停水了就去十字街联合协会问一下怎么回事，看看他们大白天的是不是又掉进杜松子酒桶里去了。\
**Willow**: Go to the water resource office, and ask the staff what's going on. If they're not there, they're probably at the Gin Barrel.

**纸信圈儿**：我知道——你想跟我说再见，那你可就没有计时算分的帮手了。\
**Flutterpage**: I know you want me to leave, but how're you goin' to track the time and score without me?

**笃笃骨**：哼。\
**Willow**: Hmph.

嘀嗒、嘀嗒、嘀嗒……\
*drip-drip-drip*

**笃笃骨**：洗净的心灵，饥饿的皮囊，正适于投身猎场，我奔跑在密林的小径——\
**Willow**: With a heart that's pure, and a body lean, to the hunt I go, through forest green.

术杖突然脱离左手，从空中掉了下来。\
Her wand unexpectedly slips from her left hand and plummets to the floor.

**笃笃骨**：该死，收拾收拾，继续。\
**Willow**: Feck. Pick it up and keep going, Charlotte.

**笃笃骨**：动作是没错的——旋转……过肩、背，以一朵天竺葵为支撑点跃起……然后……\
**Willow**: The movement's correct. First spin, then run the geranium over the shoulder, let it slide down the back, and as it falls to the ground, step on it to hop into the air, then ...

**笃笃骨**：苏利丝，苏利丝，我猎取生长的万物，作为你的牺牲……\
**Willow**: Sulis, Sulis, all life's offerings I bring, as sacrifice to you, from the growing spring ...

**笃笃骨**：呃！……不对！\
**Willow**: Ack! This is all wrong!

这次，她做到一半突然停止，皱起眉头。\
She halts, wrinkling her brow.

**笃笃骨**：……这样做不够流畅……\
**Willow**: The flow needs to be smoother.

**笃笃骨**：……再来。\
**Willow**: Alright, let's try this again.

**笃笃骨**：萌芽之光，被包于世界之蛋中……\
**Willow**: The sprouting light within the world's egg lays ...

“哒”——她轻盈地从空中平稳降落，机械假腿发出丝滑的鸣叫。\
*thud* She gracefully descends from the air, her mechanical prosthesis squeaking softly as she lands.

**纸信圈儿**：好耶——你完成了！！\
**Flutterpage**: Hooray! You did it!

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

**笃笃骨**：转体七百二十度，现在只有五百多度。\
**Willow**: This element requires a 720-degree turn. I haven't even made it to 600.

**纸信圈儿**：……啊……\
**Flutterpage**: Oh ...

**笃笃骨**：……再来。\
**Willow**: Once more from the beginning.

嘀嗒、嘀嗒、嘀嗒……\
*drip-drip-drip*

**笃笃骨**：你以遍寻无果的终曲，降下父母律法的欢言。\
**Willow**: Your endless quest brings parents' joyful days.

“咚”……那具躯体不知多少次俯卧在朽木地板上，暮间的日落将地心引力碾轧得无比沉重。\
*thud* Her body has collapsed on this rotted wooden floor countless times today, and with the setting sun, each fall feels heavier than the last.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

**纸信圈儿**：……\
**Flutterpage**: ...

**纸信圈儿**：……怎么样？\
**Flutterpage**: How 'bout this time?

**笃笃骨**：……我做到了。\
**Willow**: I did it.

**纸信圈儿**：——你说……什么？\
**Flutterpage**: You did what?

**笃笃骨**：我说，我做到了。\
**Willow**: I completed the element. I did it.

**纸信圈儿**：！！！\
**Flutterpage**: !!!

**纸信圈儿**：——太好了！！！\
**Flutterpage**: Blimey!

**纸信圈儿**：你是说，你做到了那个……那个你之前一直挂在嘴上的、的动作？\
**Flutterpage**: So you mean, you did that-that move you've always talked about?

**笃笃骨**：自由式转体720度超高难度空中抛接术杖。\
**Willow**: The two-and-a-half turn with free leg backwards and upwards, wand throw and catch.

**纸信圈儿**：完成了这个，你就能完成一整场祭祀仪式了吗？\
**Flutterpage**: Does that mean you can complete the ritual, too?

**笃笃骨**：……是的……\
**Willow**: Yes.

笃笃骨看着手里的天竺葵，粉色的、柔嫩的叶面静悄悄地躺在她的手心。\
Willow examines the geranium in her hand, the tender pink leaves quietly resting in her palm.

即使经历了刚才的一串动作，它的花瓣都没有掉下一片、损耗一厘。\
Not a single petal has fallen or been harmed in any way.

**笃笃骨**：好吧……今天的训练，可以到此为止了。\
**Willow**: Alright. That's enough for today.

**纸信圈儿**：……嗯？\
**Flutterpage**: Hmm?

**笃笃骨**：已经到了吃晚餐的时间了，我想你的妈妈一定正在家里与煮肉、油煎鲷鱼和酵母面包一起等着你。\
**Willow**: It's supper time. Your mother must be waiting for you to come home with beef stew, fried fish, and bread.

**纸信圈儿**：可是我知道，你平常到了这个点还能继续练习三个小时。\
**Flutterpage**: But why? You usually train for about three more hours.

**笃笃骨**：今天不一样，今天我累了……呵～呵欠～！累死我了……啊……\
**Willow**: Not today. I need a break. *yawn* I'm totally exhausted.

**纸信圈儿**：……唔……\
**Flutterpage**: Hmm.

纸信圈儿站在原地，全然没有离开的意思。\
Flutterpage stays exactly where she is, showing no desire to move.

**笃笃骨**：……怎么，非要逼我揪着你的蝴蝶结，把你甩到大街上不成吗？\
**Willow**: Why are you still standing there? Do I need to get His Majesty's limousine to pick you up?

**纸信圈儿**：——我懂了，这种时候要是再不离开，球刺花和毛齿精就要来挠我耳朵了。\
**Flutterpage**: Oh, I get it. If I don't leave now, the critters in the garden will bite my ears.

她小声嘀咕着，快速走到门边。\
She mumbles on to herself as she quickly makes her way to the door.

**笃笃骨**：慢走不送。\
**Willow**: Good, I won't see you off.

一阵风将古宅大门撞开后，“哐”地一声，笃笃骨竖起术杖，隔空将门狠狠扣紧。\
A gust of wind blows in through the door as Flutterpage makes her exit. With a flick of Willow's wand, she slams it shut behind her.

房间里回归鼓囊囊的寂静。\
The room settles back into its muted, oppressive stillness.

嘀嗒、嘀嗒、嘀嗒……\
*drip-drip-drip*

笃笃骨走进厨房。昏黄的日光下，她关上门，把自己拖在地上的影子斩断。\
Willow steps into the pale yellow light of the kitchen and shuts the door behind her.

**笃笃骨**：……该死、该死、该死……\
**Willow**: Ack, bloody!

**笃笃骨**：你这个发臭了的润滑脂膏，想赖在我的坩埚上不走，你争取过谁的同意了？\
**Willow**: You filthy little stain! Who ever gave you permission to stick to my cauldron?!

坐在水池旁边的笃笃骨，正专心致志地搓洗着一顶坩埚。\
Willow sits beside the sink, absorbed in cleaning her cauldron.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

**笃笃骨**：……呼……哈哈——放了一水池的餐具都没洗，倒是跟这个小小的坩埚干上了——还正好赶在停水的时候。\
**Willow**: *pant* Look at me! I have a whole sink of dishes that haven't washed, and here I am, fighting a little stain on a cauldron, and when the water's just shut off, too!

**笃笃骨**：呼，好吧——停水……我好像叫那个小知了去问水力局了，真希望她的小脑袋瓜能装进这么一点小事。\
**Willow**: I did ask Buzzie to visit the water resource office. Hopefully it didn't slip her mind, if she even knows how to use it.

**笃笃骨**：没关系……就算是停水，我也能把这顶坩埚刷干净。\
**Willow**: Never mind. I can clean it off without water.

**笃笃骨**：……呃……呃……嘿！\
**Willow**: *pant* Hah!

**笃笃骨**：哈！可给我刷下来了！\
**Willow**: Got it! It's off!

**笃笃骨**：你这个顽固的家伙……你这个——全世界都遗忘你、厌恶你、浪费你、避之不及的——臭脂膏。\
**Willow**: You stubborn little thing. Everyone loathes you, avoids you like the plague. You're just a pathetic little stain, clinging to what you can.

**笃笃骨**：还妄想黏在我的坩埚壁上，就像有些人还想残缺地进犯一个神圣的舞台？\
**Willow**: Do you have no shame? To sully the sacred floor with your artificial leg!

**笃笃骨**：就算你现在终于做出了那个动作又能怎么样？\
**Willow**: So what if you finished the element?!

**笃笃骨**：你不可能变回去，也不可能去做一个小丑，你懂吗？你配不上它，你再也配不上它……\
**Willow**: It won't bring back your leg! Without it, you're no different from a clown! How could you possibly compete again?! You're not qualified!

**笃笃骨**：是了……\
**Willow**: No, I'm not.

**笃笃骨**：从一开始就不该花钱去订做这么昂贵精致的假肢，不该每日每夜地练习——\
**Willow**: All the money I spent on this leg, all the efforts I made to finish the ritual, they're utterly pointless!

**笃笃骨**：像你现在不吃炸土豆，不吃甜食，但凡多吞下一口奶油就要用十倍的练习量来弥补过错……嗯？有意义吗……？\
**Willow**: When was the last time I ate dessert? Or even a chip, for that matter? Year after year, I've trained harder than the last to make up for my leg, but what's the point?

搓洗声戛然而止，急促的呼吸被慢慢压下。\
She flings the scrubbing brush into the cauldron, and her heavy breathing gradually slows down.

**笃笃骨**：哼……呵呵……但是没关系……现在好了，现在都好了。\
**Willow**: Heh, forget it. Everything will be alright.

**笃笃骨**：只要放弃，不要去想，不要去希望……不要回顾，也不要往前望……\
**Willow**: Just give up. Stop thinking about it. Stop hoping. Don't look back or ahead.

**笃笃骨**：看——\
**Willow**: Just look at the cauldron.

趁着微弱的灯光，笃笃骨将刷得干干净净的坩埚抬高，举到眼前。\
Beneath the dim light, Willow raises her now sparkling clean cauldron to eye level.

**笃笃骨**：这不还是被刷干净了……你再也不用强迫自己黏在埚壁上了……\
**Willow**: See how clean it is now? Stop clinging to places where you don't belong.

**笃笃骨**：——瞧你现在多干净……\
**Willow**: The world is perfect without you.

沉寂了许久的生锈水龙头，突然咳出喷射般的水柱，水花炸裂在台面的每一个角落，将还未反应过来的笃笃骨吓了一跳。\
The rusted faucet suddenly sputters out a blast of water. It splashes across the counter, startling Willow.

**笃笃骨**：——哦！\
**Willow**: Ah!

笃笃骨以运动员的条件反应力弹开，紧接着她的眼角捕捉到放在桌面的一张纸片。\
Willow leaps back with the reflexes of a true athlete. Her gaze quickly falls on the piece of paper on the table.

**笃笃骨**：……噢我的老天——！\
**Willow**: No!

她冲过去，在疯狂喷射的水柱底下救下了那片纸片。\
She dashes forward, snatching the paper away from the raging spray of water.

——那是乌卢鲁伦敦预选赛的报名表。\
It's the registration form for the Uluru London Qualifiers.

**笃笃骨**：……哈……

**笃笃骨**：……哈哈……\
**Willow**: *panting*

握着报名表的手开始缓缓颤抖起来，慢慢地，颤抖蔓延至全身。\
Her hands, clutching the form, begin to tremble. Before long, the tremors have engulfed her entire body.

**笃笃骨**：……完好，无损。\
**Willow**: Still intact.

**笃笃骨**：……哈哈哈哈哈……\
**Willow**: Hahahahaha.

**笃笃骨**：完好——无损。\
**Willow**: Still ... intact.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

已经换上训练服的卡洛琳，站在运动场地中心。她正用脚尖一点点感受着灼热的赛场大地下汩汩涨起的脉搏。\
Caroline stands at the center of the sports field in her training gear, feeling the fiery pulse of the ground beneath her feet.

**纸信圈儿**：——嘿。\
**Flutterpage**: Hey.

**卡洛琳**：——？\
**Caroline Bartley**: Hmm?

**纸信圈儿**：总算让我找着您了。\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Bartley! I finally found you!

**卡洛琳**：是你吗，纸信圈儿？这风大得我有点睁不开眼睛……让我看看你在哪儿……\
**Caroline Bartley**: F-Flutterpage? Is that you? I can hardly open my eyes in all this wind. Where, where are you?

**纸信圈儿**：我来了——\
**Flutterpage**: I'm right here!

风渐平息下来，小女孩匆忙落地，差点跌了个跟头。\
The wind subsides as Flutterpage makes a hurried landing, nearly losing her balance.

**卡洛琳**：你……你是专门来找我的？\
**Caroline Bartley**: You've been looking for me, have you? How did you find me?

**纸信圈儿**：我知道小姐在伦敦的旅馆，但是敲了半天门也没人应，还是租房的艾丽卡婆婆告诉我，能在运动场找到您。\
**Flutterpage**: I knew where you were stayin' in London, but you wasn't there when I arrived. Then, the landlady, Erika, told me to try the trainin' field. Looks like she was right.

**卡洛琳**：是的，我每天都会在这儿练习，这样能更方便我熟悉场地。\
**Caroline Bartley**: She was. I've been training here every day. You know, to settle in before the event.

**纸信圈儿**：那好——我这里有一封紧急的、秘密的、重大的信件，要递交到您的手里……还请查收。\
**Flutterpage**: Good luck, then. Actually, I've come here to deliver a very important and urgent letter to you. Here.

**卡洛琳**：……挑战书？\
**Caroline Bartley**: "A Letter of Challenge"?

上面歪歪扭扭的几个大字，耀武扬威地宣誓着这封信件的骄傲。\
The bold, crooked letters scrawled across the top proudly proclaim the letter's importance.

**纸信圈儿**：我，现在正式代夏洛特·奥黑根小姐向巴特利家的卡洛琳女士发起挑战。\
**Flutterpage**: "I, Liberti Grove, on behalf of Charlotte O'Hagan, hereby challenge Caroline Bartley to see who'll become the champion of the Floor Ritual in the Uluru Games."

**纸信圈儿**：不论你是种子选手、很多很多比赛的冠军，还是什么众人追捧的太阳……\
**Flutterpage**: "No matter if you're a seeded player, a champion, or the sun you say you are ..."

**纸信圈儿**：作为世界上唯一一个掌握了自由式转体720度超高难度空中抛接术杖技术的运动员，夏洛特·奥黑根——\
**Flutterpage**: "Charlotte O'Hagan, the only Floor Ritualist to master the two-and-a-half turn with free leg backwards and upwards, wand throw and catch ..."

**纸信圈儿**：必将在即将举办的乌卢鲁伦敦预选赛中拔得头筹，一举打败你。\
**Flutterpage**: "... will defeat you and win first place in the London Qualifiers!"

**卡洛琳**：……什……？\
**Caroline Bartley**: What?

**卡洛琳**：……你是说……\
**Caroline Bartley**: You mean ...

## LD-11 叮叮当当！ / Clang! Clang!

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：让一让，让一让！我帮福葛先生找到了他用于组装过滤器的最佳工具——\
**Freddy the Rascal**: Outta the way, outta the way! I've found the perfect component for Mr. Fog's machine!

男孩的声音穿梭在忙碌拥挤的街巷里，钻过雾气中蓝黑色的小软毡帽，他的声音最终落脚于街角广场的人群里。\
The boy darts through the bustling alley, slipping between the hats in the smog, and landing among the crowd at the corner of the square.

人群围绕着有半身大的机器，每个人都在交头接耳。\
The machine, about half the size of a person, is at the center of everyone's attention. The crowd members whisper to each other in excited tones.

**福葛先生**：——通过这一步，我们能初步评估空气中的微量分子含量……\
**Mr. Fog**: This allows us to analyze the composition of the atmosphere.

人群中冒出一个脑袋，他衣着挺拔，声音洪亮。\
He lifts his head above the crowd, his voice cutting through the chatter.

**福葛先生**：当微粒沉积计量仪上的滤纸达到校定标准的色值时，会被它认定为微粒超标……届时它会自动启动……\
**Mr. Fog**: If the color of the filter paper meets that of the pollution standard, it will determine that the air is polluted and start working automatically.

**福葛先生**：让我来演示一下。\
**Mr. Fog**: Let me show you.

人们的脑袋凑在一起，兴奋而好奇地盯着福葛先生手中的计量仪。\
Heads turn as the crowd stares intently at the measuring tool in Mr. Fog's hands.

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：让一让！嘿，福葛先生！您瞧，我找到了一个玻璃丝塞子，这不就是您说的最佳材料吗？\
**Freddy the Rascal**: Scuse me! Oi, Mr. Fog, look, I found a glass stopper! It's the one you were lookin' for, right?

一个灰发男孩手里攥着一枚塞子，积极地挤到福葛先生身边。\
Stopper in hand, Freddy eagerly pushes through the crowd toward Mr. Fog.

**福葛先生**：噢！没错！你找到了！\
**Mr. Fog**: Oh, you found it! Yes, that's exactly what I need!

福葛先生接下塞子。\
He gratefully takes the stopper.

**福葛先生**：大家请看！这就是这枚机器运作的核心之一，它能够将我们刚才评估出来的微粒过滤成洁净的空气……当然，它只是其中一个因素。\
**Mr. Fog**: Your attention, please! This glass stopper is one of the core components of this machine, which can harness the power of the sun to purify the air. Of course, this is only one component of many.

**威尔**：说了这么多，大家也一起帮了这么多忙，可是我们连吸尘器的影子还没见着呢！\
**Will**: Are you done talkin'? We've given you everythin' you need. Where's our purification machine?

**街坊Ⅰ**：是啊，到底行不行啊！\
**Neighbor I**: Quite right! We need to see the purification machine!

人群中也开始有不满和质疑的声音。\
Discontent and suspicion start to surface among the crowd.

**福葛先生**：放宽心，放宽心，大家……要相信，我一定是咱们中最希望“伦敦煤烟污染勘察与清除大使MK.Ⅱ”能成功的——\
**Mr. Fog**: No need to worry, folks. Believe me. There is no one who wants this purification machine to work more than I. So, I've been doing some experiments.

**宽檐帽**：福葛伙计！\
**Brimley**: Arthur, mate!

**福葛先生**：——！来了！\
**Mr. Fog**: Here!

福葛先生眼神明亮地回头，人群随着福葛先生眼神的方向自觉让出一条路。\
Mr. Fog looks across the crowd, his eyes bright with intent, prompting the crowd to part a path along the line of his gaze.

在这条路的尽头，宽檐帽和牙仙，以及三个码头工人，拖着一个拖车，拖车上载着一台沉重的机器，向这边走来。\
Brimley, Tooth Fairy, and three dockworkers appear at the end of the path. They're hauling a cart carrying a heavy machine.

**宽檐帽**：福葛伙计，请原谅我没能为搬运这玩意儿出上一份力，作为一个“无手派游骑”，要我在这事儿上付出体力劳动实在是有些强人所难了。\
**Brimley**: Forgive me for not helping move it. I'm afraid I'm handless and horseless. I can't do a thing.

**威尔**：这是什么？看着像一个机械怪胎。\
**Will**: What in the bloody hell is that? Some kind of mechanical freak?

**福葛先生**：大家一起瞧瞧吧。受惠于同乡们的协助，我的驱雾实验有了新的结果。\
**Mr. Fog**: Not to worry, Brimley. Now, folks, take a look at this. Thanks to your generous donations, my experiments on smog removal have finally come to fruition.

**福葛先生**：——一台集测量和甄别、吸收和净化为一体的大功率雾气净化器。\
**Mr. Fog**: Introducing the London Air Pollution Auto-Detecting Purifier MK. II! A high-power, multifunctional, air-cleaning machine!

**福葛先生**：它暂时还只支持三小时不间断运作，但距离乌卢鲁预选赛还有一段时间，我们仍有机会对其进行改良，使它足以支撑一整天的乌卢鲁赛事。\
**Mr. Fog**: The current model can only operate for three hours at a time, but I'll continue to improve its performance before the qualifiers begin. It's estimated to last a whole day by then.

**街坊Ⅰ**：好啊！太好了——！！！\
**Neighbor I**: Wonderful! Simply wonderful!

人群爆发出一阵欢呼。\
A cheer erupts from the crowd.

**威尔**：咱们不用再惧怕顶在家门口的雾气耽误咱们的大事了！\
**Will**: No more smog standin' in our way!

**街坊Ⅰ**：好家伙，我有多久没见过清澈的空气和明媚的阳光了，我的骨头都要发霉了！\
**Neighbor I**: Goodness, I can't remember the last time I saw the sun and breathed fresh air. I feel as though I've been rotting!

在欢喜喧闹的人群中，宽檐帽瞥了一眼站在一旁，始终不发一言的牙仙。\
Amidst the raucous celebration, Brimley takes a moment to glance at Tooth Fairy, who is standing silently off to one side.

**宽檐帽**：本护卫能见到基金会医生小姐的一次微笑，也算是人生中一大幸事了。\
**Brimley**: It's an honor to see that sweet smile of yours, darl.

**牙仙**：可能是受到了某种鼓舞吧。特定的节日气氛，让外来者也感到被凝聚于此，同呼同吸，充满力量。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I think I'm inspired somehow. I've always felt like a bit of an outsider in London, but this festive atmosphere makes me feel a sense of belonging.

**宽檐帽**：在这一点上，我与您的心情是一样的。\
**Brimley**: I totally understand.

**宽檐帽**：我深知我的精神故乡在遥远的红土大陆，但能被另一片乡土所接纳，感其所感地雀跃欢欣，于我们这类外乡人而言，弥足珍贵。\
**Brimley**: Though I Awakened in London, my true home is the land down under, thousands of miles from here. In some ways, I'm an immigrant. This sense of belonging is a treasure.

昏昏欲睡的车厢里，无线电广播正在机械性地转播着各类实况。\
Inside the sleepy car, the radio broadcasts a variety of live updates.

**无线电广播**：是的，乌卢鲁预选赛在咱们这儿举办当然是咱们东区的骄傲，我的心早就迫不及待地飞向那一天了……\
**Radio Broadcast**: Yes, as an East London resident, my chest swelled with pride when I learned that the Uluru Qualifiers would be held here. I couldn't wait to see what would happen.

**基金会分部成员Ⅰ**：阿、阿嚏——！\
**Foundation Branch Member I**: A-Achoo!

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：……这已经是你此行的第九个喷嚏了。\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: That's your ninth sneeze since we got here.

**基金会分部成员Ⅰ**：我能有什么办法，乌卢鲁联合组委会对我申请留在澳洲总会场的信件置之不理，他们真的找不到其他人愿意在这么个天气里来到伦敦了。\
**Foundation Branch Member I**: Don't blame me! I didn't even wanna come! The Uluru Committee ignored my application to stay at the Australian headquarters. They couldn't find anyone willing to come to London with all this smog in the air.

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：他们有他们的考量，毕竟决定在伦敦举办预选赛也不是一天两天了，突然撤销对于前期的开支成本以及当下的所有规划都是一大损失。\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: They didn't have much choice, either, mate. The Foundation's been preparing for the qualifiers in London for ages. We'll suffer huge financial losses if it's canceled.

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：需要有人来实地探查现况并决定是否要继续烧钱举办预选赛，你只能反省一下自己为什么如此优秀地成为了这样一个幸运儿。\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: Someone has to make the trip to decide whether we should cut our losses or continue to throw money at it. You must've done something to be the lucky one who has to do the job.

**基金会分部成员Ⅰ**：——！！！\
**Foundation Branch Member I**: ...!

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：——我的老天……！\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: Holy ...!

汽车猛然刹停，车头的前杠下，一队煤灰魔精灰溜溜地跑了过去，待窸窣声消失后，车子再次发动了起来。\
The car screeches to a halt as a group of sooty critters scurry by the front bumper. As the shuffling subsides, the engine revs up again.

**司机**：不好意思，外来的官老爷们，最近街道上总是在泛滥着这些小怪物。\
**Driver**: I do apologize. These little monsters are all over the streets these days.

**基金会分部成员Ⅰ**：……哈，看来这种小事在这儿已经是习以为常了。\
**Foundation Branch Member I**: Haha, he sounds so calm. You'd think he was just talking about stray cats.

**基金会分部成员Ⅰ**：你有时候不得不佩服他们在面对雾气时的斯多葛主义精神，在我看来这样的环境根本不适宜进行任何室外活动。\
**Foundation Branch Member I**: You have to admire the stoicism of the Brits, especially in the face of all this. Honestly, this environment is totally unsuitable for any kind of outdoor activity.

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：……\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: ...

同僚一言不发，只是在本子上写着什么。\
The Foundation member says nothing, quietly jotting something down in a notebook.

**基金会分部成员Ⅰ**：……嘿，你在干嘛？\
**Foundation Branch Member I**: Hey, what are you doing?

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：记录一下刚才差点发生的交通事故。这些记录最终会被用作决定是否取消预选赛，至少我们之中得有人干点事而不是一味发牢骚，不是吗？\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: Making note of the crash that almost happened. *sigh* These records will be used to decide if the qualifiers should be canceled. Someone has to be the doer since we already have a whiner on the team, eh?

**基金会分部成员Ⅰ**：……\
**Foundation Branch Member I**: ...

侧目旁观着窗外的情景，面具底下的男人发出一声叹息。\
With a sidelong glance at the scenery beyond the window, the man under the mask exhales softly.

**基金会分部成员Ⅰ**：看这窗外，他们甚至在街上挂着彩带、贴着海报，准备迎接一场子虚乌有的、空想的运动会。\
**Foundation Branch Member I**: Look at all the decorations and posters. So much preparation for an event that won't even be held.

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：……这年头光是还有人在惦记着运动会，就已经够令人讶异的了。\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: I'm surprised they even wanna hold the qualifiers given the situation.

一阵清浅的沉默回荡在车厢里，与窗外的淡黄色薄雾一样模糊透亮。\
A gentle silence fills the car, its clarity as soft and blurred as the yellowish smog outside.

**基金会分部成员Ⅰ**：……行吧，咱们公事公办，快点结束这鬼任务。\
**Foundation Branch Member I**: Anyway, let's make it quick and get this job over with.

**基金会分部成员Ⅰ**：只要证明无法继续举办预选赛，并收集到那些报名参赛的神秘学家资料，咱们就能打道回府了吧？\
**Foundation Branch Member I**: Let me see. We need two things: evidence that proves the environment isn't suitable for holding the qualifiers, and the profiles of all the participating athletes. Then we can go home.

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：……\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: ...

**无线电广播**：让我们一起来看看十字街社区承包商是如何准备这次会场的改造与修建的吧……\
**Radio Broadcast**: Next, the changes made to Cross Street. Let's see what the local community has done to prepare for the upcoming event.

正在开车的司机，颤抖地抬起手，将无线电广播的声音，调至了最小。\
The driver reaches a trembling hand to the radio and quietly turns the volume knob to its minimum.

纷繁的街道上，人们正围着福葛先生与他半身大的雾气净化器，经过再次改良，它的性能已经比之前提高了不少。\
On the busy street, a crowd gathers around Mr. Fog and his purification machine. After some further iteration, its performance has greatly improved.

机器旁，原本写着“伦敦煤烟污染勘察与清除大使MK.Ⅱ”的标志牌，现在已经加上了一笔，变成了“伦敦煤烟污染勘察与清除大使MK.Ⅲ”。\
Beside the device, the sign originally reading "London Air Pollution Auto-Detecting Purifier MK. II" now reads "MK. III" thanks to a single additional brushstroke.

**众人**：三——！！\
**Crowd**: Three!

**众人**：二——！！\
**Crowd**: Two!

**众人**：一——！！\
**Crowd**: One!

**福葛先生**：启动。\
**Mr. Fog**: Start!

福葛先生按下机器的红色按钮。\
He pushes the red button on the machine.

由不同生活用品拼凑而成的机器，其玻璃器皿中塞着一个纯金属的机械肺净化仪。“轰隆隆隆”，它此时正在抖动着。\
The contraption, pieced together from household goods, has a glass container housing a solid metal mechanical lung purifier. It comes to life with a deep rumble.

紧接着，空中的黄色薄雾慢慢被其巨大的吸纳口吸入。\
Bit by bit, the yellow smog hanging in the air is inhaled by its gaping vent.

**众人**：……噢……！喔喔喔——！\
**Crowd**: Wow!

人们惊异地望着这一奇观，望着自己身处的周遭世界开始慢慢清明。\
Eyes wide with wonder, the people watch as the world around them gradually turns clearer.

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：爸爸！你看，那是天上的云彩吗？它们就像被子里的棉絮一样厚重洁白！\
**Freddy the Rascal**: Wow! Look, Dad! Are those clouds in the sky? They're so white and fluffy!

**威尔**：——我现在终于能够理解，为什么有人说清洁的空气就如同清洁的水资源一样珍贵了。\
**Will**: The air's so fresh. I've never felt anythin' like it!

**街坊Ⅰ**：嘿！我甚至能看到五十米开外的基顿闹腾商店！——嗨！嗨！瞧，我和基顿小子还打上招呼了！\
**Neighbor I**: Hey! I can even see Keaton's store fifty yards from here! Hellooo! See, Keaton's waving back!

人们欢闹起来。\
A wave of joy ripples through the crowd as they erupt into excited conversation.

牙仙却看到福葛先生呆呆站在原地，仰着头，不知在思考什么。\
Tooth Fairy watches Mr. Fog. He's staring upward. There is no celebration from him, only a quiet contemplation.

**牙仙**：一周时间用来思考，一周时间用来执行，一周时间用来验收结果和办理手续。\
**Tooth Fairy**: The first week is for planning, the second for execution, and the last for delivery and paperwork.

**牙仙**：看来你的计划已经确凿无误地落地了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Looks like you've completed the tasks as scheduled.

**牙仙**：松了一口气吗？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Are you relieved?

福葛先生仍然仰望着蓝天。\
Mr. Fog stands there, still staring at the blue sky above.

**福葛先生**：……\
**Mr. Fog**: ...

**福葛先生**：……牙仙女士，原来阳光是金黄色的。\
**Mr. Fog**: Ms. Tooth Fairy, the sun is so golden and warm.

**宽檐帽**：牙仙女士，您别搭理我的伙计，他最近忙晕了头，说话做事呆头呆脑的。我想我们只需要理解他是想要表达喜悦，这就得了。\
**Brimley**: Don't mind him. He's all over the place after working non-stop for the last few weeks. He's just trying to say he's happy, that's all.

**牙仙**：你不觉得高兴吗？\
**Tooth Fairy**: What about you? How do you feel?

**宽檐帽**：我？我敢说，住在这顶帽子里的自由游骑之魂，早就想在这片阳光地上策马奔腾呢！\
**Brimley**: Me? The ranger's soul inside me has always wanted to gallop beneath the blazing sun!

**宽檐帽**：——咿嗬！\
**Brimley**: Yahooo!

说罢，宽檐帽蓄力冲出一米远，快乐地荡行在每个人的头顶。\
Brimley charges forward, gliding merrily above the heads of those around him.

牙仙微笑地看着这一切，但很快，她的眼角捕捉到了什么东西。\
Tooth Fairy watches with a gentle smile. Then, something catches the corner of her eye.

**牙仙**：……？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Huh?

**牙仙**：魔精——？\
**Tooth Fairy**: A critter?

**牙仙**：不……是……黑雾？\
**Tooth Fairy**: No. Is that ... the black fog?

**牙仙**：在这个时候——？\
**Tooth Fairy**: What's it doing here?

她尝试跟随自己所感应到的神秘学气息，往角落里挪动了几步。\
Guided by the traces of arcane energy, she takes a few steps over to the corner.

隐隐约约的，但猝然而至。眼前似乎出现了一层黑纱，却又瞬间消失不见。\
A faint, shadowy haze momentarily clouds her vision, vanishing just as suddenly as it came.

**牙仙**：这和我的猜想不一样……我以为雾最浓的时候才会看到黑雾的身影，但现在——\
**Tooth Fairy**: I thought the black fog was a result of the increased density of regular smog in the air, but it seems I was wrong.

**牙仙**：明明福葛先生的吸尘器已经吹散了方圆几米的雾气，可是那股黑雾的气息却依然存在，甚至更浓。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Mr. Fog's machine has cleaned up the smog around us, but the black fog's still here, and it's getting thicker. How curious.

**牙仙**：好消息是，由于浓雾散去，它的气息更清晰且指向性更强了——\
**Tooth Fairy**: At least now, without the smog covering its trail, I can sense its movements more clearly.

跟随着敏锐感知的指引，牙仙悄悄远离了欢庆的众人，挤进了一条少有人发现的小巷。\
Following her keen senses, Tooth Fairy silently slips into a narrow alleyway.

暗黄色薄雾一下子又涌了上来，呛进牙仙的鼻腔里。\
Her nostrils sting as she enters the trail of the black fog.

**牙仙**：——咳咳、咳咳咳咳！\
**Tooth Fairy**: *cough*

她一边用手挥开遮挡着视线的浓雾，一边继续追踪着诡谲的气息前进。\
Doing her best to wave it off with her hand, she continues to follow the trail of the enigmatic presence.

在巷子深处的拐角，似乎有什么黑色的小东西正在颤抖。\
Something tiny and black seems to shudder in a corner deep within the alley.

**牙仙**：那里……那是什么？\
**Tooth Fairy**: What? What's that?

**？？？**：——！！！\
**???**: ...!

那黑色的小团警觉地跳动了起来，一瞬间窜出了牙仙的视野。\
The black creature springs into motion, vanishing from her sight in the blink of an eye.

**牙仙**：嗯？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Hmm?

但眼下似乎不是关注那个小黑团的好时候。\
Now doesn't feel like the time to focus on that little dark lump.

**牙仙**：……这雾又围上来了……\
**Tooth Fairy**: The smog's back.

与雾一同围上来的，还有一些不速之客。\
The smog rolls back in, but this time it has taken on a thick, blackened quality, and it's accompanied by a handful of unexpected intruders.

**牙仙**：好吧……我记得有人提醒过我，在十字街，越是狭窄且人迹罕至的巷子，就越有可能成为这些小可爱肆意聚集的地方。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I did hear that these little things tend to gather in the quiet alleys of Cross Street. Perhaps they'd like a visit from the toothfairies.

**牙仙**：我就知道……\
**Tooth Fairy**: Slipped away at the first opportunity.

看着面前暗黄色的沉雾，牙仙已经寻不到任何一丝刚才那只诡异魔精的线索了。\
She can't make out where they went through the thickness of the smog.

**牙仙**：被它给溜了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I knew it.

有些疲态的医生小姐理了理自己的头发。\
Slightly fatigued, she pauses to tidy up her hair.

**牙仙**：但，那到底是什么呢……\
**Tooth Fairy**: But what exactly was it?

## LD-12 老木头 / Old Wood

**纸信圈儿**：嘟嘟、嘟嘟～谁能为这个世界带来好处？艺术、道德还是小叫醒工？\
**Flutterpage**: Knock, knock! Which would make the world a better place, art or a heart of gold? Ha-ha! Neither! The little knocker-upper, Flutterpage, will!

纸信圈儿敲了敲笃笃骨后花园的门，没有声响。\
Flutterpage knocks on Willow's back door, but she receives no answer.

**纸信圈儿**：……咦？今天的笃笃骨还没开始练习吗？放在往常应该已经开始做准备活动了。\
**Flutterpage**: Hmm? Where's Ms. Willow? She should be warmin' up by now.

纸信圈儿绕了笃笃骨的房子一小圈。\
She walks a short loop around the perimeter of the house.

**纸信圈儿**：难道不在家吗？——笃笃骨！笃笃骨！\
**Flutterpage**: Where's she gone? Ms. Willow! Ms. Wiiillooow!

没有人回应。\
Silence.

**纸信圈儿**：嘟嘟、嘟嘟～不要轻易下定论，贫瘠或富贵，面包总管会告诉你。\
**Flutterpage**: Knock, knock! Don't jump to conclusions. Mr. Wind will tell you the truth.

纸信圈儿借助风力将自己轻轻抬起，晃晃悠悠荡进笃笃骨家。\
A gust of wind picks Flutterpage up, raising her high in the air. She sways as she glides in through an open window.

**纸信圈儿**：嘟嘟、嘟嘟～敲开了窗户还有门、敲开了宝箱还有锁……笃笃骨～笃笃骨……笃笃……？\
**Flutterpage**: Knock, knock! I'll open all the windows and doors, and all the treasure chests, too. Ms. Willow! Ms. Willow?

**纸信圈儿**：笃笃骨——？你在干什么？\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Willow! What you doin' over there?

黑暗的角落里，笃笃骨正面对着一个奇怪的物品，无声而立。她感觉到了纸信圈儿，但并未扭头。\
In a dark corner, Willow stands silently before a peculiar object. She senses Flutterpage but doesn't turn her head.

**笃笃骨**：呵，你今天来得可真早，像你这种小屁孩儿就是耐不住性子。\
**Willow**: You're early. Why am I not surprised? You're about as patient as a dog waiting for his dinner.

**纸信圈儿**：原来你已经醒了，我还以为你一起来就会开始练习来着——咦，你坐在黑暗里干什么？\
**Flutterpage**: I thought you'd start practicin' as soon as you woke up. What you doin' in this corner?

笃笃骨将手轻轻置于那怪物之上。\
Willow softly rests her hand upon the item before her.

**笃笃骨**：来，帮我看看，它还能不能用。\
**Willow**: Come take a look at this. I wonder if it still works.

那怪里怪气的物品，沉默着。\
The peculiar item sits still.

**纸信圈儿**：呜哇……好怪的玩意儿，这是什么？\
**Flutterpage**: Hmm. What a strange thing! What is it?

**笃笃骨**：这叫“迪吉里木”。算是一种乐器吧——来，你把手放上去试试。\
**Willow**: It's a sort of instrument called the didgeriwood. Come give it a try. First, put your hand on it like this.

纸信圈儿也学着笃笃骨的样子将手放在“迪吉里木”上。\
Flutterpage, imitating Willow, lays her hand on the didgeriwood.

**纸信圈儿**：然后呢？\
**Flutterpage**: Okay. Then what?

**笃笃骨**：我教你。\
**Willow**: I'll teach you how to play it.

**纸信圈儿**：好听，雨落在角豆树。\
**Flutterpage**: It's beautiful, like raindrops patterin' on tree leaves.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

笃笃骨将纸信圈儿的手轻轻挪开，再一次将自己的手放上去。\
Willow gently puts Flutterpage's hand aside before resting her own hand on it again.

**纸信圈儿**：……咦，它不出声了？\
**Flutterpage**: Hmm? Why's it gone quiet all of a sudden?

**笃笃骨**：它坏了。\
**Willow**: It's broken.

**纸信圈儿**：我弄坏了？\
**Flutterpage**: What?! I didn't break it, did I?

**笃笃骨**：不……本来就有些毛病了。\
**Willow**: No. It's been broken for a long time.

**纸信圈儿**：它确实像是已经放了好久的样子，这些边角都发霉了。\
**Flutterpage**: Well, judgin' by the look of it, it must be old. It's got mildew all over.

**笃笃骨**：它是自由祭祀项目必不可少的助乐，与神秘学家的神秘术呼应和鸣，而运动员们根据它的曲调翩然起舞。\
**Willow**: This instrument is crucial to every Floor Ritualist. You see, we're not just dancers but music makers, using our arcane skills to play the didgeriwood while we dance.

**笃笃骨**：哈……\
**Willow**: *sigh*

**纸信圈儿**：这件事我知道，坏了的东西总是不那么容易修好的。首先，咱们可得好好擦一擦灰尘，给它来一个大清洁……\
**Flutterpage**: Don't worry, Ms. Willow. I know broken things ain't always easy to fix, but we can start with the easy part. Why don't we wipe off the dust first?

纸信圈儿随手拾起一旁的纸，想要去擦拭“迪吉里木”上的灰尘。\
Flutterpage picks up a loose piece of paper and moves to wipe the dust from the didgeriwood.

**纸信圈儿**：咦？这是……\
**Flutterpage**: Huh? Is this ...

**纸信圈儿**：预选赛的报名表吗？\
**Flutterpage**: The athlete registration form for the qualifiers?

**笃笃骨**：呃……\
**Willow**: Um ...

**纸信圈儿**：噢——\
**Flutterpage**: Oh!

小女孩的头发向不同地方翘起，她眨了眨眼睛，顿了一下，似乎在思考什么。\
The girl blinks, her hair jutting out in every direction. She pauses for a moment as she slowly reads the paper.

**纸信圈儿**：你被我发现了一个秘密——你还没有报名。\
**Flutterpage**: And look! You ain't submitted it.

**纸信圈儿**：可是……为什么呢？\
**Flutterpage**: Why not?

**笃笃骨**：截止日期，不是还没到吗……\
**Willow**: There's still time, isn't there?

**纸信圈儿**：——已经到了呀。\
**Flutterpage**: No! You already missed the window!

**纸信圈儿**：如果还没报名的话，我认为我们要赶紧去报名……找福葛先生，他说过今天会有两个负责乌卢鲁赛事的人从澳洲本部赶来，我们还可以去找他们——\
**Flutterpage**: Blimey, we've got to do somethin' about this! Hmm. Oh! That's right! Mr. Fog said that two officers from the Australian headquarters would arrive in London today. I think we can ask them to pull the ... What was the word?

但笃笃骨并没有反应。\
Willow doesn't respond.

**纸信圈儿**：——来吧，我们的确需要挪一挪身子——！\
**Flutterpage**: Anyway, we need to get a move on! I'll pull you up.

纸信圈儿拼命拽着笃笃骨。但笃笃骨却始终用顽力相抗，二人就这样僵持着。\
Flutterpage tugs desperately at Willow, who steadfastly holds her ground, leaving them at an impasse.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

**笃笃骨**：纸信圈儿……\
**Willow**: Flutterpage ...

**笃笃骨**：要不还是，算了吧。\
**Willow**: Maybe it's time to give up.

纸信圈儿愣了一下。\
Flutterpage turns her head.

**纸信圈儿**：算了？\
**Flutterpage**: Give up?

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

**纸信圈儿**：你说“算了”，是什么意思？\
**Flutterpage**: What do you mean, "give up"?

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

**纸信圈儿**：我不明白……\
**Flutterpage**: I don't understand.

**纸信圈儿**：那不是乌卢鲁运动会吗……？\
**Flutterpage**: Ain't this the Uluru Games we've been talkin' about for ages?

**纸信圈儿**：你……练习了这么久，每天都像妈妈的鸡毛掸子一样在空中飞上飞下……\
**Flutterpage**: Think of all the effort you've made. You didn't jump up and down in the garden over and over again to dust it, did you? You're an athlete, not a feather duster!

**纸信圈儿**：你还、还做出了那个动作……！对，那个……叫什么来着……\
