**Flutterpage**: A-And you finished that move! The, you know, the um ...

**笃笃骨**：自由式转体720度超高难度空中抛接术杖。\
**Willow**: The two-and-a-half turn with free leg backwards and upwards, wand throw and catch.

**纸信圈儿**：对！对，就是这个！\
**Flutterpage**: Yeah! That one!

**纸信圈儿**：……怎么会“算了”呢——？\
**Flutterpage**: See? How can you just "give up"?

**笃笃骨**：你……别这样瞪着我。\
**Willow**: Oh, please, don't look at me like that.

**笃笃骨**：相信我，这是我曾经做梦都想完成的动作。\
**Willow**: Yes, I've always dreamt of completing this element.

**笃笃骨**：能将这个动作做出来到底意味着什么，没有人比我更清楚。\
**Willow**: No one knows better than I how much this means to me.

**纸信圈儿**：是啊！那为什么……\
**Flutterpage**: Then, why are you ...?

**笃笃骨**：……别说了。\
**Willow**: I don't want to talk about it.

笃笃骨低下头。\
Willow lowers her head.

**笃笃骨**：我还得继续修理这架“迪吉里木”，走的时候把房门带上。\
**Willow**: You should leave. I need to see what I can do to fix the didgeriwood. Don't forget to close the door behind you.

纸信圈儿愣愣地看着笃笃骨半天，而后她突然嘟着嘴生气地蹲了下来。\
Flutterpage stands frozen, staring at Willow for what feels like forever, before pouting angrily and crouching down, her arms firmly crossed.

**纸信圈儿**：我不走。\
**Flutterpage**: I ain't leavin'.

**纸信圈儿**：我生气了。\
**Flutterpage**: I'm angry.

**笃笃骨**：唉……\
**Willow**: *sigh*

笃笃骨不知说什么好，只能让气氛凝滞在此。\
Unsure of what to say, Willow lets the moment hang awkwardly in the air.

二人就这样，一蹲一立，等待着老壁钟里的时间一秒秒走过，墙上的爱尔兰风景画一声不响地盯着她们。\
Beneath the painting of the Irish countryside, one stands and the other squats, the grandfather clock marking each passing second with its steady tick.

半晌，笃笃骨用手指戳了戳蹲在地上的纸信圈儿。\
Eventually, Willow lightly taps Flutterpage on the head with her finger.

**笃笃骨**：别生气了，这是我自己的事。\
**Willow**: Don't be upset. It's not that serious.

纸信圈儿并没有看笃笃骨，她用力摇了摇头。\
Flutterpage continues to stare at the floor, shaking her head forcefully.

**纸信圈儿**：我……我昨天还去找卡洛琳了——\
**Flutterpage**: I ... I talked to Ms. Bartley yesterday.

**笃笃骨**：……你是说……？\
**Willow**: You didn't ...

纸信圈儿站起来。\
Flutterpage stands up.

**纸信圈儿**：对，我代你向她发起了挑战。\
**Flutterpage**: Yeah, I challenged her on your behalf with a letter.

**笃笃骨**：——！\
**Willow**: ...!

**笃笃骨**：她无非是带着她的一号种子头衔来挑衅罢了，想看我笑话的不只她一个。\
**Willow**: She only visited me so she could show off all the titles she's won. She's not the first to come just to laugh in my face.

**纸信圈儿**：——不是的。\
**Flutterpage**: That ain't true.

**纸信圈儿**：卡洛琳很开心。\
**Flutterpage**: Caroline was happy when she got the letter.

**笃笃骨**：——你说什么？\
**Willow**: What?

**纸信圈儿**：她听说你接受了她的挑战，她很开心。她还和我讲了很多你们以前的小故事……\
**Flutterpage**: She was really lookin' forward to competin' against you. She told me why, too.

**纸信圈儿**：她说你一直是她们中最努力，也是天分最高的那一个，光是仰望你就已经足够令人脱力。\
**Flutterpage**: She said you were the most talented and hard workin' player she'd ever seen, and that it took all her effort just to keep you in her sight, let alone catch up with you.

**纸信圈儿**：因为你是不一样的，你是特别的。如果世界只有一枚桂冠，那么所有人都会甘心等待你将其摘下。\
**Flutterpage**: Because you're different, the one true master of the art. If there were only one gold medal in the history of the Floor Ritual, it'd be meant for you.

**纸信圈儿**：她是这么说的。\
**Flutterpage**: Those were her exact words.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

她花费了近一分钟的时间让自己从回忆中脱离，但很显然，她的内心仍旧被过去扯动着。\
She wrestles with her memories, yet the emotional pull of the past remains palpable.

**笃笃骨**：……一开始……\
**Willow**: I only chose to become a Floor Ritualist ...

**笃笃骨**：我们都以为我们是最天赋异禀的人，和其他所有孩子都不一样。\
**Willow**: Because I had a talent for it. I wanted to win.

**笃笃骨**：然后我们练习、练习，把一切与它无关的事都排除在外。\
**Willow**: So I practiced and practiced, paying little attention to anything else.

**笃笃骨**：所有的朋友、亲人，甚至是——一块小小的起司蛋糕。\
**Willow**: My family, my friends, my life, none of it mattered more than victory.

**笃笃骨**：成功有成瘾性。\
**Willow**: To me, there was no reward more alluring than the euphoria of winning.

**笃笃骨**：一个成功的冠军，每当他回望过去，每一个动作、每一次空中的暂停和跃起、每一次裁判的哨声与众人的欢呼，他所能看到的，都是他离满盘皆输究竟有多么近。\
**Willow**: But whenever I looked back at my past glories, I felt no happiness or excitement. Instead, I'd replay every moment in my mind, every lost point, every imperfect movement, and think about how close I was to failure.

**笃笃骨**：而他只能寄希望于下一次，至少下一次，他的奖牌应是更加完美的。任何一个小数点所带来的扣分都不能出现。\
**Willow**: So I pursued the next victory even more fervently. I thought, "Next time, I won't lose a single point. Next time, I'll be perfect."

**笃笃骨**：这就是我在贝尔丹火焰节表演赛的冠军席上所想的事情。\
**Willow**: That was what was running through my mind when I was crowned champion of the Beltane.

**笃笃骨**：可那之后，再也没有下一次。\
**Willow**: But there was no next time.

**笃笃骨**：那是我的最后一场比赛。\
**Willow**: That was my last competition.

**纸信圈儿**：……\
**Flutterpage**: ...

**纸信圈儿**：但是你可以、可以站起来，你可以继续跳，你可以有下一次的。\
**Flutterpage**: But you can still have a next time. You can still try again. Look at you! Your skills haven't dulled a bit!

**笃笃骨**：但我想要为之赢得荣誉的人……还有家乡，都已经离我太远了。\
**Willow**: What's the point? I've pushed away everyone I wanted to honor with my victories. I've strayed too far from home.

**笃笃骨**：况且……呵……\
**Willow**: Not to mention ... *sigh*

她看了一眼自己的腿，没有出声。\
She casts a silent glance at her leg.

**纸信圈儿**：可是……你自己快乐吗……？\
**Flutterpage**: Okay, but are you happy when you do the Floor Ritual?

**笃笃骨**：……快乐？\
**Willow**: Am I happy?

**纸信圈儿**：你瞧，我喜欢做小叫醒工。每天早上，会看到各式各样的睡姿，他们有抱在一起睡的，有睡得东倒西歪的，还有把自己裹成一团紧紧贴着墙壁的。\
**Flutterpage**: See, I love bein' a knocker-upper. Every mornin', I get to see all kinds of sleepin' positions: some people cuddle, others curl up in a ball, and some ain't even in bed at all.

**纸信圈儿**：然后我喜欢看到他们慢慢苏醒的样子，他们会从一个没有意识的状态慢慢变回他们自身。\
**Flutterpage**: I like watchin' them wake up, too. Like newborn kittens learnin' to crawl, hehe!

**纸信圈儿**：就像动物、或者植物，没有什么可商量的，他们会睁开眼，然后开始动起来。\
**Flutterpage**: And finally, when they completely open their eyes and stand on their feet, I feel a gust of fresh wind rushin' out the window.

**纸信圈儿**：我会感到快乐。\
**Flutterpage**: It makes me happy.

**纸信圈儿**：——你呢？运动会让你快乐吗？\
**Flutterpage**: So, what about you? Does the Floor Ritual make you happy?

**笃笃骨**：我……\
**Willow**: I ...

**笃笃骨**：我不知道……\
**Willow**: I don't know.

**笃笃骨**：现在回想起来，我只会想起，每次比赛结束之后，妈妈都会带我去一家老爱尔兰人开的蛋糕铺子，买一个最普通的盒装起司蛋糕。\
**Willow**: The only thing that comes to mind is that, after a game, my mam would take me to the old cake shop down the road and buy me a cheesecake. The same one every time.

**笃笃骨**：只有那个时候，吃起司蛋糕是被允许的。\
**Willow**: That was the only time I'd allow myself to eat dessert.

**纸信圈儿**：嗯……\
**Flutterpage**: Mhm.

**笃笃骨**：我还记得妈妈最爱买的味道，树莓可可……甜甜酸酸的，还有一股巧克力的浓密滋味……\
**Willow**: It had raspberries and chocolate drizzled on top. I can still remember the taste, sweet and tart, with a light bitterness.

**纸信圈儿**：噢～\
**Flutterpage**: Ooooh.

**纸信圈儿**：我明白了。你喜欢的是比赛结束之后的起司蛋糕，那个会让你感到快乐。\
**Flutterpage**: So what really makes you happy is the cheesecake after the game!

**笃笃骨**：——嗯？\
**Willow**: What?

**纸信圈儿**：我知道了，我们还是得去报名比赛，因为这样你才能吃到“比赛结束后的起司蛋糕”。\
**Flutterpage**: Right, then let's get you registered for the qualifiers so you can have that post-game celebration cheesecake again!

**笃笃骨**：——等等，什么……？\
**Willow**: What are you ...?

**纸信圈儿**：咱们去找福葛先生，他一定有办法让你参加预选赛的。而且咱们还有基金会的大人物牙仙女士，她可是总部调来的好医生……\
**Flutterpage**: Let's go talk to Mr. Fog. I'm sure he can find a way to get you into the qualifiers. And if your leg's causin' you trouble or anythin', Ms. Tooth Fairy can help you out. She is a doctor from the Foundation, after all.

**笃笃骨**：……等，等一下……\
**Willow**: W-Wait!

一阵小小的风吻过，她的腿却似乎没有刚才那么顽强的意志，竟真的被纸信圈儿带着跑起来。\
A delicate wind brushes past, causing her legs to lose their earlier stubbornness and follow Flutterpage out of the house.

**纸信圈儿**：你不想吃起司蛋糕吗？\
**Flutterpage**: Hmm? Don't you want to eat that cheesecake?

她们穿过描绘爱尔兰乡村景色的古旧油画。\
They walk beside the paintings of Ireland.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

她们穿过柳条扎成的火炬和奇奇怪怪的罐子。\
They wind their way through the willow-bound torches and mysterious vessels.

**纸信圈儿**：你不觉得那个蛋糕会让你快乐吗？\
**Flutterpage**: Don't you think it'll make you happy?

她们穿过屋子的大门。\
They pass through the house's front door.

**笃笃骨**：起司……蛋糕……\
**Willow**: That cheesecake ...

她们向屋外一跃而出。\
And leap out of the house.

**纸信圈儿**：那就去吧——去做让自己快乐的事，不就好了吗？\
**Flutterpage**: It will, right? Then let's go get it! Life's all about happiness, ain't it?

外界的空气一股脑闯进笃笃骨的鼻腔，她与世界撞了个满怀。\
A surge of fresh air floods Willow's nostrils, hitting her like a full-on collision with the outside world.

垂下视线，她看到那个浮在半空中个头矮小的小姑娘，一缕软软的发丝向后飘摇。\
Lowering her gaze, she catches sight of Flutterpage hovering in the air, a delicate lock of hair swaying in the breeze.

**笃笃骨**：一个……很笨的，小知了。\
**Willow**: You silly little Buzzie.

一只还没有被纸信圈儿拽疼的手，去轻轻拨动了一下那缕软软的头发。\
Using a hand spared from Flutterpage's tugging, Willow softly flicks at the silky strand of hair.

**纸信圈儿**：……咦，怎么这么多人正从会场的方向往家里走呀……？\
**Flutterpage**: Hmm? Why's everyone leavin' the stadium?

纸信圈儿拽着笃笃骨向着会场的方向跑去，却发现许多垂头丧气的居民正迎着她们往回走。\
Flutterpage is still tugging Willow in the direction of the venue, but there seem to be more and more despondent people going in the other direction.

**纸信圈儿**：嘿！——你们跑那么快，往哪儿去呢？！\
**Flutterpage**: Oi! Where you all goin'?

**威尔**：——回家。\
**Will**: Home.

**纸信圈儿**：回家？你们不去运动会会场吗？福葛先生正在那边举办驱雾仪式呢！\
**Flutterpage**: Home? Why? Mr. Fog's holdin' the ribbon-cuttin' ceremony for his machine in the stadium. Why ain't you goin' there?

**威尔**：——别去了。\
**Will**: It ain't happenin'.

**纸信圈儿**：你说什么？\
**Flutterpage**: Pardon?

**威尔**：我说，别去了——！运动会开不成了！\
**Will**: I said it ain't happenin'! The ceremony!

**威尔**：基金会的人来了，宣布乌卢鲁运动会在咱们这儿的预选赛取消了。\
**Will**: The Foundation officers canceled the qualifiers.

**威尔**：——福葛先生那台号称史上最大的吸尘器，失败了。\
**Will**: Mr. Fog's so-called "biggest air purifier ever" doesn't work.

## LD-13 剪彩仪式 / Ribbon-Cutting Ceremony

一个小时前。\
One hour earlier.

**巡逻警察Ⅰ**：请大家稍微注意一点纪律，有序地参与、参观，有序地庆祝这次雾气净化器的剪彩仪式——\
**Police Constable I**: Please enter in an orderly manner, everyone. The ceremony will begin shortly.

机器旁，原本写着“伦敦煤烟污染勘察与清除大使MK.Ⅱ”的标志牌，现在已经加上了一笔，变成了“伦敦煤烟污染勘察与清除大使MK.Ⅲ”。\
Beside the device, the sign originally reading "London Air Pollution Auto-Detecting Purifier MK. II" now reads "MK. III" thanks to a single additional brushstroke.

**威尔**：弗洛狄，你能看到福葛先生吗？这些人头挡着我的视线，我怎么踮脚尖都看不清楚。\
**Will**: Freddy, can you see Mr. Fog? I can't see a thing past all these people.

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：爸爸，你不是带了望远镜嘛？把它递给我，我能帮你看。\
**Freddy the Rascal**: You brought the telescope, didn't you, Dad? Maybe I can see if I look through it.

**威尔**：来，给你——在爸爸肩膀上可得坐稳了啊。好家伙，整个帝国最“有见识”的人都挤来了似的。\
**Will**: Good idea. Here, take the telescope and get on my shoulders. Hold on tight, you hear? This crowd's rabid. All this pushin' and shovin' just to take a look at a machine!

**威尔**：我猜他们上次亲眼所见的大新闻还得是家门口的蜜蜂大军举国攻占了白蚁王朝。\
**Will**: Then again, the most exciting thing we've had around here as of late is the rats fightin' in the underground.

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：爸爸，我看到了，看到了。\
**Freddy the Rascal**: I see him, Dad. I see Mr. Fog.

**威尔**：你看到什么了？\
**Will**: What's he doin'?

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：他们正在拍打自己身后的大机器——我的天哪！爸爸，你敢相信吗？\
**Freddy the Rascal**: Blimey! He's smackin' the machine! It's really strange lookin'.

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：那台吸尘器有福葛先生半个人那么大，机器上还连着一条长长的吸气管和一个巨大的漏斗状的吸雾口！\
**Freddy the Rascal**: About half the height of Mr. Fog, and connected to a very long tube and a massive funnel!

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：——噢！噢！那是什么？！\
**Freddy the Rascal**: Ooh! What's that?!

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：那台大机器里面，装了一个巨大的机械……机械器官，就像是一个肺！\
**Freddy the Rascal**: Right there inside the machine, there's a huge mechanical organ or somethin', like a lung!

**威尔**：……我等不及了，弗洛狄，爸爸要带你冲进前排观看了，坐好……\
**Will**: Ah, sod it. Hold tight, Freddy. Dad's goin' to squeeze his way to the front!

**威尔**：好嘞，爸爸也看到了……咦？那儿站了两个人，是他们前几天说的基金会本部派来的成员吗？\
**Will**: Alright, I can see them now. Eh? I don't recognize those two in uniform. Are they the officers sent from the Foundation headquarters in Australia?

**街坊Ⅰ**：说是这样的，他们是乌卢鲁组委会派来监督比赛的，最终的比赛结果也是由他们汇报到澳洲本部的。\
**Neighbor I**: That's what I heard. The Uluru Committee sent them here to supervise the qualifiers, and they'll report the results back to their headquarters, too.

**威尔**：好，能不能把从咱们十字街走出来的运动员送往澳洲总赛，就看他们的了。\
**Will**: Ah, so it's down to them whether our athletes make it to the finals in Australia or not. I'm countin' on them.

**街坊Ⅰ**：——玩笑开得可真有意思，能不能去往澳洲总赛场，还是得看运动员自己的。\
**Neighbor I**: Oh, please, Will. It's the players that you should count on, not the judges.

**威尔**：加油啊，卡洛琳！\
**Will**: Well, I hope they like Caroline as much as I do!

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：噢噢！爸爸！他们开始了，福葛先生开始向基金会的成员展示他的吸尘器了——！\
**Freddy the Rascal**: Look, Dad! Mr. Fog's about to give a demonstration of his purifier to the officers.

**街坊Ⅰ**：听说这台机器能全天候清除这方圆几十米的煤烟和浓雾，并且只需要休息一晚上第二天就能再次工作。这对于咱们召开为期两周的预选赛，还是绰绰有余的。\
**Neighbor I**: I heard that it can filter out the smog within ten yards of itself, and it only takes one night to process the waste. The qualifiers will only last two weeks, so it should manage splendidly.

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：它正在运作……它正在运作……\
**Freddy the Rascal**: It's workin'. It's workin'!

**威尔**：好家伙，看到了吗，它的功率大得吓人！它就像一头巨兽，正在一点点吞噬啮咬着这浓得像碗豆汤一样的雾气！\
**Will**: Blimey, it's powerful! It's gulpin' down the smog faster than a builder downs a pint in the pub!

**街坊Ⅰ**：它到底是怎么运作的，太神奇了……在这么大功率高产能的前提下，却能够做到没有一丝尾气排出，仅仅通过这个机械肺自体吸收净化——\
**Neighbor I**: I wonder how it works. It's a miracle that a mechanical lung of this size can purify so much air without letting out any waste!

**街坊Ⅰ**：人间奇迹，这真可谓是人间奇迹！\
**Neighbor I**: can purify so much air without letting out any waste!

**威尔**：开始了，我开始能够看清更多东西了……空气开始变得澄澈起来了。\
**Will**: The smog's gettin' thinner. I can see more clearly now.

**街坊Ⅰ**：——嘿，净化的范围正在扩张！我敢说不出一个小时，我家阳台的常青藤都能呼吸到最新鲜的空气了。\
**Neighbor I**: Look, it's even purifying the smog all the way out there! I dare say the ivy on my balcony will be enjoying fresh air within the hour!

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：太好了爸爸，我看到福葛先生笑了。\
**Freddy the Rascal**: Mr. Fog's smilin', Dad. Ain't that great?!

**威尔**：是的，他已经很多个礼拜没有笑过了。\
**Will**: It is. We ain't seen him smile for ages.

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：那帽子也跳起舞来了！\
**Freddy the Rascal**: The hat looks happy too! It's dancin'!

**威尔**：他又在跳那个滑稽的澳洲骑士舞吗？——快看看，那两个基金会来的家伙脸上是什么表情？\
**Will**: Is he doin' that Australian ranger dance again? Oh, look at the expression on those Foundation officers' faces.

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：……唔，看不出，不像是喜悦，也不像是愤怒，只是……\
**Freddy the Rascal**: Hmm. They don't look happy or mad. Is somethin' wrong?

**威尔**：等一下……怎么回事？那台机器怎么开始疯狂抖动起来——？\
**Will**: Woah! What's goin' on? The machine's shakin' like hell!

“哔——哔——哔——”\
*beep-beep-beep*

**街坊Ⅰ**：什么？什么声音在叫？听上去像是一种鸣笛警报声——！\
**Neighbor I**: What's that sound? Some kind of alarm?!

“嗞——吱吱——”\
*beep-beep-beep*

**威尔**：噢天哪！弗洛狄！快把耳朵捂上！该死，这啸叫声太强了……到底是怎么回事？是哪儿出了问题？\
**Will**: Oh! Christ! Cover your ears, Freddy! That howlin' will make you deaf. What in the bloody hell is goin' on?!

“轰——”\
*boom*

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：爸……爸爸？\
**Freddy the Rascal**: D-Dad?

**威尔**：怎么了？弗洛狄？\
**Will**: Freddy? Are you alright?

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：那台机器……爆炸了！\
**Freddy the Rascal**: I'm fine. It's the machine. It blew up!

**威尔**：什么？！\
**Will**: What?!

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：它那条长长的吸气管在一瞬间炸开了花，它圆滚滚的玻璃大肚子碎得像天上银河，那颗巨大的机械肺从里面滚了出来，吐出了一片黑色的血……\
**Freddy the Rascal**: First the pipe blew open, then its glass belly shattered, and the mechanical lung rolled out from inside. It's vomitin' up black blood.

**威尔**：你是说……？\
**Will**: There's no way.

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：还有——还有福葛先生！\
**Freddy the Rascal**: And, and Mr. Fog!

**威尔**：他怎么了？\
**Will**: What happened to him?

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：他、他在疯狂咳嗽……\
**Freddy the Rascal**: He's coughin' and coughin'.

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：总计用时三分半……\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: Three and a half minutes.

**基金会分部成员Ⅰ**：好吧，看来我们谁也没赢，谁也没输。这台机器能撑到的时间甚至还不如我预测的一半之久。\
**Foundation Branch Member I**: I guess neither one of us won that bet. It didn't even last half as long as I predicted.

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：不要太刻薄了，格里戈尔。我们千里迢迢从地球另一头赶来这儿不是为了看异国他乡的可怜民众的笑话。\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: Don't be cruel, Gregory. We didn't come all this way just to laugh at these poor people.

**基金会分部成员Ⅰ**：但这和我们以及本部的预测几乎一模一样不是吗？所谓的伦敦清洁大气委员会无非是一个天大的笑话。\
**Foundation Branch Member I**: But they did do even worse than predicted. That's a fact, isn't it? And it proves that the London Climate Management Agency is nothing but a joke.

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：我原谅你舟车劳顿还携带天生鼻炎，要在这个地方执行任务属实会令你烦躁不堪，但咱们能不能一锤定音、直截了当地告诉他们。\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: Listen, Gregory. I know you must be exhausted from the long journey and your constant sneezing, but you can't say that to their faces. Let's just do our job and give them the news.

**基金会分部成员Ⅰ**：告诉他们什么？\
**Foundation Branch Member I**: What news?

其中一人翻点着手里的运动员名单。\
She flips through the athlete roster in her hand.

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：告诉他们——\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: We have to tell them.

她清点好名单，确保里面准确无误，没有漏掉任何一个神秘学家运动员的名字。\
She verifies the list, ensuring that all the names of the arcanist athletes are accounted for.

而后，她轻轻拍了拍福葛先生的肩膀。\
When she's done, she lightly pats Mr. Fog on the shoulder.

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：福葛先生，福葛先生——？\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: Mr. Fog? Mr. Fog?

福葛先生缓缓回过头，他目光呆滞，似乎还停留在刚才的重大打击中无法自拔。\
Mr. Fog turns his head, his eyes vacant. It seems he hasn't yet got over the shock of this series of events.

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：请让一下，我需要用一下话筒。\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: Please move aside. I need to use the microphone.

福葛先生慢慢让开。\
Mr. Fog slowly steps aside.

**宽檐帽**：嘿，这位女士……您……您想……\
**Brimley**: Oi, Miss. What are you ...

但他很快也察觉到了自己这样阻止的不妥，他低下脑袋，轻轻飘荡在空中。\
He quickly realizes the impropriety of his obstruction, tips his brim, and floats gently in the air.

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：……咳咳，非常感谢大家的到来，也非常感谢福葛先生及伦敦清洁大气委员会举办的这一场欢迎与剪彩仪式，让我看到了东区人民在恶劣环境下却仍生机勃勃的面貌。\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: Ahem. Ladies and gentlemen, thank you all for coming to the ceremony today. We greatly appreciate your hospitality, and it heartens us to see you thriving despite the difficulties caused by the smog.

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：但是，很遗憾。诚如我们所见，“伦敦煤烟污染勘察与清除大使MK.Ⅲ”并未发挥出它应有的功效。\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: However, it is clear to us that the London Air Pollution Auto-Detecting Purifier MK. III is not able to fulfill its duty.

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：而盘踞在伦敦上空的雾气，依然日渐一日地对人民的身体健康虎视眈眈，企图寻求一个机会，夺走大家的生命。\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: Barring an effective solution, the smog shrouding London will do irreversible damage to both the athletes and the general populace if they stay outdoors for too long.

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：鉴于这一形势，乌卢鲁运动会国际联合组委会考虑再三，不得不做出以下沉痛决定——\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: In light of this, and after much consideration, the Uluru International Committee has decided ...

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：取消乌卢鲁运动会开设于伦敦的预选赛。\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: To cancel the London Qualifiers for the Uluru Games.

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：有关预选赛及乌卢鲁总赛的相关事宜，将在组委会的讨论协定后，公布给各位。\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: We will announce arrangements for the affected players once internal discussions are over.

这个在整场事件中始终置身事外的女人，透过冰冷的面具，扫视了一遍在场的所有人。\
Behind her cold mask, the woman methodically scans the crowd.

这些人将运动会会场围得里三层外三层，他们曾经吵闹喧嚣，而此刻，都保持着一样的呆滞和失望。\
The previously raucous energy of the crowd has been replaced by a uniform disappointment.

**基金会分部成员Ⅱ**：辛苦了，各位。\
**Foundation Branch Member II**: Thank you all for your hard work.

**纸信圈儿**：什么……？\
**Flutterpage**: What?

**纸信圈儿**：你是说，乌卢鲁预选赛，被取消了？\
**Flutterpage**: Are you sayin' that the London Qualifiers have been canceled?

**牙仙**：……恐怕是的。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I'm afraid so.

**牙仙**：虽然我并不在场，但宽檐帽先生向我转述了当时的情景……而福葛先生……似乎正在办公室里，拒绝见人。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I wasn't there, but Mr. Brimley told me what happened in the stadium. Mr. Fog has locked himself in his office. He's refusing to speak to anyone.

**牙仙**：听上去，似乎这场悲剧，已然成为定局。\
**Tooth Fairy**: It seems there's nothing we can do about it.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

**笃笃骨**：……呵……\
**Willow**: Heh!

笃笃骨缓缓将手从纸信圈儿的手中抽出，深重地看着纸信圈儿。\
Willow pulls her hand away from Flutterpage's and gives her a solemn look.

而后转身离开。\
Without a word, she turns and leaves.

**纸信圈儿**：——笃笃骨——！你去哪儿——？\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Willow? Where you goin'?!

**纸信圈儿**：笃笃骨！笃笃骨！！\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Willow! Ms. Willow!!

纸信圈儿想要追上，却被会场中正在卸货的工人潮挡住。\
She tries to chase after her, but a flood of workers sent to take down the site blocks her way.

**纸信圈儿**：笃笃骨！\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Willow!

笃笃骨听到纸信圈儿的声音后，回过头，看了一眼女孩儿。\
Willow turns and gives her one last glance.

而后，一言不发，走进了人海里。\
Before slipping away into the bustling crowd.

**纸信圈儿**：……哈……\
**Flutterpage**: *panting*

**纸信圈儿**：……哈……呼、哈……呼、哈……\
**Flutterpage**: *panting*

纸信圈儿抬起头，看向牙仙。\
Flutterpage lifts her head, her eyes meeting Tooth Fairy's.

**纸信圈儿**：牙、牙仙女士……\
**Flutterpage**: Ms.-Ms. Tooth Fairy ...

**纸信圈儿**：……为什么……\
**Flutterpage**: Why?

## LD-14 一粒灰尘 / Soot in the Petri Dish

**病人Ⅰ**：那可真是一场吓人的黑雾，我敢说如果在场，我会找一个坑直接把自己填了，或者找一个马桶把自己冲进去，也好过被那卷黑雾刮走。\
**Patient I**: The black fog seems terrifying. If I'd been there, I'd have buried myself in the garden or jumped into the sewer before it reached me.

**病人Ⅱ**：所幸那个时候医院里的病人们和护士们没有受到太大影响，只有伦纳德家的小女儿擦到了一些轻伤。\
**Patient II**: Thankfully, all the patients and nurses were fine. Only Leonard's daughter got a few bruises.

**病人Ⅰ**：可惜了那座建筑，那可是三百年前留下的老古董了，咱们时代最著名的画家都得管那些彩色琉璃窗上的圣母像叫师傅。\
**Patient I**: But what a shame it is that the building was ruined. It was 300 years old, you know. The stained glass alone was a masterwork.

**病人Ⅱ**：——呵，咳咳，咳咳咳咳……该死，这口痰就是咳不出来，胸口跟火烧着似的。\
**Patient II**: *cough* Bugger. I just can't seem to spit it out. I feel like my chest's on fire.

**牙仙**：你需要把这瓶药都喝了，一天三次，到明天你会感觉好一些。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Take this medicine three times a day, and you'll feel better tomorrow.

牙仙将药递出后，掏出一个随身的笔记本开始记录。\
Tooth Fairy hands over the medicine, then takes out a small notebook to jot something down.

**牙仙**：……这是第一百三十二个病患，临床反应依旧表现为胸口有灼烧感，且耳后发黑。这与普通的肺结核患者有着很大的差别，并不能将他们一概而论……\
**Tooth Fairy**: Case 132, clinical symptoms: burning sensation in chest, blackening of ears. Quite different from a regular tuberculosis patient. Maybe this is a different disease altogether.

**病人Ⅰ**：该死的黑雾诅咒，拜它所赐，咱们再也不会有任何好消息了。\
**Patient I**: Damn this black fog! The qualifiers are canceled, the fair's closed down ...

**病人Ⅰ**：乌卢鲁预选赛被取消了，商业街已经收到了闭市通知，乌卢鲁集市再也不可能举办了，那些贴着运动员支持率的牌子也被那些小广告盖住了……\
**Patient I**: Even Cross Street's been cordoned off. To see the posters of the athletes all covered up with flyers ... It's utterly hopeless.

**病人Ⅰ**：工人们开始抗议罢工，就跟前些年似的，除了他们没人敢在街头闲逛。人们再也不需要叫醒，因为他们大多数人一夜之间丢失了工作。\
**Patient I**: The workers are striking again, just like the old days. They seem to be the only ones who dare to go outdoors. Although, since so many have lost their jobs, I suppose they don't have any reason to go out anymore.

**病人Ⅰ**：嗯？……牙仙女士，您在做什么？\
**Patient I**: Hmm? What are you doing, Ms. Tooth Fairy?

**牙仙**：采集病人的唾液样本，可以放入培养皿观察培育。上一个培养皿这两天似乎已经有了动静……\
**Tooth Fairy**: Collecting saliva samples to put in Petri dishes. I want to see what will grow. The sample I collected two days ago has already grown something unusual.

**病人Ⅰ**：什么意思？\
**Patient I**: Something unusual?

**牙仙**：一小团黑雾，比我之前亲眼所见的要更弱小。气息不尽稳定，形态也一日一变。\
**Tooth Fairy**: A ball of black fog, weaker than the one I met in the alley. Its existence is unstable. Its form changes daily.

**牙仙**：它看上去还并不具备生物意识，但据我之前的追踪调查，这种魔精应该是有一定智力的。\
**Tooth Fairy**: It doesn't appear to have any self-consciousness, but that critter in the alley was definitely intelligent.

**病人Ⅰ**：……这，这玩意儿……有点像我给儿子读的老书里的插图啊。\
**Patient I**: Huh, this thing. It looks like the illustration in the old book I read to my son.

**病人Ⅰ**：封皮折损了，想不起来书叫什么，但里面提到过一种生物，跟它尤其相似……\
**Patient I**: I can't quite remember the title, but it does mention a creature like this.

**牙仙**：尤其相似的生物……？\
**Tooth Fairy**: A creature like this?

**宽檐帽**：嘿——！牙仙女士——！\
**Brimley**: Oi! Ms. Tooth Fairy!

一顶令人熟悉的帽子大惊失色、跌跌撞撞地飞驰而来。\
The startled hat hurtles toward them, wobbling as he goes.

**宽檐帽**：牙仙女士——！大事不妙！这位忠诚的护卫一眼都见不得这种事发生！\
**Brimley**: It's an emergency, darl! The little tacker's in danger!

**护士**：嘿……这、这位帽子先生，您——您是不被允许在医护站大吵大嚷的，这会打扰到病人们的休息……\
**Nurse**: Please, Mr. Hat, keep your voice down in the hospital. The patients need to rest.

**宽檐帽**：牙仙女士，他、他们说在老钟塔上看到一个小女孩儿，就站在最尖的高顶上，似乎正要往下坠！\
**Brimley**: Sorry about that, but this can't wait. Ms. Tooth Fairy, they said a girl's climbed to the top of the old bell tower, and she's planning to jump off!

**牙仙**：什么——？你是说……\
**Tooth Fairy**: A girl? You mean ...

**宽檐帽**：是纸信圈儿，不是她还能有谁会爬那么高——？！！\
**Brimley**: Yeah, Flutterpage! No normal girl could climb all the way up there!

**路人Ⅰ**：嘿！孩子！快下来！那儿危险——！！！\
**Passerby I**: Oi, girl! Get down! It's dangerous up there!

行人和车马已经将这条路堵得水泄不通，但喧闹声却闯入不了高空的塔楼。\
Not even the noise of the carriages and the crowd can reach as high as the bell tower, let alone the shout of one passerby.

高塔之上，小女孩状似惬意地晾着被单。\
At the top of the tower, Flutterpage is contently airing out her linens.

**纸信圈儿**：小叫醒工有很多的想法，每一条想法都会成为一个吻～\
**Flutterpage**: Knock, knock. The little knocker-upper loves hangin' sheets. Every one of them brings back a sweet memory.

**纸信圈儿**：第一天的白被单，小黄瓜和烤烟草的味道；第二天的白被单，夜露与星辰的味道；第三天的白被单，妈妈咸泪水的味道……\
**Flutterpage**: The first sheet smells like cucumber and tobacco; the second, night dew and stars; the third, hah, Mummy's cuddles.

**纸信圈儿**：嘟嘟……嘟……\
**Flutterpage**: Knock, knock.

**牙仙**：如果你想要把白被单晾在天空中，那么不用操心，云层已经替你做了这件事。\
**Tooth Fairy**: You know, you didn't need to come up so high just to hang your sheets.

**纸信圈儿**：牙仙女士——？你、你怎么在这儿……\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Tooth Fairy?! Wh-What are you doin' here?

脚踩在最后一节吱吱作响的朽木楼梯上，牙仙喘了一口气。\
Having finally reached the top of the tower, Tooth Fairy exhales heavily.

**牙仙**：呵……不如说，你在这里做什么？\
**Tooth Fairy**: I wanted to ask you the same thing.

**纸信圈儿**：这是我的……秘密基地。\
**Flutterpage**: I'm havin' some quiet time in my secret base.

**纸信圈儿**：去、去……一会儿再听你唱歌……\
**Flutterpage**: Off you pop. We'll meet up later.

她偷偷将脚边的金丝绵雀呼扇走。\
She gently shoos the canary fluttering near her feet.

**牙仙**：我认可你对独立空间的需求。但鉴于现在几乎全伦敦的人都知道有一个小女孩即将从钟塔上跳下去，我非常怀疑“秘密”这个定义。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I understand your need for privacy, but given that almost everyone in London is talking about a girl who's about to jump off the bell tower, I'd say this isn't the spot for it.

**纸信圈儿**：——跳下去？不不不，我不会坠落，我只会顺着风飞行，只要有风就不会坠落，会一直飘到……\
**Flutterpage**: Jump off the bell tower? Oh, like I might fall? Don't worry. I'll be fine as long as the wind's blowin'. I'll ride it all the way to ...

**牙仙**：澳洲？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Australia?

**纸信圈儿**：澳洲，对，那里肯定已经在举办乌卢鲁运动会了……\
**Flutterpage**: Yeah, Australia. They must be preparin' for the finals there.

女孩儿局促地玩弄着自己戴在头上的小发夹。\
The girl fidgets nervously with the clip haphazardly tucked into her hair.

**纸信圈儿**：来吧，牙仙女士，请坐在这里。\
**Flutterpage**: Come here, Ms. Tooth Fairy. Have a seat.

牙仙优雅地将脚跨出围栏，二人一起坐在塔楼之上。脚踩云层，安安静静。\
Tooth Fairy gracefully swings her leg over the railing, and the two sit quietly side by side, their feet swinging among the clouds.

**路人Ⅱ**：下来！利伯蒂——！快下来——！上面危险！！！\
**Passerby II**: Come on down, Liberti! Quickly! It's dangerous up there!

**路人Ⅲ**：——嘘，你在说什么话呢！你不能这么跟她说，她说不定会直接跳下来——！\
**Passerby III**: Don't listen to him, Liberti! Oi, you, watch your words! She might jump right off the bloody thing!

塔楼底下人声与喇叭声依然喧闹着。\
The clamor of the streets below continues.

**纸信圈儿**：为什么……？\
**Flutterpage**: Why?

**牙仙**：什么？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Why what?

**纸信圈儿**：……他们有些人叫我下去，有些人又叫我不要“下去”。为什么这个世界上有那么多人沉迷于指使和命令别人，甚至超过约束自己？\
**Flutterpage**: First, they told me to get down, and then they told me not to. Why'd they change their minds so quickly?

**纸信圈儿**：就像他们有时候离开，有时候回来；有时候说要，有时候又不要；有时候说想，有时候又不想。\
**Flutterpage**: Not just them. It's like, all of a sudden, everythin's changed. People said they wanted the qualifiers, but then they canceled them. They said they'd find a solution, but then they just completely gave up on solvin' the problem.

**纸信圈儿**：可是没有一个人愿意爬上来看一看。其实只要足够高，就能看到云层之上的世界。\
**Flutterpage**: Why couldn't they just keep at it until they achieved somethin'? It's like climbin' this bell tower. You've got to push through and keep goin' until you reach the top. Otherwise, you'll never get to enjoy the view.

**牙仙**：或许他们只是……\
**Tooth Fairy**: Maybe they ...

短暂地思考后，牙仙摇摇头。\
After a quick moment of reflection, Tooth Fairy shakes her head.

**牙仙**：嗯，我也不知道为什么。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Well, I don't know.

**纸信圈儿**：牙仙女士……\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Tooth Fairy.

**纸信圈儿**：我好像，做了一件错事……\
**Flutterpage**: I think I did somethin' wrong.

**纸信圈儿**：我会自己剪头发，会自己扣纽扣，我会躲起来读大人们丢进垃圾桶的报纸。这些东西不用老师教，我自己全能搞懂——\
**Flutterpage**: I can cut my own hair, cook my own meals, and do my own laundry. No one taught me. I just figured it out myself.

**纸信圈儿**：只要我去尽情想象，这个世界就会清晰得像一只鱼缸，而所有的答案，就是里面游动的小金鱼。\
**Flutterpage**: I used to think the world was like the fish tank I had at home. No matter how many questions I had, the answers were all inside, just like the fish swimmin' in there.

**纸信圈儿**：我很有耐心，我会一条一条抓上来，通过它张开的口往里面看，直到看见它的肠子和鱼泡——我不会放弃。\
**Flutterpage**: I was patient, too. I'd take the fish one by one and carefully look them over, and I wouldn't stop until I'd checked every scale—yep, every single one.

**纸信圈儿**：……至少，在爸爸妈妈责怪我前，我不会放弃。\
**Flutterpage**: Well, unless Mum and Dad scolded me.

**纸信圈儿**：事实上，我有时候不知道为什么妈妈要打我、爸爸要怪我……我只是想搞明白很多为什么。\
**Flutterpage**: Actually, sometimes I couldn't figure out why they hit me. I just had a lot of questions, and I wanted to know the answers.

**纸信圈儿**：现在我好像真的搞明白了……\
**Flutterpage**: Anyway, now I've learned the truth about the world.

**纸信圈儿**：原来，这个世界和我想的不太一样。\
**Flutterpage**: It's different from what I imagined.

**纸信圈儿**：我以为它是圆的鱼缸，可是它是方的……我以为里面装的是小金鱼，但它可能是小丑鱼、是鲨鱼，甚至可能只是一些饼干屑。\
**Flutterpage**: I thought it was a round tank, but it was actually square. I thought there were goldfish swimmin' inside, but actually there were pinchin' crabs and chompin' sharks, sometimes even just pieces of rubbish.

**纸信圈儿**：它永远和我想的不一样。我搞明白的事实是——我永远也不可能搞明白任何事。\
**Flutterpage**: The round tank only existed in my mind, and all the answers I found were nothin'—just my imagination.

**纸信圈儿**：在这个过程中，我什么答案都没有得到，却还伤害了其他人。\
**Flutterpage**: And what's worse is that I hurt others with my imaginary answers.

风的吻同时降临在二人的发梢。\
A gentle breeze rustles their hair.

**牙仙**：你是指……夏洛特小姐吗？\
**Tooth Fairy**: You mean Ms. O'Hagan?

**纸信圈儿**：……\
**Flutterpage**: ...

**纸信圈儿**：花园拒绝我了……\
**Flutterpage**: I let her down.

淡淡的柠檬香一掠而过。牙仙忽然笑了。\
A faint scent of lemon floats by. Tooth Fairy gives an unexpected smile.

**牙仙**：我——在人类的学校度过了整个少年时代。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I ... I spent my entire youth learning how to get along with others.

**牙仙**：你知道我发现的最有意思的事情是什么吗？那就是——“答案”，对于他们很多人来说没有意义。\
**Tooth Fairy**: And you know what I realized? People will change as long as the result benefits them.

**牙仙**：当他们掌握了“答案”，让自己成为了“更好的人”，然后，他们就忘记了如何提问。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Once things are going well, whether expected or not, people often forget the goals they set before they reached that point.

**牙仙**：而答案真正的意义，其实存在于问题里——以及……提问者的心里。\
**Tooth Fairy**: What I'm trying to say is, we need to remember who we really are and what we really want.

纸信圈儿感兴趣似的扭头看向牙仙。\
Flutterpage turns her head to look at Tooth Fairy, curiosity in her eyes.

牙仙则偏着头，似乎在思考着什么。\
Tooth Fairy tilts her head to the side, as though deep in thought.

**牙仙**：作为本世纪自由祭祀运动最小年纪的纪录保持者，笃笃骨小姐一定手握很多“答案”，但她如今想要把它们都扔掉。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Ms. Willow must've known what she really wanted. Otherwise, she wouldn't have become the youngest Floor Ritual record holder of the century.

她停顿了一下。\
She pauses.

**牙仙**：其中的缘由和滋味，她一定懂。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I'm sure she understands that it wasn't your fault.

**牙仙**：你没有伤害她，事实上，你没有伤害任何人。\
**Tooth Fairy**: You didn't hurt her. In fact, you didn't hurt anyone.

**牙仙**：你只是，还没有抓到属于自己的那条金鱼。\
**Tooth Fairy**: You just need to look at the fish tank in a new way.

**纸信圈儿**：……\
**Flutterpage**: ...

纸信圈儿回过头，继续看向远方。\
Flutterpage looks off into the horizon.

**纸信圈儿**：哎哟……好痛……\
**Flutterpage**: Ugh. It hurts.

纸信圈儿吃痛地捂住嘴，皱起眉头。\
She presses her hand to her cheek, her little face scrunched up small.

**牙仙**：怎么了，我看看？\
**Tooth Fairy**: What's wrong? Let me take a look.

**牙仙**：你换牙了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Hmm. You're losing a tooth.

**牙仙**：新的牙齿把旧的牙齿顶了出来。\
**Tooth Fairy**: A new tooth is pushing out the old one.

**纸信圈儿**：换……换牙……？可是我已经都换过了。\
**Flutterpage**: A new tooth? But I've already lost all my baby teeth.

**牙仙**：来，张大嘴，不要怕，不会痛的——\
**Tooth Fairy**: Open your mouth. Don't worry. It won't hurt.

**纸信圈儿**：啊——啊——啊……唔……唔！唔唔！痛痛痛！……唔……\
**Flutterpage**: Ah ... Ugh ... Ugh! Ouch!

**牙仙**：拔下来了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: It's out.

**牙仙**：看。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Look.

牙仙摊开手，一颗牙齿完整地躺在她的手中。\
She opens her hand, revealing a perfectly intact tooth.

**纸信圈儿**：我、我还以为我已经全都换完了。\
**Flutterpage**: I-I thought I didn't have any baby teeth left.

**牙仙**：嗯，它是最后一颗。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Well, you don't anymore. This was the last one.

纸信圈儿凑近去看。\
Flutterpage moves closer to get a better look at it.

**纸信圈儿**：唔，它臭乎乎的。\
**Flutterpage**: Ew, it stinks!

**牙仙**：是的，看来这最后一颗乳牙，是我的了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: It does. I suppose I'll keep this, then.

牙仙拿出手帕，满意地将这颗小小的乳牙包起来，塞进口袋里。\
Tooth Fairy produces a handkerchief, contentedly wraps the tooth, and stows it in her pocket.

## LD-15 触底反弹 / Back in the Game

**无线电广播**：来看看她当年的一篇采访。\
**Radio Broadcast**: Let's listen again to the interview she had all those years ago.

**无线电广播**：“你身为本世纪年龄最小的冠军及纪录保持者，世界冠军的头衔近在咫尺，还有什么是你想要实现的？”\
**Radio Broadcast**: "As the youngest Floor Ritual record holder of the century, you're just one step away from becoming the world champion. What else do you wish to achieve in your career?"

**无线电广播**：“我认为，我的长期目标就是乌卢鲁决赛的冠军。”\
**Radio Broadcast**: "My ultimate goal is to win the finals of the Uluru Games."

**无线电广播**：“而且还不止一项，我会尽我所能报名参加更多项的比赛。”\
**Radio Broadcast**: "But I'll also register for as many events as possible."

**无线电广播**：“我有很多目标，但我很有耐心，我会一步一步去实现它。”\
**Radio Broadcast**: "I have a lot I want to achieve, but I'm patient, and I'm sure I can do it all eventually."

“喀哒——喀——”黑暗中传来金属的声音。\
*clink—clunk* The sound of metal cuts through the darkness.

**笃笃骨**：来吧，老朋友。\
**Willow**: Now, old friend.

笃笃骨将机械腿卸下，伸出修长的手指去取放在柜子上的润滑脂。\
Willow removes her prosthetic leg, her long fingers stretching out toward the machine lubricant resting on the shelf.

**笃笃骨**：我们现在只剩彼此了，不是吗？\
**Willow**: It's just you and me, isn't it?

她伸出的手指在摸索润滑脂的时候，感受到了旁边一张被揉烂的纸的触感。\
As she gropes for the lubricant, she comes across a piece of crumpled paper.

**工人Ⅰ**：轻拿轻放，伙计们。动作慢一点，小心一点，这可是铁架子，要是砸到了脚可得在医院住上一段呢。\
**Worker I**: Careful with the scaffolding, fellas. You wouldn't want it to fall on your feet. You'll be hobblin' about for months!

几个工人正在将刚搭好的会场舞台卸下，每人抬着一个木头桩走到门口。\
Workers are busy disassembling the stage, carrying wooden posts and equipment to the door.

**福葛先生**：来，这是您的赔偿申请表，只需要在上面填上金额明细，并附上购买单或材料损耗证据，我会统一联系乌卢鲁组委会赔偿您的损失的。\
**Mr. Fog**: Here's the reimbursement application form. Just fill in the numbers and give me the receipts for the materials. I'll contact the Uluru Committee for your compensation.

**工人Ⅰ**：福葛先生，真的办不成了吗？伙计们当时把运动场架起来的时候，可没有想过现在这样啊。\
**Worker I**: Is there really no hope, Mr. Fog? We didn't build all this just to tear it all down.

**福葛先生**：实在抱歉。\
**Mr. Fog**: I'm sorry.

**工人Ⅰ**：说实话，即便您帮我们争取修建会场的赔偿，我们也不想把这里拆了。\
**Worker I**: To be honest, we'd rather not do this, even if we are gettin' paid for it.

**工人Ⅰ**：我们当时搭建的时候可是充满希望啊。您瞧，那个巨大的广告牌、那个高高的开幕会舞台，还有擦得干干净净的观众席。\
**Worker I**: We were over the moon when we got the job. I mean, just look at this place. The huge billboards and that lovely stage background.

**工人Ⅰ**：这一切多好啊，下一次在咱们这儿举办如此大型的比赛也不知道要到什么时候了。\
**Worker I**: How could we not be? It's been yonks since we last had an event like this, and who knows when we'll have another?

**工人Ⅰ**：——真的什么都做不了了吗？\
**Worker I**: Is there really nothin' we can do?

**福葛先生**：……我……\
**Mr. Fog**: I ...

**卡洛琳**：——不好意思……请问……\
**Caroline Bartley**: Excuse me. Um ...

从工人的木桩后传出一个声音。\
A voice floats over from behind the ladder in the workers' arms.

**工人Ⅰ**：——噢！不好意思，瞧瞧我，扛着这大木头梯子堵在门口，挡着大家伙离开会场了。\
**Worker I**: Oops! Look at me, blockin' the doorway with my ladder! Beggin' your pardon, Miss.

**卡洛琳**：没关系，我们愿意站在门口听你们多聊聊天，毕竟没有谁愿意这么快离开这里。\
**Caroline Bartley**: That's quite alright. I'm glad to stay a little longer and talk with everyone. None of us want to leave, actually.

**工人Ⅰ**：运动员女士说得我心里挺难过，是啊，没有人愿意就这么离开这儿。\
**Worker I**: How sad. But it's true. Who'd want to leave after all the trouble we've gone to?

**福葛先生**：卡洛琳女士——？我们竟然在这里又见面了。\
**Mr. Fog**: Ms. Bartley? I must say, I didn't expect to see you here after all the qualifiers were canceled.

**卡洛琳**：福葛先生，您好，天气不错——我很高兴看到您缓过来了。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Hello, Mr. Fog. I'm glad to see you back on your feet.

**福葛先生**：哈哈，总得做点事不是吗？预选赛取消后，还有一堆事没处理呢，它们可不等人。\
**Mr. Fog**: Well, I can't wallow all day. There's a lot of cleaning up to do, and someone has to do it.

**福葛先生**：那您呢，卡洛琳女士，您已经准备回去了吗？\
**Mr. Fog**: How about you, Ms. Bartley? Will you be leaving shortly?

**卡洛琳**：是的，我可能会离开伦敦等待后续组委会的通知。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Yes. I suppose I'll go home and wait to hear the arrangements the committee's come up with.

**福葛先生**：……\
**Mr. Fog**: ...

**宽檐帽**：……您不考虑在这儿再多呆几天吗？\
**Brimley**: Why don't you stay for a few more days?

**卡洛琳**：或许，没有太大的意义了……\
**Caroline Bartley**: Well, I don't think there's much point.

她抬眼遥望了一下人丁稀落的会场。\
She looks around the almost deserted venue.

**卡洛琳**：实际上，我并不需要来参加预选赛，我已经拿到了组委会特批的决赛门票。\
**Caroline Bartley**: In fact, I'm the number one seed this year, so I don't even have to participate in the qualifiers to advance to the finals.

**卡洛琳**：他们会根据运动员全年的积分表现选取个别选手直通决赛。据说这是向人类的标准化赛事靠拢的一项鼓励措施。\
**Caroline Bartley**: It's a new system they introduced to get a step closer to the standardization of human sporting events.

**卡洛琳**：我这次来，只是想在自己的家乡参加一次运动会——\
**Caroline Bartley**: I only joined because I couldn't pass up the opportunity to compete in my hometown.

**卡洛琳**：我的……最后一次运动会……\
**Caroline Bartley**: This was going to be ... the last competition of my career.

她叹了一口气，顿了顿，继续开口。\
She sighs. Then, after a moment's hesitation, she speaks again.

**卡洛琳**：以及，我还以为……不，没有什么。\
**Caroline Bartley**: And I thought ... No, never mind.

**卡洛琳**：事实上，这个结果也算是情理之中，只是我们大家都愿意去做一个自欺欺人的梦罢了。而梦总该醒来……\
**Caroline Bartley**: I wasn't surprised when the news came out, to be honest. We were just fooling ourselves before, and now it's time to face the fact that—

**工人Ⅰ**：呃……福、福葛先生，不好意思，请容许我打断一下——不是我说，现在是不是天黑得太快了一点。\
**Worker I**: Sorry to interrupt you, but ain't it too early to be gettin' this dark, Mr. Fog?

正在聊天的人抬起头，世界一瞬间浸入浓墨般的黑暗中。\
The three of them look up at the sky as the world is plunged into darkness.

**宽檐帽**：呃、福葛伙计，现在几点了？\
**Brimley**: Crikey. What time is it, mate?

**福葛先生**：不用看表都能猜到，至少绝对不会是深夜。\
**Mr. Fog**: I don't have to look at my watch to know it isn't night yet.

**宽檐帽**：那咱们现在到底是……\
**Brimley**: Then what's going on?

黑黄色的浓雾突然如巨臂一般腾起，几乎要将人卷起。\
The thick black-and-yellow smog surges upward, like a massive arm poised to sweep them away.

**宽檐帽**：噢噢噢噢——看在上天的份上，现在到底是怎么回事——？！\
**Brimley**: Whoa! What the bloody hell is happening?!

**牙仙**：——你们没事吧？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Are you alright?

**宽檐帽**：我们没事，谢谢你们的关心。托老天爷的福，刚刚那到底是什么东西？\
**Brimley**: All good, thanks. What the blazes was that?

**牙仙**：和我刚到伦敦时，那个将医院屋顶掀翻的黑雾一模一样。\
**Tooth Fairy**: It looked just like the black fog that attacked the hospital.

**牙仙**：但并没有上一次那么巨大，形状也不尽相同……\
**Tooth Fairy**: Only smaller. And it was a different shape.

**牙仙**：福葛先生，具体情况，我们需要去你的办公室详聊。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Let's move to your office, Mr. Fog. There's something we need to talk about.

**牙仙**：我怀疑，伦敦的大雾、病人的“肺结核”以及这场乌卢鲁预选赛的取消，或许都跟它有关。\
**Tooth Fairy**: I believe all these problems we're having—the smog, the tuberculosis, the failure of your machine—have something to do with the black fog.

**福葛先生**：这……\
**Mr. Fog**: What?

**牙仙**：我们现在首先要做的，是疏散群众，离开会场，以防它再次袭来。\
**Tooth Fairy**: But first, we need to get everyone out of the stadium in case it attacks again.

一进到办公室，宽檐帽便走到那台雾气净化器跟前，有些好奇地敲着它顶部的玻璃罩。\
Upon entering the office, Brimley heads straight to the purifier and gives its glass top a curious tap.

**福葛先生**：放过它吧，它躺在那儿有些时候了。\
**Mr. Fog**: Leave it be. It's no use worrying about it now.

福葛先生瞥了一眼角落里那台备受瞩目的雾气净化器，它如今只能静静地躺在角落。\
Mr. Fog glances at his once-revered purification machine, now sitting inert in the corner.

**宽檐帽**：老伙计，你给它施加的压力太大了。\
**Brimley**: You pushed it too hard, mate.

**牙仙**：你能把它造出来已经很不错了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Don't be too hard on yourself, Mr. Fog. The fact that you made something that worked at all in just a matter of weeks is an achievement in itself.

**福葛先生**：哈哈，别安慰我了，牙仙女士。它现在没有作用了，就不该再放在这里占地方……我只是、呃……\
**Mr. Fog**: Haha, I appreciate it, Ms. Tooth Fairy. I know it doesn't make any sense to keep it around after it failed so spectacularly, but I just ... ugh!

福葛先生想要用力将其抱起，挪动一下位置，但他失败了。\
He tries to raise it off the ground to shift it, but doesn't succeed.

**福葛先生**：——还不太想把它拆了——毕竟它注入了我的神秘术，与我同呼同吸，共同净化，现在倒是有点跟我同病相怜的意思了……咳咳……\
**Mr. Fog**: I can't bear to break it down. At least not for now. I enchanted it with my arcane skill, so we're linked together. It used to breathe as I did, and now I cough and splutter just like it does. *cough*

**牙仙**：你还是尽快到医院就诊比较好。\
**Tooth Fairy**: You should go to the hospital as soon as possible.

**宽檐帽**：哈！我都已经提醒这伙计多少次了，他就是不听。\
**Brimley**: See? How many times have I told you that, and you never listened?! Even the doctor's saying so!

**宽檐帽**：所以牙仙女士，您要跟我们说的是什么？——那个黑雾，究竟是怎么回事？\
**Brimley**: Anyway, what was it that you wanted to talk about, Ms. Tooth Fairy?

**牙仙**：这是我这几天在做的实验。实验皿中装的，是我从黑雾离开的角落中采集到的一点黑雾的尾翼。\
**Tooth Fairy**: The experiments I've been doing these days. Here's a sample of the black fog. I collected it from the alley after it attacked me.

**牙仙**：而我从病患唾液中检测到了与它一模一样的成分，几乎可以断定这种将自己隐藏在雾中的魔精，正是那些“雾病诅咒”的罪魁祸首。\
**Tooth Fairy**: As for the tuberculosis, I analyzed the black fog's composition and found some components very similar to those in the patients' saliva. I've concluded that this fog critter is the root cause of the disease.

**牙仙**：将更多的雾气注入时，这种魔精会溶于雾中，它以煤烟和雾气为养料，变换自己的形态，无法触碰也无法实质性地将其消灭。\
**Tooth Fairy**: This critter is fog-soluble, can change its form, and is indestructible. It feeds on smog, and, most interestingly, sensitive emotions, which it seems to absorb to nourish itself.

**牙仙**：可以说，它生之于雾又以雾为食。\
**Tooth Fairy**: In conclusion, the answer to our problems lies in capturing and containing these critters.

**牙仙**：而另一方面，假设在所有变量都不变的情况下，我们将其置于阳光中。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Also, in one of my experiments, I cultured two samples under the same conditions and put one of them in the sun, like this.

牙仙轻轻将装着黑色小魔精的玻璃瓶放在窗边。\
Tooth Fairy delicately places the bottle containing the black critter on the windowsill.

**牙仙**：你们看，即便是在光线如此弱的环境下，它也会很快缩小。\
**Tooth Fairy**: See? Even in today's dim sunlight, it shrinks very quickly.

**牙仙**：甚至……\
**Tooth Fairy**: Just wait a moment, and you'll see ...

**牙仙**：露出它的实体。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Its true being.

**牙仙**：阳光是它们的死敌，晴朗的天气会使它们无处遁逃。所以你很难在这片土地之外见到它们的身影。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Sunlight is their weakness. That's why you never see them in areas with clear skies.

牙仙停顿了一下，似乎为了加重语气。\
She pauses, as if to add gravity to her point.

**牙仙**：而这就是我们能够捕捉它的机会。\
**Tooth Fairy**: As you can see, London provides the perfect conditions for it to survive and multiply: heavy smog and the anxiety and depression caused by the cancelation of the qualifiers.

沉默在小办公室内荡漾而开。\
A thoughtful silence falls in the office.

**福葛先生**：……我相信您的假设……但，想要从雾气中把它逮住又谈何容易？\
**Mr. Fog**: I do believe you're right, but it won't be easy to capture these things.

**牙仙**：关于这个……\
**Tooth Fairy**: No, definitely not.

**牙仙**：我也在思考……也许我们会有一种办法能够将它引出来……但，不好把控，不好预估，也就不好做准备……\
**Tooth Fairy**: I'm still trying to figure that one out. We may be able to lure them into a trap, but we need to make a specific plan so that the process is controllable and the results predictable.

**福葛先生**：什么办法？现在我能想到的办法只有向上帝祈祷。\
**Mr. Fog**: A specific plan? The only plan I can think of is to pray to God!

**牙仙**：祈祷，是的。有时向神灵寻求答案也是一种方法，但走不走得通又是另说了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Some people may seek answers from the divine, but whether that works or not is another matter.

**纸信圈儿**：嘿——\
**Flutterpage**: Oi!

**牙仙**：……？！\
**Tooth Fairy**: ...?

**宽檐帽**：嗯？\
**Brimley**: Hmm?

**纸信圈儿**：你能看得到我吗？\
**Flutterpage**: Helloooo!

**福葛先生**：我怎么好像听到纸信圈儿的声音。\
**Mr. Fog**: Is that Flutterpage's voice?

**宽檐帽**：——在窗外，老伙计，窗外——！\
**Brimley**: Sure is. Over there, mate. Outside the window!

窗户被推开。\
There's a tap at the window.

撑着一个白被单的纸信圈儿飘荡在空中。在她身下，是一群人，老老少少，他们正一起沿着十字街街道向运动场进发。\
Outside, Flutterpage drifts in the air, a white bedsheet clutched in her hands. Below her, a crowd of all ages makes their way along Cross Street, all heading for the sports stadium.

**纸信圈儿**：想要加入我们吗？\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Tooth Fairy, Mr. Fog, Mr. Brimley! Would you like to join us?

**牙仙**：什么？\
**Tooth Fairy**: What?

**纸信圈儿**：加入我们——我们，全十字街的居民都在一起请愿，继续举办运动会！\
**Flutterpage**: The residents of Cross Street have got together to petition for the reopenin' of the qualifiers!

纸信圈儿用一只手撑着被单，另一只手兴奋地指着街道上聚集在一起的人群。\
Flutterpage uses one hand to steady the bedsheet and the other to point excitedly at the crowd congregating below.

**威尔**：嘿，大家看看用这个当铅球怎么样？这口大锅也算是我们家的家产了。\
**Will**: Oi, folks! How 'bout this iron? It's a family heirloom, but it'll be perfect for the Floating Shot Fling!

**街坊Ⅰ**：——我！我可以当记分员！我最擅长在发呆的时候数秒，能够数得一分不差呢！\
**Neighbor I**: And I'll be the stopwatch! I'm an excellent timekeeper. I can keep time down to the millisecond!

**街坊Ⅱ**：咱们不需要一个公正正直的裁判吗？作为一个二十年来在维修工岗位上兢兢业业的老管道工，我要求自荐！\
**Neighbor II**: We also need a fair judge, right? Then I'll put myself forward! Everyone on Cross Street knows I'm an excellent mediator!

**纸信圈儿**：看呐，大家都已经把自己家所有能用的工具都拿来了！木梯子、晾衣杆、热水壶……大家要一起把拆了的舞台重建起来——！\
**Flutterpage**: Everyone's brought things from their homes! Ladders, hangin' rods, clotheslines, anythin' that might be useful. We're goin' to rebuild the stadium together!

**纸信圈儿**：要加入我们吗？——牙仙女士、宽檐帽先生、福葛先生？\
**Flutterpage**: So? Will you join us?

**福葛先生**：这、这是在做什么？！\
**Mr. Fog**: What? Are you serious?!

**宽檐帽**：——我，我也一时间无法在头脑中寻找到一个合适的词汇去描述和形容……我——\
**Brimley**: Strewth! I don't know what to say. This is unbelievable!

人潮浩浩荡荡地涌向运动会场，甚至每经过一栋住宅，都会有一两个人从里面走出，加入到游行队伍中。\
The crowd pushes on to the stadium, a few individuals joining the throng as they pass by their homes.

他们脸上洋溢着一种决绝的欣喜。仿佛没有什么事，能够撼动他们热切的期盼。\
There is a resolute happiness in the air, as though no force could diminish their fervent hope.

**纸信圈儿**：——如果，预选赛无法举办，那么就举办一个属于我们自己的运动会。\
**Flutterpage**: Since the qualifiers have been canceled, we'll just have to hold our own Games.

**纸信圈儿**：牙仙女士，我找到属于我的那条金鱼了。\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Tooth Fairy, I've found the right way to look at the fish tank.

## LD-16 我们的乌卢鲁 / Our Uluru Games

**福葛先生**：所以，你支持重新举办运动会——？\
**Mr. Fog**: So, you're going to join them?!

**宽檐帽**：……我……你了解我……我热爱一切超乎常理的可能性。\
**Brimley**: I ... You know me. I'll always jump brim first into the unknown.

**福葛先生**：可基金会已经撤资了，承包商正在等待赔款，运动员们开始安排转移……这样的情况下，我们不可能再……\
**Mr. Fog**: But the Foundation's already pulled their funding. The workers are already awaiting their reimbursement, and some players have already left ... How could we possibly hold a—

**宽檐帽**：老伙计，事实上……\
**Brimley**: Mate, listen up.

剑拔弩张的气氛在办公室回荡，这似乎是这两个老友第一次争吵。\
There is an unfamiliar tension in the office. This may be the first real disagreement between the two old friends.

**宽檐帽**：那两个本部来调查的官老爷，你看他们脸上的表情就知道，他们根本不在乎这个预选赛能不能举办。\
**Brimley**: Those officers from the headquarters didn't give a damn whether the qualifiers were held or not. You could see it all over their faces.

**宽檐帽**：他们只是想要省事，拿到撤销许可，该赔偿的赔偿、该承诺的承诺，到最后却是一再把计划延后。\
**Brimley**: All they wanted was to minimize their trouble. Did you see how quickly they applied for the cancelation and reimbursement? How hastily they made promises to pacify the people? I've never seen anyone more ready to get things over with.

**宽檐帽**：——或许十字街以外的人已经决定忘记这个比赛了。官老爷们只在乎我们递给他们的一纸名单，并不在意这个比赛本身。\
**Brimley**: Their job was done as soon as they got the player list. They'd probably already moved their attention to the qualifiers in other regions.

**宽檐帽**：对于世人来说，这场运动会可有可无，但是……\
**Brimley**: After all, our qualifiers are no different from the others to them, but ...

**福葛先生**：……\
**Mr. Fog**: ...

**宽檐帽**：……作为一个自由的骑士被唤醒，我的本性呼唤我驰骋、奔腾、超越速度的极限、它渴望呐喊、渴望冲撞、渴望忘记烦恼的沉浸。\
**Brimley**: It means something to us, doesn't it? At least for me. This could be my chance to go to Australia. My very nature wants me to run free on the red land, to holler out and forget all my troubles.

**宽檐帽**：我想大伙也正是如此。\
**Brimley**: I think that's what we all want.

**宽檐帽**：你的心在哪儿，你的运动会就在哪儿。\
**Brimley**: In the heat of competition, people are at their best, their most pure.

**宽檐帽**：老伙计，我跟着你忙前忙后，不是只有你在意这台吸尘器到底应该在比赛场上大放异彩还是躺在你的办公室里发霉。\
**Brimley**: Think about it, mate. You're not the only one who's put a lot of effort into this machine. It hurts me to see it rotting in the office, too.

**宽檐帽**：如果你要因为那两个官老爷一句话就放弃咱们准备这么久的比赛，那我可能得拿出一名斥候的严厉态度。\
**Brimley**: If you're really going to give up because of a few words from an authority, then as your partner, I have to tell you:

**宽檐帽**：因为我不允许有任何人肆意丢弃你的赫赫战功，包括你自己。\
**Brimley**: Don't ever let anyone deny your achievements! Including yourself!

宽檐帽最后一句话像从空中俯冲而落的惊鸟，将刚才的讨论砸成碎片。\
These words hit like a bomb, bringing his grand speech to an end.

**福葛先生**：放宽心……放宽心……\
**Mr. Fog**: Alright, calm down, old chap.

**牙仙**：福葛先生，这是一场运动会，是展现每个人意志的地方。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Mr. Fog, the people want the qualifiers because they're for everyone.

**牙仙**：每个人，每种意志，它都会一并容纳，并使它大放异彩。\
**Tooth Fairy**: They provide each and every person with an equal opportunity to shine.

看着福葛先生犹豫不决的神情，牙仙微笑着补充道。\
Sensing Mr. Fog's uncertainty, Tooth Fairy smiles as she offers her contribution.

**牙仙**：所以，这也会是你我的舞台，或者说是……战场。\
**Tooth Fairy**: And that includes you and me. Although, for us, it'll be more like a battle to fight.

她低头看着窗外的人们，有些许无奈地摇了摇头。\
She gazes out the window at the people below, her head shaking gently in quiet frustration.

**福葛先生**：……\
**Mr. Fog**: ...

一句枣核般的话卡在嗓子里，咽不下也吐不出。半晌，福葛先生才叹了口气。\
Words lodge in his throat like a date pit, neither going down nor coming up. After a pause, he sighs deeply.

**福葛先生**：真是的，是谁给我的办公室里塞满了请愿信的？这两天我一来办公室都能收到好几封！\
**Mr. Fog**: Honestly, will these people stop sending me petitions?! I've been absolutely inundated with them!

他绕到办公桌后面，拉开抽屉，状似愤愤地将一沓信封摔在办公桌上。\
Circling to the back of the desk, he opens a drawer and throws a pile of envelopes onto the desk with feigned anger.

宽檐帽和牙仙并不知道他想要表达什么，只愣在原地。\
Brimley and Tooth Fairy remain silent, unsure of how to interpret his intent.

**福葛先生**：算上我一个吧。我拦不住你们，但是……我至少要保证你们的健康。\
**Mr. Fog**: *sigh* Fine. Someone has to keep everyone healthy. I'll do everything I can to minimize the damage from the smog.

过了一会儿，福葛先生抬起头。\
After a moment, Mr. Fog lifts his head.

**福葛先生**：放宽心，我会去跟管理局那边协商好，争取给大家把这场民间运动会，办得顺顺利利。\
**Mr. Fog**: Don't worry. I'll talk to the Relief Centre to sort out all the paperwork for the event.

**纸信圈儿**：这是您的，这是您的，这是您的……我们需要保证每个人手里都有一份应急指南，大家请一定要仔细阅读，它能保证我们在发生紧急状况时有应对策略。\
**Flutterpage**: Here you are. This is yours. Please come here for a copy of the emergency guidebook if you don't have one! Make sure you read it carefully. We don't want anyone hurt if there's an emergency.

**纸信圈儿**：还有这个，大家可以裹上我特制的小被单，它们注入了我的神秘术，是我这两天灵机一动的好念头。\
**Flutterpage**: And here, take this special sheet I enchanted to protect you from the smog. I came up with the idea a couple days ago.

**纸信圈儿**：它能伴随着风腾起，并驾驭着风驱散自己面前的雾——虽然只有一点点范围……但也总好过没有。\
**Flutterpage**: It can drive away the smog around you by controllin' the wind. Not very effective, but it's better than nothin'.

**工人Ⅰ**：不得了，你自己一个人为我们准备了这么多？\
**Worker I**: Blimey, you did all this yourself?

**工人Ⅱ**：小叫醒工操心什么呢？放心吧，我们已经在这大雾天里工作、生活了几代了，还怕在这大雾天里开一个运动会吗？\
**Worker II**: Cheers, little knocker-upper, but you don't need to worry about us. We've lived in the smog for generations. What can it hurt to hold a little sportin' event in it?

**威尔**：没错，我们想要继续举办这场运动会，就算是有任何情况，我们也能自行承担。\
**Will**: Agreed. We asked for the exhibition ourselves, so we'll pay the price if anythin' happens.

**福葛先生**：这是你们的申请确认表，你们的应急预案已经获得了应急管理局的批准。我和我的同僚会与管理局一起保障大家的安全。\
**Mr. Fog**: Here's the confirmation of your application. Your contingency plan has been approved by the Relief Centre. My colleagues and I will do everything we can to keep you all safe.

**福葛先生**：我的“伦敦煤烟污染勘察与清除大使MK.Ⅲ”，虽然在之前的展示环节失败了，但……我会尽力修好它。\
**Mr. Fog**: As for the London Air Pollution Auto-Detecting Purifier MK. III, I'll do my best to fix it.

**福葛先生**：就像大家一致决定的，将还未离开这座城市的运动员们召集起来，举办一个不计分的小型比赛。\
**Mr. Fog**: Next, we'll gather the athletes who have yet to leave the city and hold a small exhibition game.

**宽檐帽**：至少，运动员们这么多日的练习和辛苦，还能换来一个舞台，还有一群观众在看。\
**Brimley**: Of course, it won't be an official event, but at least it'll give an opportunity for the athletes to demonstrate their hard work to a group of spectators.

**宽檐帽**：而这些观众也依然能赌赛，能喝彩，能为自己喜欢的运动员鼓气，再等一切结束后，带上这股热情的余温回到他们的日常生活里。\
**Brimley**: I'm sure they'll be a great source of inspiration for the people of London as they cheer on their favorite athletes!

**威尔**：——嘿！福葛先生！您来了，瞧我给您带的，丽娜婆婆熬的玉米羹，还有面包和黄油。\
**Will**: Oi, Mr. Fog! I brought you this. It's Mrs. Brown's leek and potato soup with bread and butter.

**福葛先生**：……噢天哪，感谢婆婆挂心——大家都吃了吗？\
**Mr. Fog**: Oh, Mrs. Brown. Please give her my thanks. Has everyone eaten?

**威尔**：都吃上了，我、丽娜婆婆、琼斯太太，还有大本家的小儿子，从清晨四点就在忙活大家的午餐了。\
**Will**: Yeah. Mrs. Brown, Mrs. Jones, Ben's son, and I have been cooking since four in the mornin' to get food out to everyone.

**威尔**：根本不够吃，全十字街的青壮几乎都来了。我这会儿还得赶紧回去看看炖的汤好了没有，回见了！\
**Will**: But it still ain't enough. Almost everyone in the neighborhood's coming. Alright, I have to go make more soup. See you later!

**工人Ⅱ**：小叫醒工刚刚给的什么玩意儿？\
**Worker II**: Hey, what's that you got from the knocker-upper?

**工人Ⅲ**：不知道，照她的说法是拎起这被单一角，然后对着它吹口气。\
**Worker III**: An enchanted sheet, apparently. She told me to blow it when I need to use it.

**工人Ⅱ**：呼——！\
**Worker II**: *blow*

**工人Ⅱ**：好家伙，这被单刮起一小阵风。还挺凉快的！正合适咱们干活。\
**Worker II**: Would you look at that? It conjured a gust of wind! We can use this while we're workin'.

**工人Ⅲ**：我感觉眼前的雾气好像也被吹散了一点——呃、噗，好吧，就一点儿。\
**Worker III**: Yeah, it blows the smog away. Alright, well, sort of.

**小丽莎**：福葛先生——！福葛先生——！我也来了！！\
**Little Lisa**: Mr. Fog, Mr. Fog! I'm here to help!

**福葛先生**：噢……你……是之前在集市那个……？\
**Mr. Fog**: Oh, you. You're the girl from the market, aren't you?

**小丽莎**：对的，先生。\
**Little Lisa**: Yes, that's me.

**小丽莎**：先生不要伤心，大机器坏了可以修，就算修不好，运动会也还是可以办的呀——！\
**Little Lisa**: Let's try our best to fix the machine together. But there's no need to worry. Mr. Fog, we can still hold the exhibition even if we can't do it!

**福葛先生**：……\
**Mr. Fog**: ...

**福葛先生**：……运动会……嗯。\
**Mr. Fog**: The exhibition. Alright.

**无线电广播**：接下来，由我转播今天有关运动会会场的最新情况。\
**Radio Broadcast**: Next, introducing the London Uluru Exhibition Games.

**无线电广播**：截至目前，已有整整二十八个运动员报名本次运动会，本次运动会为期六天，每天会举行一个项目的冠军争夺……\
**Radio Broadcast**: So far, 28 players have registered for the six-day event, which will host one sport per day.

**工人Ⅰ**：来，大家一起搭把手——三、二、一——\
**Worker I**: Alright, everyone, let's push together! Three, two, one!

**无线电广播**：我们有许多居民自发组织在这里重建已经拆除了一半的场馆……\
**Radio Broadcast**: The residents of Cross Street have taken it upon themselves to rebuild the stadium.

**小丽莎**：嘻嘻……你画的这个不对，这个不是戴着金牌的反舌鸟，我这个才是。我们要庆祝它在唱歌比赛里拿了第一。\
**Little Lisa**: Hey, your painting's totally off theme. Look, mine's a mockingbird with a gold medal. It just won first place in the singing competition!

**淘气鬼弗洛狄**：唱歌比赛不对，你要画体育比赛，就像我这个，一条剑鱼，在我的想象中它有一条邮轮那么大。\
**Freddy the Rascal**: The Uluru games ain't got a singin' competition. You should've drawn somethin' more athletic, like my sailfish. It's the fastest swimmer in the world.

**无线电广播**：多新鲜啊！一脚踢开基金会，我们要举办一个自己的乌卢鲁运动会。\
**Radio Broadcast**: How exciting! Our very own Uluru Games without any interference from the Foundation!

**纸信圈儿**：牙仙女士——！\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Tooth Fairy!

**纸信圈儿**：我已经把所有报名参加运动会的运动员名单都整理好了，虽然……大多数已经走了，但是还是有一部分运动员愿意留下来，和我们待在一起。\
**Flutterpage**: I've made a list of all the athletes who signed up for the qualifiers. A lot of them have left, but some would like to stay for our exhibition.

**牙仙**：我这边也统计好了每天的到场人员，基本上都是按照之前购票申请的名额和座位来安排。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Good. And I've made a list of the daily attendees based on the tickets they bought for the qualifiers.

**牙仙**：福葛先生和宽檐帽先生，现在正在场外跟应急管理局和安保局的人沟通如何维护比赛期间的治安问题。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Mr. Fog and Mr. Brimley are discussing the possible security issues of the event with the Relief Centre staff and the police.

**牙仙**：没有想到，我们居然能按照原定日期开赛。\
**Tooth Fairy**: We may actually start the Games on the day the qualifiers were originally scheduled.

**牙仙**：鉴于这一切都过于临时，到时候可能会有更多先行无法预估的情况，我们都需要做好准备。\
**Tooth Fairy**: But, since this is all improvised, we'll probably encounter some unexpected problems as the Games continue. We need to be prepared.

**纸信圈儿**：是的——我知道。\
**Flutterpage**: Yeah, I know.

女孩慢慢从兴奋中拔出，眼神有些落寞地扫视着运动会会场。\
The girl's enthusiasm dims as she looks over the sports venue, eyes tinged with quiet regret.

**纸信圈儿**：唔……\
**Flutterpage**: *sigh*

**牙仙**：……你辛苦了，整理运动员报名表，也是一件很令人头疼的事，但是你完成得很好。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Thank you, Flutterpage. It must have taken a lot of effort to make the athlete list. You've done an excellent job.

**纸信圈儿**：……\
**Flutterpage**: ...

她依然在扫视着会场，似乎想要寻找什么。\
She continues to scan the venue, as if searching for something.

**牙仙**：所以，整理了这么多份，你看到想看的名字了吗？\
**Tooth Fairy**: So, you saw the whole athlete list. Did you see the name you were hoping for?

**纸信圈儿**：啊……！\
**Flutterpage**: Ah! How did you ...

**纸信圈儿**：……牙仙女士……我……\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Tooth Fairy, I ...

她皱着眉头嗫嚅着。\
She hesitates, her brow furrowed. Her lips are barely moving.

**宽檐帽**：——纸信圈儿！纸信圈儿！\
**Brimley**: Flutterpage! Flutterpage!

**宽檐帽**：来跟咱们和管理局解释一下，你那个裹在人们身上的白被单是什么原理——！\
**Brimley**: Come here. We need you to explain to the Relief Centre how your little sheets work!

女孩看着严肃的官方人员，有些踟蹰。\
The girl hesitates as she looks toward the somber officials.

**牙仙**：去吧，没关系。他们那边更着急，毕竟这可是关系到运动会能不能顺利举行的事。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Just go. They need you more than I do. Your explanation may decide whether the Games can be held.

**纸信圈儿**：——那，那牙仙女士，咱们回见！\
**Flutterpage**: Alright. I'll talk to you later!

女孩蹦跳着向会场大门的方向跑去。那里宽檐帽和福葛先生正抱着手等待着她。\
She skips excitedly toward the door of the venue, where Brimley and Mr. Fog await her arrival.

一个抱着木架的工人经过后，她的身影完全消失不见了。\
As a worker carrying a wooden frame passes, she disappears from view.

**牙仙**：你给自己换了一身新行头，要我说，非常合适。\
**Tooth Fairy**: You've got yourself a new outfit. It looks great on you.

黑暗中，走出一名瘦削高挑的女子。她的尖皮鞋整洁而矜持地点在地上。\
A tall, slim woman emerges from the shadows, her pointed leather shoes gliding along the floor with poised restraint.

**笃笃骨**：……呵，我也很喜欢你的大衣。\
**Willow**: Oh, I like your coat, too.

**牙仙**：谢谢。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Thank you.

**笃笃骨**：我那爱吃甜食、前两年送回老家庄园下葬的外婆生前也有一件跟你这一模一样的。\
**Willow**: My grandmother had one just like it. She died two years ago, had a proper sweet tooth, too.

**牙仙**：那我们肯定很聊得来。\
**Tooth Fairy**: We'd have got along well.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

**笃笃骨**：你怎么知道我藏在这里的？\
**Willow**: How did you know I was here?

**牙仙**：噢，不是我发现的，是我的“牙仙”们发现的。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Oh, I didn't until my toothfairies found you.

**笃笃骨**：给自己找到了一个很好的借口，以后所有不想承认的话题都可以落在你的小东西头上。\
**Willow**: Heh. So you have a whole jar of scapegoats who can take all the blame for you? How convenient.

**牙仙**：……你看上去心情好了一些，连嘲讽都变得有活力了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: You've pulled yourself together, haven't you? Even your sarcasm has become bitter again.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

**牙仙**：所以呢，怎么突然想要出门，来这里看看？\
**Tooth Fairy**: So, why are you here?

**笃笃骨**：呼吸呼吸“新鲜空气”。\
**Willow**: Just getting some fresh air.

**牙仙**：……\
**Tooth Fairy**: ...

二人一时无话，共同注视着眼前混乱的会场。有工人吆喝，有孩童嬉闹。\
The two of them remain silent as they observe the mayhem of the sports ground, workers shouting and children running back and forth.

**牙仙**：喜欢吗？这样的运动会。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Look at them. They're all so happy. What do you think?

**笃笃骨**：——这是我见过，最破烂、最简陋、参加人数最少、准备最凌乱的一届运动会，没有之一。\
**Willow**: I've never seen such a rudimentary, disorderly, and poorly prepared event in my life.

**牙仙**：是的，它是一个半成品。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Well of course, it's totally amateur.

**牙仙**：但它仍然是一场运动会。\
**Tooth Fairy**: But it's built on enthusiasm and sportsmanship.

**牙仙**：有运动员在这里奔跑，有观众在这里呐喊，有无数人的精神凝聚在这里，释放他们的热情。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Athletes will go head-to-head, spectators will cheer, and the stadium will be lit up by the energy they release together.

**牙仙**：它的迷人就在于，它残缺，但它包容，它即将召开。\
**Tooth Fairy**: It's imperfect, yes, but it's inclusive and unstoppable. And that's what makes it special.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

**笃笃骨**：……哼。\
**Willow**: Hmph.

笃笃骨的手里，捏着一张被揉皱的报名表。\
Willow holds a crumpled registration form in her hand.

## LD-17 开幕式 / Opening Ceremony

威廉叔叔，康蒂婶婶，小玛丽，老汉斯……\
Uncle Bill, Aunt Connie, Little Mary, Old Harold ...

十字街的居民们齐齐地站在台前，他们还手执锤头和木锯，老汉斯悄悄地将铁锹踢到了身后。\
The people of Cross Street stand gathered at the front of the stage, hammers and saws in their hands. Old Harold discreetly moves a shovel out of sight.

金丝绵雀在树上神经质地频繁扭着头，好奇地盯着这群于阴沉的冬日中聚集起来的人们。\
Perched on a tree, a canary nervously swivels its head to watch the crowd assembled on this bleak winter day.

**宽檐帽**：由我来吧，女士。\
**Brimley**: Leave it to me, darl.

牙仙微微颔首，宽檐帽便走上了木头临时搭建起来的主席台上。\
Tooth Fairy gives a slight nod, and Brimley ascends the makeshift wooden podium.

**宽檐帽**：测试，测试。\
**Brimley**: Testing. Testing.

**宽檐帽**：女士们，先生们，今天是乌卢鲁运动会预选赛举办的日子。\
**Brimley**: Ladies and gentlemen, your attention, please! Today marks the beginning of the London Uluru Exhibition Games.

**宽檐帽**：但同时，令人郁闷的，也是个有雾的日子。\
**Brimley**: As you can see, the weather isn't looking great. The smog still sits heavy in the sky.

台下的人们看着宽檐帽，脸上还留着水泥与煤灰的痕迹。\
The crowd beneath the platform looks up at Brimley, cement stains and coal smudges on their faces.

**宽檐帽**：没有风，没有阳光，天阴冷得吓人，我的帽檐上也潮潮的，总之是令人不舒坦。\
**Brimley**: There's no wind, no sunshine, no warmth, and even my brim is soggy from the damp. It's truly miserable out here.

**宽檐帽**：没有辉煌雄伟的赛场，参赛的运动员人数也令人难以启齿。\
**Brimley**: On top of that, the stadium's shabby, and we only have a limited number of athletes.

**宽檐帽**：这是一届令人失望的、不被人看好的乌卢鲁运动会预选赛。\
**Brimley**: To many, these games would be seen as disappointing.

**宽檐帽**：但是，各位！即便失去了基金会的资金支持，我们仍旧靠我们的双手和对运动的热情，在几天之内，搭建起了一个标准规格的赛场！\
**Brimley**: However, even without the support of the Foundation, we've managed to rebuild this stadium with nothing but our own hands and determination!

**宽檐帽**：身为一个合格的政府官员的助手，我能肯定地说，我们搭建的赛场是符合各类法条的检验标准的，它足以得到基金会的认可！\
**Brimley**: I've confirmed that our stadium meets all the standards required by the government, and there's no doubt that it matches the Foundation's, too!

**宽檐帽**：并且，通过各类业内人士与民间爱好者的帮助，我们还组建起了一个足够专业的工作团队。\
**Brimley**: As for the operation of our Games, we've built a reliable team consisting of various Uluru professionals and supporters.

**宽檐帽**：他们正在赛场的各处，为预选赛的正常举办做着各类准备工作。\
**Brimley**: They are currently in every corner of the stadium, working their hardest to prepare for the upcoming event.

**宽檐帽**：这些人将成为本届乌卢鲁运动会预选赛的脊梁，撑起整场比赛，保证预选赛能够顺利进行。\
**Brimley**: They will be our backbone, supporting the entire Games to ensure that everything runs smoothly.

**宽檐帽**：所以，我认为，它是一届充满热情的、永不服输的乌卢鲁运动会预选赛！\
**Brimley**: As we all come together, I believe the passion of our Games will burn as hot as the sacred fire of Uluru itself!

**宽檐帽**：现在，我宣布——\
**Brimley**: So, without further ado, I hereby declare ...

**宽檐帽**：乌卢鲁运动会伦敦预选赛，正式——开始！\
**Brimley**: That the London Uluru Exhibition Games have begun!

人们如热锅上的滚水珠般，喧闹且忙碌着。\
The crowd bustles and chatters like a flock of birds.

纷至沓来的问题围绕着牙仙、宽檐帽和纸信圈儿三人。\
Tooth Fairy, Brimley, and Flutterpage are quickly bombarded by a flood of questions.

**裁判组成员Ⅰ**：牙仙小姐！叩门飞匙赛的裁判不够了！弗朗茨的时间跟别的项目撞上了！\
**Judge I**: Ms. Tooth Fairy! We don't have enough judges for the Winged Key Archery! Frantz has been put on to umpire two events at the same time, so he left to do the other one!

**牙仙**：不够了？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Two events at the same time?

**牙仙**：他是明天那个项目的裁判，他记错时间了，叫他回来。\
**Tooth Fairy**: The other event starts tomorrow. He must've mixed up the schedule. Get him to come back.

**广播声**：请参加1500米负重竞速的选手到第三准备区集合，请参加1500米负重竞速的选手到第三准备区集合。\
**Broadcast**: All athletes participating in the 1500-Meter Weighted Run, please report to the third preparation area. I repeat, please report to the third preparation area.

**参赛选手Ⅰ**：您好，我的号码牌丢了，能再给我一张吗？\
**Player I**: Umm. Excuse me. I-I lost my name tag. Can I get a new one?

**牙仙**：带着你的证件，直走左转，去证件补办处找一名叫“纸信圈儿”的小女孩补办。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Certainly. Go straight ahead, and take the first left to get to the player office. There's a girl called Flutterpage in there. Show her your ID, and she'll give you a new tag.

**裁判组成员Ⅱ**：来吧，好兄弟，我带你去。\
**Judge II**: I'll take you there. Follow me, friend.

**参赛选手Ⅰ**：好，好，谢谢。\
**Player I**: Sure. Thanks.

**宽檐帽**：哦哦哦！等一下，“好兄弟”，我怎么从来没有见过你？\
**Brimley**: Oi, hold on a minute. "Friend," why haven't I seen you before?

宽檐帽有些疑惑地盯着这名裁判组的成员，一把扯过他掖在大衣内的裁判证。\
Brimley examines the judge suspiciously before pulling his ID card directly from the inside of his coat.

**宽檐帽**：这个证件是伪造的，安保人员！\
**Brimley**: This ID is fake. Security!

**裁判组成员Ⅱ**：我只是一名爱好者罢了，一切好说行吗？放开我！我……\
**Judge II**: I-I'm just a big fan. Please, don't kick me out! I just—

负责安保的志愿者们闻声赶来，将伪装成裁判的狂热爱好者带了出去。\
The volunteer security team quickly swoops in and removes the impersonator.

其中一人趁机与宽檐帽耳语了几句。\
One of them whispers a few words to Brimley.

**宽檐帽**：牙仙女士。\
**Brimley**: Tooth Fairy, my darl.

**牙仙**：怎么了，安保队长？\
**Tooth Fairy**: What is it, Head of Security?

**宽檐帽**：有人告诉我，一位绅士伙计想要在会场内张贴广告语。\
**Brimley**: I've been told that a mate of ours would like to post some fliers in the stadium.

**牙仙**：我们之前已经与别人达成了合约，恐怕你得拒绝他。\
**Tooth Fairy**: We already have a sponsor. I'm afraid you'll have to turn him down.

**宽檐帽**：是福葛伙计。\
**Brimley**: By mate, I mean Arthur.

顺着宽檐帽转去的方向，牙仙在会场的入口看到了一条白底黑字的横幅。\
Tooth Fairy glances over to where Brimley is looking and catches sight of a black-and-white banner at the entrance to the venue.

“吸雾有害健康。”\
Smog Kills.

**牙仙**：他一直和他那个坏掉的机器坐在横幅下吗？\
**Tooth Fairy**: Has he been sitting all this time under that banner with his machine?

**宽檐帽**：是的，福葛伙计从运动会开始时便守在那里，借由那台破铁块，向每一位前来参加运动会的人展示吸入过多雾气的后果。\
**Brimley**: Yeah. He's using it to show everyone what could happen if they breathe in too much smog.

**牙仙**：是该说他立场不坚定，还是该说他过于固执？\
**Tooth Fairy**: I don't know if I should call him wavering in his principles or completely stubborn in them.

**宽檐帽**：福葛伙计一直都是一位真心为选民服务的政府官员，正直地、坚韧地、强硬地影响着他身边的人。\
**Brimley**: Arthur's always been a righteous official. He truly cares about the people. He's tough, tenacious, and has a powerful ability to influence others.

**牙仙**：你是位天生的发言人。\
**Tooth Fairy**: You sound more like an official than he does.

牙仙转向在会场中备赛的运动员和为运动员呐喊助威的观众们。\
Tooth Fairy looks over at the athletes preparing to race and the crowd cheering them on enthusiastically.

**观众Ⅰ**：加油！加油！\
**Spectator I**: Come on! Go for it!

**观众Ⅱ**：第一名！！！\
**Spectator II**: First place! Yes!

**观众Ⅲ**：呜——呜——\
**Spectator III**: Waahhh ... No ...

**参赛选手Ⅱ**：谢谢！谢谢～\
**Player II**: Thank you! Thank you!

正准备起跑的运动员向观众们做出了飞吻的回应，又获得了一阵欢呼声。\
The athlete blows kisses at the spectators, triggering another wave of excitement.

**牙仙**：这些雾是阻挡不了人们对运动的热情的，不论如何，人们都要将乌卢鲁运动会举办下去。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Not even the smog can stop the people's enthusiasm for sports. No matter the obstacle, they will always find a way to enjoy it.

**牙仙**：他还不愿接受纸信圈儿的小被单吗？\
**Tooth Fairy**: I suppose Mr. Fog is still refusing to take one of Flutterpage's sheets?

**宽檐帽**：按照福葛伙计的意思，身为雾行者是不可向浓雾低头的，他不会逃避，而是会“迎战”。\
**Brimley**: Of course, he is. Arthur said he'd never run away from the smog. As Fogwalker, he has to "confront" it.

**宽檐帽**：笨拙的福葛伙计……\
**Brimley**: He's stubborn, just as you said.

**广播声**：请参加自由祭祀的选手到第五准备区集合，请参加自由祭祀的选手到第五准备区集合。\
**Broadcast**: Floor Ritual competitors, please report to the fifth preparation area. I repeat, please report to the fifth preparation area.

**宽檐帽**：哦！是笃笃骨女士的项目……\
**Brimley**: Oh! That's Ms. O'Hagan's event.

**牙仙**：嗯。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Yeah.

**宽檐帽**：她会上场吗？\
**Brimley**: Do you think she'll show up?

**纸信圈儿**：牙仙女士，宽檐帽先生，你们听到了吗？自由祭祀要开始了！\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Tooth Fairy, Mr. Brimley, did you hear that? The Floor Ritual's about to start!

**纸信圈儿**：笃笃骨在哪里呢？\
**Flutterpage**: But where's Ms. Willow?

牙仙与宽檐帽对视了一眼，牙仙看不到宽檐帽的眼神，但她从帽檐的微动作中感受到了一些迷茫。\
Tooth Fairy looks at Brimley. Though he has no eyes for her to read, the slight shifting of his brim carries a sense of trepidation.

二人似乎都不知该对这个孩子说些什么，不知该点燃她的希望，还是戳破她的幻想。\
Neither knows how to respond to the child, hesitating between igniting her hopes and destroying her dreams.

亦或是正中她的下怀？\
Or perhaps the truth is exactly what she's hoping for?

**牙仙**：你去自由祭祀的会场那边看看吧，纸信圈儿。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Go check the Floor Ritual venue, Flutterpage.

**纸信圈儿**：去干嘛呢？难道笃笃骨会在那里吗？\
**Flutterpage**: What for? Is Ms. Willow there?

孩子似乎猜中了牙仙的言外之意，她直直地盯着牙仙的眼睛。\
She looks directly at Tooth Fairy. Her eyes widen as they begin to sparkle.

**纸信圈儿**：难道笃笃骨会在那里吗？\
**Flutterpage**: She's there, isn't she?!

**牙仙**：不去看看的话，怎么会知道呢。\
**Tooth Fairy**: You'll have to go there to find out.

牙仙微微笑着。\
She can't help but give a slight smile.

**宽檐帽**：“证件补办处”这里由我值守更好些，你去吧，纸信圈儿。\
**Brimley**: I'll cover for you at the player office. Just go, little tacker.

**牙仙**：去吧。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Go on, then.

孩子的脸上先是冒出了笑容，却又现出了一些迟疑。\
Flutterpage starts to smile, but a flicker of doubt quickly clouds her expression.

**纸信圈儿**：这次……我不会再带给笃笃骨坏消息了。\
**Flutterpage**: This time, I won't disappoint her.

**纸信圈儿**：我真的为她带来了一场盛会，它不是我梦里咬一口却没有味道的烤鸡，它真实得不能更真实了。\
**Flutterpage**: I've brought her a real game. No need to climb the tower and hide away anymore. This is real.

像是下定决心一般，孩子向牙仙和宽檐帽挥了挥手。\
She raises her hand and waves to Tooth Fairy and Brimley, a determined look on her face.

**纸信圈儿**：那边见！\
**Flutterpage**: See you later!

言罢，纸信圈儿便跑走了。\
With that, Flutterpage turns and runs off.

第五准备区，候场的自由祭祀运动员们在各自做着热身运动。\
At the fifth preparation area, the Floor Ritual competitors are warming up.

**2401号选手**：看看这个场地，随便哪所女子学校的操场也比这个好，这届乌卢鲁运动会预选赛真是有趣。\
**Player No. 2401**: Look at this place. You could find a better venue at any school in the city. These Games are really something.

**卡洛琳**：这是在几天的时间内搭好的，我们也不能要求太多了。\
**Caroline Bartley**: They built it in a matter of days. We can't ask for much.

**2401号选手**：哦，天呐，卡洛琳女士，您好……\
**Player No. 2401**: Oh my! It's an honor to meet you, Ms. Bartley.

2401号赶紧擦擦手，然后向卡洛琳伸去。\
The competitor hurriedly wipes her hands before extending one to Caroline.

**卡洛琳**：练习的时候要小心了，不要磕到自己。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Take care warming up. You wouldn't want to get hurt just before the competition.

**2401号选手**：谢谢，您真温柔。\
**Player No. 2401**: You're very kind. Thank you.

一名戴着志愿者工作证的工作人员从门口走了进来。\
A staff member with a volunteer ID strides in from the doorway.

**志愿者Ⅰ**：请各位参加自由祭祀的选手确认上场顺序，比赛马上就要开始了。\
**Volunteer I**: Floor Ritual competitors, the event will start in one minute. Please confirm your numbers, as I will be calling you to enter the floor in numerical order.

**志愿者Ⅰ**：2401号选手，请上场。2402、2403号选手，请在这里候场。\
**Volunteer I**: Competitor No. 2401, please enter the floor. Competitors 2402 and 2403, please wait in the locker room.

**2402号选手**：祝你好运。\
**Player No. 2402**: Good luck!

几名候场的运动员向2401号选手送上祝福，2401号向众人挥手告别后，就走向了赛场。\
The first competitor receives a few well-wishes before waving goodbye as she makes her way to the competition floor.

听到了比赛开始的消息，卡洛琳停下了热身运动。\
Now that the event has begun, Caroline stops warming up.

**卡洛琳**：夏洛特呢？\
**Caroline Bartley**: Hmm. What about Charlotte?

**笃笃骨**：呼——\
**Willow**: *deep breath*

**卡洛琳**：夏洛特，你果然在这里，这么多年，你的习惯一直没变。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Charlotte, you're here. I knew you wouldn't be able to stay away. You haven't changed a bit.

**笃笃骨**：嗯？\
**Willow**: Hmm?

笃笃骨停下了正在做的伸展运动。\
Willow pauses in the middle of her stretch.

**笃笃骨**：你有什么事？\
**Willow**: What do you want from me?

**卡洛琳**：什么事？你忘记挑战那回事了吗？\
**Caroline Bartley**: What do I want? Have you forgotten about the challenge?

**卡洛琳**：你是几号？\
**Caroline Bartley**: What's your number?

**笃笃骨**：与你有什么关系……哦，我明白了，越是高贵的人做起志愿者来就越迷人。\
**Willow**: I don't think that's any of your concern, or are you trying to win over the organizers with a little goody-two-shoes act? The ever-so-helpful competitor-turned-volunteer, Ms. Bartley?

**卡洛琳**：我真不懂……你怎么能源源不断地吐出这么多刻薄的话。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Oh, I didn't know you could be so sarcastic.

**笃笃骨**：你还需要接着适应呢。\
**Willow**: You better get used to it.

**卡洛琳**：是吗？你以后还会与我讲许多话吗？\
**Caroline Bartley**: Really? You mean we'll chat again in the future?

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

笃笃骨别过头去。\
Willow turns her head away from her.

**笃笃骨**：我不再是之前那个夏洛特了，别老是过来套近乎。\
**Willow**: I'm not the Charlotte you used to know. Stop trying to bond with me.

卡洛琳向夏洛特走了过去。\
Caroline walks toward her.

**卡洛琳**：但我觉得没有区别呀，夏洛特。\
**Caroline Bartley**: But you are the Charlotte I used to know.

**卡洛琳**：你一直就是我追寻的那只黑天鹅，是你在赛场的身影为我带来了成为自由祭祀运动员的梦想，可你成为冠军后便销声匿迹了……\
**Caroline Bartley**: You're still that black swan I've always chased after. When I saw your performance, the grace, the beauty of it, it inspired me to become a Floor Ritualist. But you just disappeared after you became champion.

**卡洛琳**：不过……呵呵～\
**Caroline Bartley**: Well, as long as you're back ... Heh heh.

**笃笃骨**：有什么好笑的？\
**Willow**: What's so funny?

卡洛琳坦然地看着笃笃骨，脸上带着微微的笑意。\
Caroline looks at Willow with a quiet composure, her lips forming a slight smile.

**卡洛琳**：赛场见。\
**Caroline Bartley**: See you on the floor.

简短地告别后，卡洛琳便回到了候场区。\
Caroline heads back to the preparation area.

**志愿者Ⅰ**：2406号选手，卡洛琳，请上场。\
**Volunteer I**: Player No. 2406, Caroline Bartley, please enter the floor.

志愿者的声音从房间内传出，人声因为墙壁的阻隔而显得失真。\
The sound of the volunteer's voice filters into the room, muffled and distorted by the walls.

笃笃骨跺了跺略微僵硬的右腿，发出了“笃笃”的声音。\
Willow stamps her slightly stiff right leg.

**笃笃骨**：我也该回去了。\
**Willow**: Time for me to head in, too.

**笃笃骨**：请让一下。\
**Willow**: Excuse me.

笃笃骨来到了观众席，坐在一个角落中。\
She finds her way to the spectator seats, settling into a corner.

卡洛琳踏着轻盈的脚步上了场，向裁判们示意后，她轻轻地抚摸了放于场前的“迪吉里木”，然后回到场中，摆出预备的姿势。\
Caroline gracefully strides onto the floor, pausing to give a gentle bow to the judges. Then, she brushes her hand across the didgeriwood, and positions herself in the center, ready to begin.

**广播声**：2406号，卡洛琳，请开始。\
**Broadcast**: Player No. 2406, Caroline Bartley, whenever you're ready.

卡洛琳舞蹈了起来，与此同时，“迪吉里木”接收到了卡洛琳灌输而来的能量，也开始了它的奏鸣。\
Caroline starts to dance. Receiving her channeled energy, the didgeriwood produces a rich, resonant sound.

## LD-18 灰黄的对话 / Hazy Memories

第1日。\
Day 1

**夏洛特**：老师，这是什么？\
**Charlotte**: What's this, Ms. Raven?

**乌鸦教练**：你的密友，你心底的溪流……它的根从澳大利亚伸到了你的脚心，它与你一起共舞。\
**Coach Raven**: A seed that will settle in your heart and soon grow to be your closest friend. Its roots will stretch all the way from Australia to the soles of your feet, and together, you will make the music to your Floor Ritual.

**乌鸦教练**：好好听听它，听听你跟它说了什么，听啊，听！\
**Coach Raven**: Now, my dear, listen closely. Listen to what it has to say. Listen!

**乌鸦教练**：摸它，扼住它，要让它知道你的脾性。\
**Coach Raven**: Hold it. Feel it. Let it know who you are.

**乌鸦教练**：它不是木头，是镜子，远古的人们传给我们的镜子。\
**Coach Raven**: It isn't just a piece of wood, but a mouthpiece passed down through the ages.

**乌鸦教练**：有了它，你才能知道，你祭祀时，那些神灵究竟听到的是什么东西！\
**Coach Raven**: It allows us to understand what our god hears during the ritual!

**夏洛特**：但它摸上去和普通的木头没有区别……\
**Charlotte**: It doesn't look all that special to me.

**乌鸦教练**：嘿嘿……你要先跟它说话啊，用神秘术说，它只能听懂这个！\
**Coach Raven**: Haha, silly girl. If you want it to speak, you must greet it with your arcane skill first. It's the only language it'll understand!

**夏洛特**：嗯——\
**Charlotte**: Alright.

**夏洛特**：它回应我了！\
**Charlotte**: It's responding!

**迪吉里木**：叮～～～叮～～～～铛！！！！！\
**Didgeriwood**: *#$%^&*&*)#@*

**夏洛特**：真难听……\
**Charlotte**: Ugh, that sounds awful.

**乌鸦教练**：不是它说的难听，是你说的难听。\
**Coach Raven**: That's because you greeted it awfully.

**夏洛特**：您是说……只有稳定的神秘学波动，才能使它奏出好听的乐曲？\
**Charlotte**: I greeted it awfully? You mean the fluctuation of my arcane skill wasn't stable enough?

**乌鸦教练**：是的……对，你要先好好跟它说话才行……\
**Coach Raven**: Yes. Speak to it politely, and it'll respond with politeness.

第7日。\
Day 7

**夏洛特**：呜呜……老师……我好痛……\
**Charlotte**: *weep* Ms. Raven, that hurts.

**乌鸦教练**：一条人群熙攘的朝圣路，一条必经之路，你只能一步一步地踱。\
**Coach Raven**: The path of pilgrimage is full of thorns. It offers no shortcuts. You must make your way, inch by inch.

**乌鸦教练**：否则无法抵达那聚光之地，荣耀圣所。\
**Coach Raven**: Otherwise, you'll never reach the sanctuary of glory—the place where all the lights gather.

**乌鸦教练**：也无法为人所知。\
**Coach Raven**: And you'll die a nobody.

**夏洛特**：人群熙攘……是不是我现在多进行练习，就会快点脱离痛苦？\
**Charlotte**: Full of thorns. So, will I be freed from pain if I keep training?

**乌鸦教练**：来吧，来吧，用你的头紧紧地贴着胫骨，模仿那神子的姿势。\
**Coach Raven**: Shush. Press your head against your shin, just as the divine son did.

**夏洛特**：嗯……呃——\
**Charlotte**: Okay. Ugh!

**乌鸦教练**：贴好……紧紧贴着！\
**Coach Raven**: Closer! I want that head tight against your shin!

**夏洛特**：嗯————\
**Charlotte**: Ugh!!

**乌鸦教练**：越紧越好。\
**Coach Raven**: The tighter, the better!

**夏洛特**：好————\
**Charlotte**: Yes, Miss ... Ah!

第93日。\
Day 93

**乌鸦教练**：迷茫，迷茫从你的发丝滴了下来，我感受到了你的悲伤。\
**Coach Raven**: Confusion, sadness, I can see it all over you.

**夏洛特**：学校里的同学……他们嘲笑我……说我只会用特权来逃避学习……\
**Charlotte**: My classmates were making fun of me. They said I was using the training to avoid my duties.

**夏洛特**：他们说我不来上课，不参加学校的运动会，也不跟他们一起去夏令营……\
**Charlotte**: They said I never do anything with them. I've skipped classes, sports days, and the summer outing.

**夏洛特**：每天只会在这间练习室里跳些奇怪的东西，变些戏法……\
**Charlotte**: They said that all I do is train to be a clown in a show.

**夏洛特**：老师，哪怕只有一天，我能跟同学们一起去做点别的吗？\
**Charlotte**: M-Ms. Raven, can I take a break, just for today? I want to spend time with my classmates.

**乌鸦教练**：不行，不行，你与我约定过。\
**Coach Raven**: No, no. You made a promise, remember?

**夏洛特**：因为我要与全世界的运动员们比拼，一天都不能放松，我的一切付出都是为了那块金牌。\
**Charlotte**: Yes. I promised to focus on my training and never slack, no matter what. If I want to be a champion, I need to be able to beat every other Floor Ritualist in the world.

**夏洛特**：每滴汗和每滴泪都将铺成我通向冠军的路。\
**Charlotte**: Every tear, every drop of sweat, will pave my path to the podium.

**乌鸦教练**：你记得，你都记得。\
**Coach Raven**: So, you do remember it, every word.

**乌鸦教练**：神灵只能听见最虔诚的声音，最虔诚，最虔诚……你需得将每时每刻都奉献给它，你的心，你的血肉，你的……从这里，到这里。\
**Coach Raven**: Our god can only hear the most faithful prayers. Yes, only the most faithful. You must offer everything you have to him. Your heart, your flesh, from here to here.

老师的手指从夏洛特的头划到了脚。\
She traces a path from Charlotte's head to her toes with her finger.

**乌鸦教练**：不然，就会有人排在你的前头，神灵绝不会看你一眼……\
**Coach Raven**: If you can't do that, you'll be surpassed and never win the attention of our god.

**乌鸦教练**：就像你完全不存在……你就会完全不存在……你想这样吗？\
**Coach Raven**: If that happens, you'll be completely forgotten, like you never existed. Is that what you want?

**夏洛特**：不想。\
**Charlotte**: No.

**乌鸦教练**：那……你为什么还不开始？\
**Coach Raven**: Then what are you waiting for? Begin.

第569日。\
Day 569

**乌鸦教练**：哒，哒哒，哒……不，不行。\
**Coach Raven**: Tsk, tsk. No, not like that.

**夏洛特**：这个角度是可以得分的！\
**Charlotte**: Why? This element will score me points!

**乌鸦教练**：还不够！\
**Coach Raven**: Yes, but not enough!

**夏洛特**：凭什么不够？你去修订比赛标准好了！\
**Charlotte**: Not enough? Then, they should revise their scoring system!

**乌鸦教练**：它不够，不够！不完美，不虔诚！我看不到。你是不想，还是不能？\
**Coach Raven**: By "not enough," I mean it's imperfect, unfaithful! Our god won't hear you. Are you unwilling to try a better element or simply unable to?

**夏洛特**：呵！做这个动作就像走路一样简单。\
**Charlotte**: Oh, please! I can do any element without even trying!

**乌鸦教练**：来，来，让神灵看看。\
**Coach Raven**: Then show it to our god!

**夏洛特**：知道了！别再重复了！\
**Charlotte**: I've got it! Stop nagging me!

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

**笃笃骨**：呵，我沉浸得太深了，还以为是……\
**Willow**: Heh, I suppose I got carried away. This applause isn't for me.

**笃笃骨**：那是我本该拥有的。\
**Willow**: But it should be.

笃笃骨揉揉眉心，表情凝重地看着场内接受众人致意的卡洛琳。\
Willow rubs her brow, a heavy expression on her face as she peers at Caroline. She's being showered with applause.

**笃笃骨**：什么时候开始走神的？大概是从看到卡洛琳那连脚尖的弧度都堪称完美的动作那时起……\
**Willow**: What distracted me? It must've been that graceful element that Caroline finished perfectly. She had it down to the smallest detail.

**笃笃骨**：在这方面的要求，我们谁都不比谁低，也正因如此……\
**Willow**: In that way, we're alike. Sticklers for detail. That's why ...

笃笃骨眯了眯眼，看着场内的卡洛琳。\
She squints as her eyes continue to follow Caroline.

**卡洛琳**：谢谢，谢谢大家！\
**Caroline Bartley**: Thank you! Thank you, everyone!

**笃笃骨**：我才会如此躁动。\
