**Willow**: I'm feeling so restless.

行礼过后，卡洛琳便退场了。\
With a respectful salute, Caroline exits the floor.

**广播声**：2407号，安娜，请开始。\
**Broadcast**: Player No. 2407, Anna Smith, please enter the field.

名为安娜的运动员上场，并做好了开始的准备。\
The ritualist named Anna makes her way to the floor and gets into position.

**卡洛琳**：夏洛特，我跳得怎么样？\
**Caroline Bartley**: What did you think, Charlotte?

卡洛琳从笃笃骨的身后拍了拍她的肩。\
Caroline pats Willow's shoulder from behind.

**笃笃骨**：能看出来这几年还是在进行训练的。\
**Willow**: Well, you certainly haven't skimped on your training these past years.

**卡洛琳**：就只是这样吗？\
**Caroline Bartley**: That's it?

笃笃骨昂着头，睨着卡洛琳。\
Willow shoots Caroline a sharp look.

**笃笃骨**：比当年那个9岁的小孩好。\
**Willow**: You're better than when you were nine. I'll give you that.

**卡洛琳**：哈哈～\
**Caroline Bartley**: Haha!

**卡洛琳**：不过……\
**Caroline Bartley**: But ...

卡洛琳走到了观众席的围栏前。\
Caroline steps toward the railing of the spectator area.

**卡洛琳**：这么浓的雾，你真的能看清我的动作吗?\
**Caroline Bartley**: Are you sure you saw my performance clearly? The smog's rather heavy.

笃笃骨和卡洛琳一起向雾中望去，浓雾之中，那名叫做安娜的运动员正起舞着。\
Side by side, Willow and Caroline peer through the dense smog as they watch Anna perform her routine.

另一边。\
Meanwhile, on the opposite side.

**牙仙**：纸信圈儿。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Flutterpage.

**纸信圈儿**：牙仙女士，宽檐帽先生！你们来啦！\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Tooth Fairy, Mr. Brimley! Good timin'!

**宽檐帽**：我们来得还算及时吧？运动会的好帮手是不会错过笃笃骨小姐的表演的！\
**Brimley**: Just in time, eh? Well, we wouldn't want to miss Ms. Willow's performance, now, would we?

**纸信圈儿**：现在这名运动员叫安娜，下一个就该笃笃骨啦，但是，我什么都看不见呀。\
**Flutterpage**: The lady doin' her routine right now is called Anna. It should be Ms. Willow next, but I can hardly see a thing.

**牙仙**：雾确实有点太浓了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: True. The smog's too heavy.

**牙仙**：希望笃笃骨上场的时候雾会散去一些。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Hopefully, it'll clear before Ms. Willow comes out.

这时，“迪吉里木”的奏乐戛然而止。\
Suddenly, the didgeriwood's song comes to a grinding halt.

**宽檐帽**：音乐呢？\
**Brimley**: What's wrong?

浓雾中的选手停止了舞蹈，并向裁判组请示着什么。\
Anna stops mid-routine and gestures toward the judges. Her mouth is moving.

观众席开始骚乱起来。\
An unease spreads among the crowd.

**观众Ⅰ**：她怎么了？\
**Spectator I**: Why'd she stop?

**观众Ⅱ**：看这个手势，是申请了暂停。\
**Spectator II**: I think she's requesting a timeout.

**观众Ⅲ**：暂停？她不想参加乌卢鲁运动会了吗？\
**Spectator III**: A time-out? Is she hurt?

安娜离开了赛场，观众们讨论着现在的情况。\
As Anna walks away from the floor, the crowd buzzes with speculation.

一段时间之后，广播声响了起来。\
After some time, the speakers crackle to life with an announcement.

**广播声**：滋滋——请安静，请安静……现在播报来自裁判组的通报。\
**Broadcast**: *buzz* Silence, please. An announcement from the Floor Ritual judges.

**广播声**：由于——滋——不可抗力的影响——滋滋——\
**Broadcast**: Due to ... *buzz* ... force majeure ... *buzz* ...

**广播声**：安娜选手滋——申请了暂停比赛——经过裁判组的商讨——比赛暂停。\
**Broadcast**: Player No. 2407, Anna Smith ... requested suspension ... *buzz* ... After discussion ... the judges have decided to ... suspend the game.

**纸信圈儿**：暂停了？那笃笃骨怎么办？我们看不到笃笃骨了吗？\
**Flutterpage**: Suspended? What about Ms. Willow?! Will she not get to compete?

听到了广播的消息，一些心急的观众起身准备离场，但仍有观众坚持留在原地。\
A number of spectators start to leave, while others stay put.

**观众Ⅰ**：怎么能暂停？我们好不容易才办起来的！她怎么能退缩？\
**Spectator I**: Suspended?! We gave everything to hold these Games! How could she just back out like this?!

**观众Ⅲ**：我还听说，叩门飞匙赛那边有运动员撞到墙了。\
**Spectator III**: I heard that a Winged Key Archery player got injured. Maybe that's why.

**观众Ⅱ**：走吗？后面没有了吗？我还没有看够。\
**Spectator II**: What, so we're supposed to just leave? The Games have hardly begun!

**纸信圈儿**：牙仙女士……怎么办？下一名就是笃笃骨了……这样的话太可惜了……\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Tooth Fairy, what should we do? Ms. Willow was next. It'll be such a shame if she can't play.

**牙仙**：……\
**Tooth Fairy**: ...

牙仙看着暗黄的浓雾，叹了口气。\
Tooth Fairy looks into the murky yellow smog and sighs.

## LD-19 雾中独舞 / Dancing in the Smog

**卡洛琳**：你听到了吗？比赛暂停了。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Did you hear that? The Games have been suspended.

**笃笃骨**：嗯。\
**Willow**: Yes.

卡洛琳走回了笃笃骨的身边。\
Caroline walks back to Willow's side.

**卡洛琳**：那我们今天先回去等通知吧？也许等雾散去，比赛会继续的。\
**Caroline Bartley**: I suppose we should head home and await further notice. Maybe the Games will continue once the smog clears.

浓雾中，会场上似乎有工作人员在收拾着什么东西。\
The workers appear to be clearing up something from the floor.

**笃笃骨**：那这几天我们的付出算什么？\
**Willow**: What, go home and spit in the faces of everyone who worked so hard to make this happen?

**卡洛琳**：嗯？\
**Caroline Bartley**: Hmm?

四周的观众纷纷起身，决定离开这个黯然失色的盛会。\
More and more spectators get to their feet as they prepare to leave.

**笃笃骨**：……不。\
**Willow**: No.

**卡洛琳**：不？\
**Caroline Bartley**: What do you mean, "no"?

**笃笃骨**：我不想再等了。\
**Willow**: I won't wait any longer.

说完，笃笃骨便直接离开了观众席，走向裁判组的帐篷。\
Willow turns and strides directly toward the judges' tent.

**卡洛琳**：夏洛特……\
**Caroline Bartley**: Charlotte ...

看着笃笃骨走向裁判组的背影，卡洛琳明白了她的意思，一股冲动涌上心头，她转身面向观众席。\
Realizing Willow's intent, a sudden impulse takes hold of her as she spins to face the stands.

**观众Ⅳ**：扫兴！这破雾！\
**Spectator IV**: Damn this bloody smog!

一些观众摸索着扶手，准备从观众席走下。\
A few spectators reach for the railings as they get ready to leave.

**卡洛琳**：各位，请等一下，比赛还没有结束！\
**Caroline Bartley**: Wait, everyone! The Games aren't over yet!

**观众Ⅳ**：都没有运动员会上场了，我们还留在这里干什么？\
**Spectator IV**: But the competitors aren't even competing! What's the point of staying?

**观众Ⅴ**：就该让我上去给他们跳一段！\
**Audience Member V**: *sigh* Why don't I go and dance on the floor instead?

**广播声**：滋滋——\
**Broadcast**: *buzz*

**广播声**：请等一下，笃笃骨选手……\
**Broadcast**: Everyone, please return to your seats. Player No. 2408, Willow.

**观众Ⅳ**：什么？\
**Spectator IV**: What?

笃笃骨那黑色的身影，已然在会场中站定。\
Willow's dark silhouette now stands firm at the center of the floor.

如第一日那般，她抚上了场前的“迪吉里木”。\
Just as she did all those years ago, she touches the didgeriwood at the front of the arena.

**笃笃骨**：蛰居十年，日夜与自负相伴……这是只有我自己才知道的滋味，由舌尖至心底。\
**Willow**: I've lived in seclusion for ten years. Trained alone with nothing but the pain in my leg and my own arrogance.

人们对乌卢鲁的期盼之声源源不断地传递至她的耳廓。\
The sounds of people's hopes for Uluru flow steadily into her ears.

**笃笃骨**：我要起舞……并不需要他人的评判。\
**Willow**: Therefore, on this day, on this floor, I will perform without care for what anyone thinks.

笃笃骨在浓雾中摆出了预备的姿势，随后，“迪吉里木”奏出了笃笃骨的乐曲。\
Willow strikes her beginning pose, a black swan in the smog, and the didgeriwood starts to play.

**笃笃骨**：淡黄继而淡黄，拓摹为神光……\
**Willow**: Palest yellow turns to godly light ...

**笃笃骨**：太阳的照耀会生出阴影，夜幕中的明月是何等耀眼！\
**Willow**: The sun births shadows, the moon shines bright!

**笃笃骨**：于黑暗中重生的太阳之神莱伊，我重走一遍你走过的路。\
**Willow**: Lugh, reborn from dark's embrace, I walk your path, in sacred space.

**笃笃骨**：生之尽头为死地，亡骨转而为生灵！\
**Willow**: Life's end is death, but bones to life ascend!

**笃笃骨**：太阳之神莱伊，面向我，我走出冥府。\
**Willow**: Lugh, before me, from underworld I wend.

**笃笃骨**：太阳之神莱伊，看着我，我带来死亡的阴影。\
**Willow**: Lugh, gaze on me, I rise from shadows dark.

**笃笃骨**：太阳之神莱伊，回应我，我正如您，您正如我！\
**Willow**: Lugh, heed me, your power impart, as you are me, and I your counterpart!

**观众Ⅰ**：雾散了！\
**Spectator I**: The smog ... It's clearing!

**观众Ⅲ**：快回来，可以看了！\
**Spectator III**: Everyone, come back! The Games are on again!

**观众Ⅰ**：雾里……雾里有东西！\
**Spectator I**: There's something there! There in the smog!

**“黑雾”**：嗷————\
**Black Fog**: *roar*

随着“迪吉里木”发出了空洞又悠长的梵音，群体祭祀也被笃笃骨引导着进入了几近忘我的状态。\
The didgeriwood sounds a long, hollow note as Willow leads the crowd into an almost trance-like state.

众人跟随着笃笃骨的动作，怀着对运动的热情和对阳光的渴望，喊出一遍又一遍祷词。\
Following Willow's lead, the crowd chants the prayer over and over, fueled by a zeal for the sport and a longing for the sun.

在群体祭祀的作用下，“黑雾”的躯体消解了。\
In the wake of the mass ritual, the black fog dissolves into nothingness.

**“黑雾”**：嗷————\
**Black Fog**: *roar*

失去了大部分躯体的“黑雾”只剩下了一层薄如轻纱的煤灰包裹着核心，它四处乱窜，慌乱地躲避着日光。\
With its body almost entirely disintegrated, the black fog is reduced to a core of thin, smoky soot as it scrambles frantically to avoid the sunlight.

**福葛先生**：见不得光的家伙，来好好吃点苦头吧！\
**Mr. Fog**: Alright, you filthy little thing! It's time you learnt a lesson!

**“伦敦煤烟污染勘察与清除大使MK.Ⅲ”**：砰砰！嗡——\
**Air Purifier MK. III**: Thud! Sssss ...

福葛先生打开了他带来的“伦敦煤烟污染勘察与清除大使MK.Ⅲ”，在喷出几股黑烟后，它再次发动了起来。\
Mr. Fog activates his London Air Pollution Auto-Detecting Purifier MK. III, and after a few puffs of black smoke, it roars to life.

**福葛先生**：我现在以“雾中爵士”的名义逮捕你，你的罪名为涉嫌触犯“危害公共卫生”及15条相关的法律，好好在这里反省你的一生吧！\
**Mr. Fog**: You are under arrest for the pollution of the sky as well as 15 crimes in violation of the Public Health Act! Take a good look around, because before long, you'll be rotting behind bars!

**“黑雾”**：呜……！\
**Black Fog**: Aww ...

福葛先生将“伦敦煤烟污染勘察与清除大使MK.Ⅲ”对准了惊慌的“黑雾”，将剩余的黑色煤灰物质统统吸了进去。\
Mr. Fog aims the purifier at the panicked black fog and sucks in every last bit of the remaining coal ash.

**“黑雾”**：呜……呜？\
**Black Fog**: Aww ... Aw?

“伦敦煤烟污染勘察与清除大使MK.Ⅲ”的玻璃罩瞬间被黑色的粉尘塞满，但马上，它们凝聚成了一团团的小黑球。\
The purifier's glass dome fills with black dust in an instant before it coalesces into a number of small black orbs.

它们分波躲藏在那颗千疮百孔的铁肺中，迷茫又好奇地望着玻璃罩之外。\
The little orbs peer out of the glass dome with a curious and confused expression.

**福葛先生**：即使它坏了——但吸点脏东西还是绰绰有余的！\
**Mr. Fog**: It may be broken, but it's still an air purifier!

“迪吉里木”的乐声渐渐停止了。\
The didgeriwood's melody slowly dies down.

笃笃骨立在场中，汗如雨下。\
Willow stands in the center of the field, panting and drenched in sweat.

**笃笃骨**：谢谢大家……我的表演……结束了。\
**Willow**: That's all ... from me ... Thank you ... for watching.

言罢，笃笃骨深深地向会场中的众人鞠下躬去。\
She gives a deep bow.

众人也终于回过神来，冬日，许久未见的日光正一视同仁地铺洒在每个人的身上。\
The spectators return to their senses, and the long-absent winter sun shines down on them once more.

再也不是铁青色和灰黄色笼罩的世界。\
No longer is the world shrouded in shades of steel gray and ashen yellow.

他们惊讶地看着身边的人，脸色是如此鲜活，他们忍不住将手探入阳光中，感受这和煦又温暖的抚摸。\
They stare in amazement at each other, a few reaching their hands into the sunlight, feeling its warm caress.

人群中的角落，掌声响了起来。\
Applause breaks out from a corner of the crowd.

如溪流汇聚成江河。\
It soon builds into a raucous cheer.

有人自发地走上前去，拥抱了笃笃骨。\
One spectator spontaneously steps forward and embraces Willow.

越来越多的人加入了拥抱，在阳光下，以最简单的肢体语言表达着内心的喜悦之情。\
The crowd swells as more and more people step forward to embrace her in the simplest and most pure expression of joy.

使生命蓬勃，使隔阂消失，使人们团结，这便是乌卢鲁运动会的意义。\
To infuse life with vitality, to eliminate all boundaries, to unite people—that is the true meaning of the Uluru Games.

**纸信圈儿**：耶——！耶——！\
**Flutterpage**: Yay! Yayyy!

纸信圈儿挤不进来，她在人群外跳跃着，向笃笃骨挥手，而远处，卡洛琳仍站在观众席，得体地为笃笃骨鼓掌。\
Unable to squeeze her way through, Flutterpage leaps over the crowd, waving to Willow as she hangs in the air. Meanwhile, Caroline remains in the stands, elegantly applauding.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

看着喜形于色的纸信圈儿和远处的卡洛琳，笃笃骨最终还是向她俩轻轻地点了点头。\
Willow gives the two of them a subtle nod.

## LD-20 伦敦今日晴 / London, Sunny

一周后。\
One week later.

“叩叩”。\
*knock-knock*

**Z**：请进。\
**Madam Z**: Come in.

一个棕色的身影款款步入由黑白灰的方格建构而成的房间里，窗边，身着黑色大衣的女士转过身来。\
A figure in brown enters the Foundation office. By the window, Madam Z turns to face her.

**牙仙**：Z女士，这是本次外派行动的报告。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Madam Z, here's the report for my mission.

牙仙将一本厚厚的报告书放在了办公桌的左上角。\
Tooth Fairy sets a thick report down at the corner of the desk.

和她走时不同，Z女士的办公桌上已经堆满了各式各样的报告书。\
Madam Z's desk is cluttered with papers.

**牙仙**：看来你这边也并不清闲。\
**Tooth Fairy**: It seems you've been busy too.

Z女士端起热气腾腾的搪瓷杯，茶水的浓淡似乎与工作量呈正相关的趋势，随着文件的堆积，现在已是一杯苦涩。\
Madam Z winces a little as she takes a sip from her mug. The strength of her tea seems to correspond with her increasing workload. As the stack of documents grows, the more bitter it becomes.

**Z**：拜“重塑之手”高调行事所赐，即使我们已经确定了时代动乱与“暴雨”的关联性，却还是余不下一丝空闲。\
**Madam Z**: Even though we've confirmed the connection between societal turbulence and the "Storm," there is no time to catch a breath.

**Z**：谁都无法灭掉那些未燃之火，我们只能尽力去维稳……可是火一旦烧起来，却能瞬间吞没一个时代。\
**Madam Z**: Once chaos breaks, it will be the end of another era, but we can't resist the inevitable. All we can do is maintain order to postpone it as long as possible.

Z女士轻轻地叹了一口气，杯中的热气不自然地扭曲了一下。\
Madam Z heaves a soft sigh as the steam from her mug swirls unnaturally.

**Z**：你这次的伦敦之行，有什么新的收获吗？\
**Madam Z**: So, any findings in London?

牙仙摊开了手掌，里面是一粒煤灰和一颗乳牙。\
Tooth Fairy opens her hand flat. There's a speck of coal dust and a baby tooth resting in it.

**牙仙**：一颗瓦尔普吉斯——也就是“黑雾”，的牙齿，和……一位孩子的最后一颗乳牙。十分稀有的藏品。\
**Tooth Fairy**: A Walpurgis's tooth, from the black fog, and the last baby tooth of a child. Very rare, even for my collection.

**Z**：哦——\
**Madam Z**: Hmm.

Z女士推了推眼镜，屏住了呼吸，凑上前来。\
Madam Z pushes her glasses up and holds her breath as she inches forward.

**Z**：嗯……有所收获就是好的。\
**Madam Z**: Right. Well, that's good to know.

Z女士端详了一会后，便站直了身体。\
After a few moments of examination, she straightens her posture.

**Z**：我听说，伦敦分部的同事们仍在致力于重现乌卢鲁运动会分会场上的那次祭祀仪式？\
**Madam Z**: I heard the London branch is still trying to replicate the ritual that was carried out at the Exhibition Games. What was that?

**牙仙**：那是一个巧合……\
**Tooth Fairy**: It was a coincidence, actually.

牙仙看向窗外，厚实而软塌的白色云层落在地平线上，也许伦敦现在也是这样的好天气。\
Tooth Fairy peers out the window, watching the soft, white clouds gathered on the horizon. Perhaps London, too, is enjoying such beautiful weather.

**牙仙**：通过对福葛先生提供的活体样本进行调查，伦敦分部的同事们得出了结论，这只瓦尔普吉斯是一种已消失了数个世纪的魔精“西欧罗斯”的变异种。\
**Tooth Fairy**: After analyzing the live sample provided by Mr. Fog, the London branch concluded that the Walpurgis is a mutant of the Cyoeraeth, a critter species that's been extinct for centuries.

**牙仙**：运动会结束后，笃笃骨向伦敦基金会分部的同事们提供了一本家传残本，上面记载着一个古老的太阳神祭祀仪式，笃笃骨的舞步正是来源于此。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Ms. Willow lent one of her heirlooms to the London branch after the Games, a book that details an ancient ritual meant to worship the god of the sun. This is the ritual she performed on the floor.

**牙仙**：但当笃笃骨小姐再次在福葛先生捕获的瓦尔普吉斯前进行祭祀仪式时，那只瓦尔普吉斯却毫无反应。\
**Tooth Fairy**: But when Ms. Willow performed the ritual again in front of the Walpurgis, nothing happened.

**牙仙**：我猜测，应该是随着西欧罗斯的消失，原本的祭祀仪式也慢慢失传了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: My guess is that, since the Cyoeraeth disappeared, the ritual fell out of use and became fragmented over the years. Her version of it is probably incomplete.

**牙仙**：但在分会场，可能是某位参与仪式的人的舞蹈姿势，可能是“迪吉里木”发出的音乐，或者是现场火炬的燃料，会场的磁场……\
**Tooth Fairy**: The conditions must've happened to align at that moment to allow the ritual to work. It could've been any combination of things—Ms. Willow's dancing, the music from the didgeriwood, the fire from the torch, the magnetic fields around the stadium ...

**牙仙**：总之，多个潜在的条件结合到了一起，才凑巧复原了这个失传已久的仪式，而这个仪式刚好能够诱捕那只造成伦敦浓雾的瓦尔普吉斯。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Or perhaps it was all of them. The ritual also happened to have the power to capture the Walpurgis, which put an end to the heavy smog in London.

**牙仙**：崇拜太阳神的仪式能够诱捕遮天蔽日的怪物……这其中的内在逻辑是连贯的。\
**Tooth Fairy**: It makes sense, really, that a ritual used to worship the god of the sun would capture a monster that covers the sky and plunges everyone into darkness.

**牙仙**：这是一个由多方因素堆砌而成的巧合。\
**Tooth Fairy**: In conclusion, the ritual's success was a near-unrepeatable coincidence.

**Z**：一只濒临灭绝的魔精，以及一场早已失传的祭祀仪式……\
**Madam Z**: An endangered critter and a long-forgotten ritual ...

**Z**：可能这就是为什么人类一直坚持着从时间的长河中浪里淘沙吧，我们总能从前人的经验中找到一些办法。\
**Madam Z**: I guess that's why humans are always sifting through their past. There's always wisdom to be found in history.

Z女士啜饮了一口杯中的浓茶。\
Madam Z takes a small sip of the tea in her mug.

**Z**：泡得太久了，该一口气干掉了。\
**Madam Z**: It's gone bitter. I should've finished it earlier.

Z女士放下了杯子，重新坐回到办公桌前。\
She sets the mug aside and sits down at her desk.

**Z**：对了，你的长假，我已经批准了。\
**Madam Z**: By the way, I've approved your vacation request.

**Z**：这次应该不会有人再来打搅你的假期了。\
**Madam Z**: No one should disturb you this time.

**牙仙**：那么，辛苦你了。\
**Tooth Fairy**: Thank you. Have a good day.

牙仙再次在桌上放下一颗奶糖后就离开了。\
Tooth Fairy sets another piece of milk candy on the desk and walks out.

**Z**：这种糖的味道，只会让我更想家……\
**Madam Z**: Milk candy ... Makes me miss the rabbit candy back home.

**Z**：不过也好。\
**Madam Z**: Well, at least it goes with the tea.

Z剥开了糖纸，再次将它放入口中。\
Madam Z unwraps the candy and pops it into her mouth.

**纸信圈儿**：笃笃骨！我拿到了！\
**Flutterpage**: Ms. Willow! I got it!

人未至，声先到。\
Flutterpage's voice arrives before she does.

笃笃骨从行李清单中抬起头来，听着欢快又踏实的脚步声咚咚地靠近过来。\
Willow raises her eyes from her packing list as she hears bright little footsteps heading closer.

**纸信圈儿**：基金会承认了预选赛！我拿到你的邀请函和我们的门票了！\
**Flutterpage**: Look! The Foundation's recognized our Games! Here's your invitation and our tickets!

**笃笃骨**：呵，飞是比走着的要快些。\
**Willow**: Heh. I suppose your flying does come in handy after all.

笃笃骨将行李箱合上，接过了纸信圈儿手中的文件袋。\
Willow shuts her suitcase and takes the folder from Flutterpage.

**纸信圈儿**：你收拾的怎么样了？\
**Flutterpage**: Are you done packin'?

纸信圈儿从不会闲下来，她四处打量着笃笃骨房间的变化，看她带走了哪些物品。\
Flutterpage looks around Willow's room, making note of what's moved and what hasn't.

**纸信圈儿**：这块奖牌，你不带走了吗？\
**Flutterpage**: Ain't you takin' this medal with you?

纸信圈儿指着壁橱中新放入的这块奖牌，这是笃笃骨近十年内获得的第一个荣誉。\
Flutterpage points to the medal recently placed in the cabinet—the first Willow has earned in almost a decade.

**笃笃骨**：不用，这就是最好的证明。\
**Willow**: No. This is proof enough.

笃笃骨拍了拍文件袋，里面装着1张邀请函和2张门票。\
Willow pats the folder holding the invitation and two tickets.

**纸信圈儿**：那可是预选赛第一名哦？\
**Flutterpage**: But that medal's for the winner of the qualifiers!

**笃笃骨**：区区预选赛。\
**Willow**: Oh, please, they're just qualifiers.

笃笃骨嗤笑了一声。\
Willow scoffs.

“叮咚”。\
*ding-dong*

**笃笃骨**：谁？\
**Willow**: Who's that, I wonder?

**卡洛琳**：哇，花园已经变得这么美丽了吗？\
**Caroline Bartley**: Wow, what happened to the garden? It's beautiful!

**宽檐帽**：是的，自从笃笃骨女士获得了预选赛第一名，花园就变得容光焕发起来了。\
**Brimley**: Ms. Willow's put a lot of care into it ever since she won first place in the qualifiers.

**卡洛琳**：呵呵，夏洛特真是好懂。\
**Caroline Bartley**: Ah, Charlotte, ever predictable.

庭院中，卡洛琳和宽檐帽正欣赏着冬日中难得一见的枝繁叶茂。\
Caroline and Brimley look around the garden, enjoying the rare sight of foliage flourishing in winter.

**传声花**：你们来做什么？\
**Voiced Flower**: What are you doing here?

**宽檐帽**：笃笃骨女士，我们是想与您一起出发。\
**Brimley**: We want to invite you to join us. Let's go to Australia together!

**传声花**：卡洛琳为什么也在？\
**Voiced Flower**: With Caroline, too?

**卡洛琳**：前三名都要去澳洲参加乌卢鲁运动会的总决赛啊，若不是你碰巧收拾了那个瓦尔普吉斯，我们谁是冠军还真不好说呢。\
**Caroline Bartley**: For your information, Charlotte, the top three athletes all qualify for the finals. And besides, I might have beaten you if you weren't so lucky as to capture that Walpurgis.

**宽檐帽**：而且，我们乘坐的轮船，正是卡洛琳小姐家中的产业。\
**Brimley**: By the way, the ship we're taking is owned by the Bartley family.

**笃笃骨**：什么？\
**Willow**: What?

**宽檐帽**：卡洛琳小姐还说，会为我们升到总统套房。\
**Brimley**: So, Ms. Bartley said she'd arrange a presidential suite for us.

**纸信圈儿**：总统套房，是总统才能住的地方吗？\
**Flutterpage**: A presidential suite? Like, for presidents?

纸信圈儿毛茸茸的头从笃笃骨身后探了出来。\
Flutterpage's head sticks out from behind Willow.

**卡洛琳**：看来我们还要相处很久呢。\
**Caroline Bartley**: It seems we'll be spending quite some time together in the coming weeks.

**笃笃骨**：……\
**Willow**: ...

**纸信圈儿**：总统套房！我们之中谁是总统？是卡洛琳吗？原来你是总统吗？\
**Flutterpage**: But which one of us is a president? It's Caroline, ain't it? It must be!

**笃笃骨**：你先安静一点！\
**Willow**: Would you shut your mouth?!

**纸信圈儿**：我不会再被你吓唬住了哦。\
**Flutterpage**: Hah. You can't scare me anymore.

**卡洛琳**：呵呵……\
**Caroline Bartley**: Heh-heh.

黄昏将世界染成了金色，遥远的河畔旁，货轮发出了悠长的汽笛声。\
Dusk paints the world gold, and from a distant riverbank, a freighter sounds its horn.

今日，伦敦，晴。\
Today, the skies of London are clear.
